Po uhafi uwakati uwene pabhelaga isiku ilwa papwe Herode abhandalila atalamu abhakwe ishelehe, na adadamu nalongozi ami Galialaya.
Phipo ulendu wa Herodia ahinjila nacheze witazi wabhene, afulaiswa uHarode na jenyu abhakhile uwakati uwishalwe shalwevhela. Epo utawala abhula ulendu, “Undavhe hahondti uwaza nani izahupele.”
Alapilizya huje, hahudi hubha ndavhe, izahupele, ahata inusu iyitala wani.”
Afuma huzi avhuzya anyina wakwe, “Indavhe yenu?” Abhula, “Itwe ilwa Yohana uwa Wonza.”
Shisho ahinjila watawala ahanda ayanje, “Iwaza muhati musahani, itwe lwa Yohana uyawozwa.”
Utawala aswiga sana, lelo ululapo ulwalapile na ajenyi, haga hawezywa hukhanile ilwa labhile.
Isho, mutawala ahatuma asinjala abha gulaga abhalajizywe abhale alilete itwelwa yahanaulizi abhatile adumule wijela.
Ahaleta itwe kwenye sahani na hupele ulindu ulindu apela unyina wakwe.
Asundwa bhakwe pabha huvha isho, bhahabhala abhale aweje ubhilyi gwakwe bhala asywile hunghugwa.
Atumwa bha bhungana witazi wa Yesu, bhabhula gunthi agabhombile na gabhamanyizyaga.
Wope abhabhula, “Izaji mwemwe pasili tutuye hashe.” Abhantu abhinji bhali bhahweza nashile wala habhapata inafusi iyolye.
Bhinjila mumashuwa bhala amahali pasili bhene.
Lelo bhahabha lola pabhashila bhahabhamanya abhahanyila lwimagaga upaka humiji guthi, bhope bhafiha shavhasili abhene.
Pahafiha pwani, bhalola ibhuga ingosi bhahabhasajila, pipo bhali nishi ingole izwasazili nu ndimii. Ahanda abha manyizye amambo aminji.
Abhazyo pahedelela sana, asudwa abhahemwizila bhaha bhula,”Ipa tuli mahali pisili umuda gubhalile.
Ubhalaje bhashilaje aweze ishalye humiji hujiji ivipipi.”
Lelo abhajibhula ayanga, “Bhapeli amwe ishalye.” Tugawezwa awepe nakale amabumunda angisamani na mimbili tubhapele hahalye?”
Ahabhabhula,” Muna amabumunda galinga? Mubhale mwenye.” pabhavhaga bhahabhula, “Amabumunda gasanu ni samaji nsivhile.”
Bhahamuliswa abhantu bhakhale mumasole amolo.
Bhaha khazywa makundi; makundi mamia na amhamsini.
Ahenga amabumunda gasanu na samaki zibhili, na wenye humwanya, ahasanya aha pela asudwa waweke mbele ya umati. Bhabhishe nasamaki zibhili, na zitatu wabhathu bhuthi.
Bhahalya bhuthi bhayile.
Bhabhunganya amabumuda sangile, Vyaha mema ivitundu vhibhele, nivindumushila ivisamaki.
Bhali alume elufuzisanu abhalile amabunda.
Abhabhula huje bhande mashua bhabhale isemu iyinji, Bethsaida, uwakati abhalaga ulubhungano.
Pabha habha bhashila, abhala wi gamba alavhe.
Pawahahavha shalyevhela na mashua yabho ulwo ili pahati pazhumbi alimwene panzi inyumu.
Ahalola bhatamiwa akhome makasiapipo ihala ihapingaga. Pahuhabha hupambazuha nashaphii abha bhalila, ajendaga amizi ahazaga ashizanye.
Lelo pahalola ajenda amwanya iyimeze, bhapata uwasi wasi bhagazimu hata bhakhola.
pipo bhahalola vhahijila ishaka. Ahagana yanje anabho abhabhula, “Mubhanje bhadadamu! nene! Mganje abhe nihofu.”
Ahinjila muhati mumashua, na ihala ihaleha avungume na haswiga kabisa.
Haga bhahelewa imana iyagala amabumunda. Injele zhwabho zyalidodo.
Bhope pali bhaloushe isyila bhafiha insi ya Genesareti mashua ikati nanga.
Pabhahaguma huzi iye mashua, bhahatabula.
Bhahanyila atangazwe mkowa gwundhi bhahandu abhalete avhinu mzego mzega, shila pahuvhaga huje awiza.
Pundi pahinjilaga huvijiji, au mumiji, au munzhi, bhabhihaga avhinu pasoko, bhalamba huje bhapala mazhwaje amenda gakwe. Na bhundti abhakhete bhaponile.
Mafalisayo nabhamo asimbi ambao bhafumila hu Yelusalemu bhahabhungana huzhwongule umwene.
Bha hulolie bhamobhamo huje asunda bhakwe bhalile ibumunda humakhono amachafu; saga gahoziwe.
(wa Mafalisayo na Yahudi bhundti sabhalya upaka bhozizye amakhono gao shishinza; bhakhatila utamanduni agosibhabho. Huwakati
Amafalisayo pabhabhuya afume mahali pasoko, sabhalya paka bhoje kwanza na huli ishelia zimo zimo abhuzywo bhazida gakabisa, ikiwa abhozye ivikombe, amafulila, ivhombo ivhishaba, na hata amatengo agatuniha uwakati uwishalye.)
Amafalisayo na asimbi bhalihubhuzye uYesu, “Kwa nini asudwa bhaho sabhakhala afatane nagosi, bhao bhalwaibunda nabila asungusule amakhono?”
Lelo umwene ahabhabhabhula, “Isaya ahakuwashinza huje amwe mulibhivhi, asimba, 'Aje abhantu ibha bhanogopa humalo mu golo, lelo amoyo ga bho gali hutaloi nani.
Bhabhombela inyiputoizywaswazya zyizyo izyasazi welewelewewa sazimuhimu bhamanyiziwa italabu izywa bhanadamu gabha poshala agao.'
Muleshile iatalatibu izywa Nguluvhi namuzywejile izishibinadamu ugatwaposhile.”
Ahayanga wa bhene muzikhanile amuli izwa Nguluvhi ishilaisi ili muziute izyinyu!
Lelo pipo uMose ayajile, umwogopaje udada waho nunyina waho,' uwayanga amavhivhi wa dada au wamai wakwe lywoli aifwa.'
Lelo amwe, 'muyanga huje umuntu akhayanga wadada wakwe au mai, “Usada gwagwunti gula ugwa hunda mwe jelela je afume hulini iyo mbuta yinyiputo,”' (ubho wayanje huje ifumile wa Ngulubhi')
isho ahuruhusu abhombe ijambo lwa lwunti alibhombe kwaajili ya dada au ya mai wakwe.
Muyi bheha amuli Nguluvhi huje yilwene alete inyiho zywinyu. Na mambo aminji aga gali isho angamuomba.”
Abhakujile amakutano andthele nabhabhule, “Huje munuvhaje ane, amwe mwindhe, namu nelewe.
Nahamo hahunti huziwa muntu hahuchafula mtu kiingiapo kwake. Bali ni kile kimtokacho mtu ndicho kimchafuacho.
(Azingatile: usitali ugu, “khamba umuntu amakutu agahuvhwe ayuvhaaje” nashimo munakili izihalyi).
U Yesu ahagaleha amakutano abhala khaya, asundwe bhahabhuzwa ufwano ugwo.
U Yesu ahayanga, “Namwe nantele saga muwelewa? Samulola hahunti ahahumwinjila umuntu hawezwa huchafule,
pipo sahabhala huwoyo gwakwe, lelo ishashiwinjila muvhanda vhakwe shishizanya nabhale hucho.” Hu ma elezo iga uYesu abhiha ivhalwe vhunti abhe vinza.
Ayanjile, “Shila isha shihufuma umuntu shashi huchafula.
Pipo hafuma muhati mwa muntu, huzihu mwoyo gafuma amawazo amachafu, akwesane, uwibha, agoje,
amabhibhi iga gunti hutamani ishibhibhi, ubhibhi uwaswovhe, akwesane, uwivu aphuyile, awivune, nulema.
Amabhibhi iga gunti gafuma muhati, gaga huchafula umuntu.”
Abhuha afume pala nashile ukowa wa Tiro na Sidoni. Ahainjila muhanti haga ahazaga umuntu yayundhe amanyaje huje aliipo, lelo haga ihazehana hufise.
Lelo ghafla ushi, ula umwana wakwe udodo ani roho ichafu, ahuvha ihabali hakwe, ahiza, naha gwa magaga agakwe.
Ushi uyo Muyunani, wikambela ilwa Kifoeniki. Alambile umwene anyizhwe ipo afume wa lyindu wakwe.
U Yesu ahabhula ushi, “Bhateshe abhana bhaliziwaje huje sashili aweje ibumunda ilwabhana azitajile ibwa.”
Lelo ushi ajibule nayanje, “Ena Bwana, ibwa panzi yimeza ivhavhi sagala ivhalye vha bhana.”
Abhula, “Ahuje pepo uyanjile ishi, uli mwaushe ashile. Iphepo ifumile ulindu waho.”
Ushi ahabhuya khaya yakwe ahamwaga ulindu wakwe agonile pashitala, iphepo ali afumile.
U Yesu afumile inje yikowa wa Tiro na ashizanije Sidoni abhalile hunsumbi ya Galilaya pakakanda ya Dikapolisi.
Bhahaleta umuntu uya sahuvha uyasawezya ayanje shishiza, bhalambile uYesu huje abhishe amakhono pamwanya yakwe.
Ahumwefwa hunzhi ikundi shisili abhiha inyovhe makutu gakwe, bada ya aswe amate apala manzywa ulumili lyakwe.
Ahenyizhwe humwanya amaso ahutuya na hubhule, “Efata,” isuo wa huyanje “fuguha!”
Umuda gwagula amakutu gahiguha, nahala ahazijile awezywa ayanjeshishinza.
Abhamulila bhaganje hubhele umuntu wabhunti. Lelo pali abhamulila bhanje hubhule umuntu pabha zidile ayanje ibhahalileizyo zinyijii.
Lyoli bhashijizhiwe, nayanje, “Abhombile shila hantu shishinza. Hata abhombile abhasa bhahuvha amakutu ahuvhe na bhabubu ayanje.”
Lele inzhiku izyo, paliiibuga ingosi, salinishalwe. U Yesu abhakuga asundwa bhakwe ahabhula,
“Injisajila ibuga ini bhendelile abhe nani inzhiku zitatu na sani shalye.
Khimba nyaphanye huje bhabhuye huzinyumba zyabho bila alye bhagazimila mwidala nizala. Mhati yabho bhamo bhafuma hutali sana.”
Asundwa bhakwe bhajibula, “Tubhagaje wii amabumunda agabhaye bhutnthi ibha nabha kutizye abhantu ibha ineo ilyaleshilye?”
Ahabhabhuzya, “mulini vipande vhilinga ivhimabumunda?” Bhayanga, “Saba.”
Awamulila ibhuga bhakhale panzi. Ahega amabumunda saba, ahasalifya Ungulubhi, na budulanye. Abhapela asunda bhakwe bhagabhishe witanzi lyabho, bhahagahiha witanzi libhuga.
Bhope bhali ni samaki zindodo nyishe, na bada yahusalifye, abhamulila asudwa bhakwe bhaganyiivhi vhope.
Na bhahalya naye. Nabhabhunganya ipande ivhisangele ivitundu, ivigasi saba.
Bhelega abhantu elufu zine. Aheleha bhashalaje.
Mara ahinjila mashua nasundwa bhakwe, nabhashila katika ukanda wa Dalmanuta.
Amafalisayo bhafumahuzina wande adalisanye nawo. Bhazaga ishimanyilo afume humwanya, bhajelaga.
Asebha sana mmwoyo gwakwe ayanga, “Yenu ishizazi ishi shiwaza imanyilo? Imbabhula amwe lyoli, na shimo ishimanyilo ishashaifuma hushi zazi ishi.”
Ipo ahambaleha, ahinjila muhati mmashua anthele ahashila awelekele upauwenje.
Umuda ugwo asudwa bhahi wilwe aweje amabumunda. Sagabhali nishipande shashundhi ishibumunda hata shimo ishali mashua.
Abhonya hayanje, “Mubhanje maso na witunze ishilela aluzu iya Mafalisayo na haluzu aHarode.
Asundwa bhayangana bhene wabhene, “Pipo sagatuli namabumunda.”
U Yesu ahamanya ili nabhabhula, “Yenu muyangana pasamuli namabumunda? Hamuminye bado? Hagamuwelewa? Amoyo ginyu mapupusu?
Amaso hamulola? Munakutu, sagamuhuvhwa? Hagaamukumbuha?
Pihagabhaya amabumunda gasanu wa bhantu elufu zisanu, mwahejile ivitundu vhilyinga ivhavimemile amabumunda?” Bhahajibula “ilongo navhele.”
Pahagabhanya amabumunda saba huelufu ine, muhega ivitundu vhilinga?”
Bhahayanga, “Saba.” Ahabhabhula, “Bado haga muwelewa?”
Bhajiza Bethsaida. Abhantu ibho bhahuleta wa Yesu umuntu uwafyile amaso bhahalamba uYesu akhate.
U Yesu ahukhata nukhano ola uwafyile amaso nahulongole huzi ishijiji ahaswa amante pamwanya yimaso nagolosye amakhono pamwanya yakwe, ahabhuzwa, “Uhalola hahunte?”
Ahenyizywe humwanya nayanje, “Imbalola abhantu bhabhoneha nishi amapishi gajenda.”
Ipo ahagolosya amakono gakwe pa mwanay iyimaso gakwe, umuntu ola gafunguha amaso gakwe, ahalola nanhele, ahalola shilahandu shishiza.
U Yesu ahaleha ashila akhaya yakwe nahabhula, “Unganje aeinjile hujini.”
U Yesu ashila nasundwa bhakwe huvijiji ivha Kaiseria ya Filipi. Bhali mwidala abhabhuzwa asundwa, “Abhantu bhayiga ni nanu?”
Bhahajibula bhahayanag, “Yohana uwabhozwa. Bhamo bhayanga, 'Eliya' na bhamo, 'Muntu umo Nakuwa.”
Ahabhabhuzwa, “Lelo amwe muiga ane ninanu?” Petulo ahabhula, “Awe wi Kristi.”
U Yesu abhula bhanje hibhule umuntu yayunti uwahusu umwene.
Ahanda abhamanyinzye huje umwene Mwana wa Adamu lazima alavhe humambo aminji, ayikanwa nalongozi na achungaji agosi nasimbi, na gagwe bada yinsiku zitatu aizyuuha.
Aliyanjile iga apazelu. Epo uPetulo ahamwega paka pashinje anda hudamile.
Lelo uYesu agaluhana na bhenye asundwa bhakwe na ahadamila uPetulo nayanje, “Sahinzanya huhosi yane Setano! Haga usaga amambo aga Ngulubhi, ila amambo agabhantu.”
Ipo ahakuga ibuga nabhasundwa abhakwe palishimo, nabhabhule, “Kama huli umuntu uya wanza afwuate awikhane nyuyo, ayegaje ishikhovhehanyo shakwe na afhunte.
Wahuje wabhunti uya wanza awokole amaisha gakwe aigatenzwa nauyantezywa amaisha gakwe kwa ajili ya lini na kwa ajili izyo ayokola.
Aipata yenu umuntu khapate inzhi yunthi wa pante ihasala akahle wakwe?
Umuntu agawezya afumwe yenu badala yaifumwe ubhumi wakwe?
Uwaindolela inshoni ninogwa zywani ishizazi ishinishi zazi ishabhivhivhi, Umwana wa Adamu ayilolela inshoni paiyinza nubhutawala uwa dada wakwe palishimo naa wandumi azelu.
Ayanjile wabhene, “Lwoliiyanga hulimwi bhawili abhanthu abhabhimilile epha ambao hagabhaibhoja ufye shausilye utawala uwa Ngulubhi pawayinza wikhone.”
Na bada yinshikutanda, uYesu abhega aPetulo, Yakobo na Yohana palishimo numwene wigamba, bhene. Ndipo ahandile agaluhane mbele yao.
Amenda gakwe gaga luhana gana amulishe alabhe sana nabhe mazelu zaidi uzeluuwasa bhulavha wabhonthi munthi.
Phepo aEliya pamoja nu Mose bhahafumila witazi lwabho, bhali bhayanga nu Yesu.
U Petulo ajibula uYesu, “Umwalimo, shinza ati akhale epa, shimo shaliwe, shimo kwa ajili ya Mose na isha mwabhosha Eliya.”
(Haga amenye ahawaziwa ayanje, bhahogopha sana.)
Ibhingo lwa fumila nabha kwi shile. Ipo isauti ihafuma mwibhingo ihayanga, “Unu mwana wane uwingine. Mutejele zyaje yuyo.”
Ghafla, pali bha wenya sabha halola uyalinao palishimo, ila uYesu mwene.
Pali bhahwiha afume wigamba, amulila huje bhasaheze hubhele umuntu numo gala gunti agabha galolile, paka Umwana wa Adamu piizhyuha afume wabhafwe.
Ipo paha ga uta amambo bhibho. Lelo bhayangana bhene kwa bhene lwenu imana yakwe “azyushe afume wa bhafwe”
Bhaha bhuzya uYesu,”Yenu abhandishi bhaiga uEliya ayize nasonti?”
Abhabhula, “lwoli Eliya sagabhiza afume ivhintu vhunti. Yenu isimbilwe Mwana wa Adamu lazima apate amalabha gaminji navhitililwe?
Lelo iyanga hulimwi lelo uEliya ahezele, bhahabhomba shabhayingine nishishila shaiganile, nishi amasimbo shaga yanga ahusu umwene.”
Pabha habhuya wasudwa, bhaha ilola imbunga ingosi izyungulile na Masadukayo bhabisanyaga ahabho bhabisanyaga anabho.
Pala pahalola, ibhunga yunti bhahashyiga nahunyilile hulamushe.
Abha bhuzywa asundwa abhakwe, “Mubisanya nao kuhusu iyenu?”
Umuntu umo muhati yabho ahajibula, “Mwalimo ihale ta umwana wane huliwe; ana iroho iyithavu ihubhomba huje anganda yayanje,
ihu fanya aje atete mamanje na hugwisye panzi, nafume ipofu mwilomu nasye amino naga gandane. Ihabhalabhile asundwa bhaho humwefye, lelo hagabhawezizwe.
Abhajibu, “Ishizazi ishasa shiwamini izakhale namwe humuda bhuli? Izawejelane namwe paka lii leti hulini? Mleteni kwangu.”
Bhaleta umwana wakwe. Iroho inhavhu palalala uYesu, gafla ihapela ateteme. Usahala agwile paka panzi naafumhe ipovhu wilomu.
U Yesu ahabhuzya uyise, “Ihali ine ili awande muda ulyi?” Uyise ayanjile, “Aje afume uwana wakwe.
Mumomumo itwala humwoto au mumenze naije la humwanga mizywe, kama uwezwa abhombe hahunthi utuhulumile natusaidile.”
U Yesu abhulyile, “Akhashele uli tayali? Hala hantu hawezeha na waya yunthi uya wamini.”
Ghafla uyise wa mwana ahalila nayanje huje, “Iwamini! Nisaidie asinte awamini wane.”
Uwakati uYesu pahalola imbuga inyila abhale wabhene, ayikemela iroho inthavu nayanje, “awenohobubu uwasaga uhuvha, ihuwamuruleshe, usahinjile wamwene nanthele.”
Ahalila wikhone na huhangaisye umwana na iroho ihafumile. Umwana abhoneha uga afyile, Ipo abhinji bhayanjile, “Aje afyile,”
Lelo uYesu amwega nukhono abhusywa, umwana ahimelila.
Lula uYesu pahinjila muhatyi, asundwa bhakwe bhahabhuzya shisili, “Yenu satawezizye humwefye?”
Abhabhulile, “pipo ini haga iwepa ila pwavhile.”
Bhahepa pala najendele wi Galilaya. Haga ahazanga umuntu yayuthi amanye pawilyi,
pipo amanyizywaga asudwa bhakwe. Abhabhulile, “Umwana wa Adamu atwalya makhono mwa bhantyu, nahugoje. Paivha afwile, baada yinsiku tatu aizyuha nanthele.”
Lelo haga bhaha mwelewa agawelezya iza, bhahogopa hubhuzywe.
Ipo vhahafiha Karperinaumu. Wakati uhuo pali muhanthi nyumba abhuzizye, “Mwayanga naga yenu mwidala”?
Lelo bhaha puma mie. Yani bisanya mwidala huje yunanu uwazabhe gosi zaidi.
Ahakhala pansi abhakuga ilongo na bhamo bhabhilye pamo, ayanga nabho, “Umuntu khawaza abhe wa kwanza, nilazima abhe wa malishilo na wabhatumishile bha bhunthi.”
Ahamwanya umwana udodo abhiha pahati yabho. Amwega makhono gakwe, ayanga,
“Wabhodthi nishi unu witawa lyane, oyaabha amboshile ninengashele umuntu aposha, saga aphola nene tu, lelo nayula uwantumile.”
U Yohana abhula, “Umwalimu tulolile umuntu kwa wefya iphepo witawa lwaho tuhathubhila, pepo haga atidaga anti.”
Lelo uYesu ayanga, “Munganda hukhane pipo numo uwaibhomba imbombo ingosi witawa lwani na ipi pamandi ayanje injango imbivhi lwa lyunti.
Wa bhuntyi uwasagali tofauti natwe ali hu pande witu.
Wabhuntyi uya yipela ishikombe iminzye agamwele pipo uli Kilisite, lyoli imba bhala hagaitezya usahala gwakwe.
Wa bhuntyi uyakosezwa hawa bhali bhali bhadodo abhanamini anye, wali shinza wa mwene apinyilwe inganga ilwasyele huzhingo natagwe muzhumbi.
Khamba ukhono gwaho kha hukosela gundumulaje. Hubha washi awinjile huwomi bila khono kwiko awinjile kwenye hulozi ulinamakhono gutyi. Mula mumwoto “ugwasaguzimiha”.
(Inatila: Ulutanani ulu, “Pamahali ambapo intofyi sazifwa numwoto ugwasazimiha.” saga uwili katika nakala zakale).
Igaga khashele likosezywa, lidumula. Je shiza huliwe awijile huwumi khalilema, kuliko atagwe hulozi namagaga gavhili.
(Inatila: Ulutanani ulu, “Amahali itofi hazifwa numwoto usiyoweza azimishe hagagu wili nakala izihali).
Kama iliso lwaho khahukosezwa lisenyaje shinza hwilwe awinjile Utawala uwa Ngulubhi uli niso limo, kuliko kwingia ukiwa maso guntyi ulaje huje mwoto.
Pala apali nintafyi izya sazifya, numwoto ugwa saguzimia.
Lelo phipo shila muntyu aifyula numwoto.
Umwonyi mwinza, lelo umwonyi khagutezye uwiza wakwe, gubhabhombe bhuli uwinza bhuye nathyena? Munje mwonyi muhatyi yinyu, na uwaushe wa shila umo.”
U Yesu ashila amali pala na habhala katika ukowa ugwa Huyahudi ni eneo ilya witanzi ili Soho Yorodani, amakutano gadagaga na tyena. Abhamanyizwe tyena, nishi pibha kawaida yamwene abhombe.
Na Amafalisayo bhaheza hujele bhahabhuzwa, “Ni halali wa muntu ulume aleha nushi awakwe?”
U Yesu abhajibula, “U Mose amulile yenu?”
Bhayanga, “Mose aruhusu ahusimbile ikalata iyalene nahunyizywe ushi.”
“Pipo amoyo nginyu makhome shashisho abhasimbila ishalia ini, “U Yesu ahabhala.
“Afume huwandilo wiumbaji, 'Ungulubhi aumba ulume nushi.'
Inamuna ini ulume aileha uyise wakwe nu nyina wakwe aibhungana nushi wakwe,
na eo bhabhili bhaibhabhili gumo; Pipo saga bhabhiatyele, lelo bhali bili gumo.
Kwa hiyo abhunganisye Ungulubhi, umwanadamu anje alehanye.”
Pali muhati inyumba, asundwa bhakwe bhahahuzywa nantyena asuili.
Abhabhula, “Ula uwileha ushi wakwe na weje uwinji uyo abhomba malaya pamwanya yakwe.
Na ushi wope khaila ulume wakwe na wegwe nulume uwinji, abhomba malaya.”
Bhope bhahuleta abhana adodo akhate, lelo asimbi bhakwe bhahabha damila.
Lelo uYesu pahamanya ilwo, haga amojelela nalwo kabisa abhabhula, “Bhalesheli abhana adodo bhinze hulini, munganjebhazije, pipo abhabhalinishi ibha utawala uwa Ngulubhi wabhene.
Lyoli imbaula, yayunti uwa saposhela utawala wa Ngulubhi nishi abhana adodo lyoli haga aiwezywa awinjile utawala wa Ngulubhi.
Ipo abhega abhana makhono agakwe abhasaya nabhabhishe akhono panya yabho.
Pahanda isafali yakwe umuntu umo anyililila ahafugamila amafuugamo witazi lwakwe, abhuzwa, “Mwalimu Umwinza, imbombe yenu ili bweze erithi uwomi uwa wilawila?”
U Yesu ayanga, “Unguga mwema? Numo ulimwema ila yu Ngulubhi mwene.
Uziminye imuli: 'Uganje agoje, unganje afunye umalaya, unganda awibhe ungande ande ilenga unganje akhopele, uheshimwaje uyese waho nu nyina waho'.”
Umutyu ulo ahayanga, “Mwalimo, iganguntyi awande uwana wanhe.”
U Yesu amwenya nahugane. Abhula, “Upungushilwe ahatyu hamo. Uwaziwa ukazye uvhili navho nabhapele apina, uhaibha ni mbuto humwanya. Khasha winzaje andaje.”
Lelo akatile itama hunongwa iyaheleziwe iga; aliondoka akiwa mwenye huzuni, ahepa nusumane phepo alimale nyinji.
U Yesu ahenya upande bhutyi abhabhula asundwa bhakwe, “Nishi bhuli ishashashilyi pakhome utajili awinjile hutawala uwa hu mwanya!
Asundwa bhaswijiziwa humaneno iga. Lelo uYesu abhabhula nantyele, “Bhana, ni jinsi bhule ishili shikhome awinjile utawala Ungulubhi!
Laisi wingamia ashizanye mwilina lisindano, pakuliko umutyu utajili awinjile hufalume uwa Ngulubhi.”
Bhaswijiziwa sana nayangana bhene, “Esho yunanu uwa yokolewa”
U Yesu abhenya nayayanje, “Wabinadamu hagaiwezehana, lelo saga wa Ngulubhi. Wavhavhuthi wa Ngulubhi shiwezehana wa Ngulubhi shiwezehana.”
“Petulo handa ayanje nabho, “Enya tuleshile vhutyi tudajile.”
U Yesu ayanga, “Lyolyi imbabhula amwe, numouwaila inyumba, au ukulu, au uilumbu, au unyina, au uyise, au abhana, au ugunda, kwa ajili yangu, na kwa ajili ya lumbelele,
uwaha gaiposhela mala mia zaidi yisalaini ipa pansi: inyumba, ukulu, uyilumbu, au unyina, au abhana, au uinsi, humalabha, ulimwengu ugwa guweza, uwumi uwawila na wila.
Lelo vhinji avhali wanda bhaibhabhahumalishilo abhali bhahumalishilo bhawanda.”
Pabhabha mwidala, bhabhala Yelusalemu, uYesu abhatangulila witanzi lyabho. Asundwa bhasyijile, nabhala abhali bhafuta khosi yabho bhahogopa. Ipo uYesu abhefa pashinje antele bhala ilongo nabhabhili ahanda abhabhule hala hazafumile ishi papipi:
“Enya, tushila hula hu Yelusalemu, nu Mwana wa Adamu anzafisiwe wachungaji agosi nasimbi. Bhanzahulonje afwe bhanza humwefwe wa Bhapanzi.
Bhanza hulyeule, bhanza huswile amate, bhanzahukhome nusanzo, nahugaje. Lelo bada yinsiku zitatu azyuha.”
U Yakobo nu Yohana, abhana bha Zebedayo, bhahinza wamwene nayanje, “Mwalimu, tuwanza tubhombele hahundi atuhulabha.”
Ahagamuyiga, “Imbabho mbele yenu?”
Bhahayanga, “Turuhusu tukhale nae husisya waho, umo hukhona ugwahulilo umo hukhono gwa humongo.”
Lelo uYesu abhajibula, “Sagammenye ilyamulabha. Mugawezya amwelele ishikombe ishimwela ane au ajimbe au uwoziwa uwi woziwa?”
Bhaha bhala huje, “Tuwezya” uYesu abhabhula, “Ishikombe ishimwela mgawezya, amwe mwelele. Na ulyozyo ambao ininoziwe, mnzajimbilile.
Lelo uwakale ukhono ugwa hulilo au uugwa humongo saga nini uwafumwe, lelo wabhala ambao wavhene bhala ibhahandaliwe.”
Bhala asundwa bhamo ilongo pahahuvhaiga bhaha vitililya aYakobo nu Yohana.
U Yesu abhakuga wamwene nayanje, “Mumenye ahuje bha abhasivhililwa bhatabhalwa bhabhatyu abhapansi bhatabhala, nabhantyu avhikhapho bhalanga mamlaka pamwanya yabho.”
Lelo saga iwanziwa avhe ishi muhati yinyu. Wabhundi uwanza abhe gosi kati yinyu atumishilaje abhanji,
na wabhutyi uwawaza abhewanda pahati lazima abhanje watumishe wabhuntyi.
Wahuje Umwana wa Adamu hagaahiza atumishilwe bali atumishe nafume maisha gakwe abhvhe lisombo wa vhinji.”
Bhahinza Yeriko. Pahali ashilaga Yeriko nasundwa bhakwe ni mbuga ingosi, umwana wa Timayo, Batimayo, uwafwile amaso, uwalabha mashinje insumbi.
Pahavha huje yu Yesu Mnazareti, ahanda akhole nayanje, “Yesu, Mwana wa Daudi, hulumile!”
Abhinji bhahadamila ula uyafumile amaso, bhabhulaga phumaa. Lelo alilaga husauti sana, “Mwana wa Daudi, hulumile!”
U Yesu ahima nahumula mulile akugwe. Bhahakuga ula uyafwile amaso, bhahayanga, “Huje shuja! Bhuha! U Yesu ahukuga.”
Ataga ikoti lwakwe hushinji ahanyila sana, na winze wa Yesu.
U Yesu ahajibu nayanje, “Uwanza huje ibhombele yenu?” Ula ulume uwafwile amaso ahajibu, “Mwalimo, iwanza alole.”
U Yesu ahabhula, “Bhalanga. Awamini waho huponizye.” Pepo amaso gakwe gahalola; ahadaga uYesu wibalabala.
Ulyo ulya bha hizaga hu Yelusalemu, pabha hyela ga Besthfage na Bethania, wi Gamba ilya Mizeituni, uYesu abhatuma bhabhili muhati umwo mwa sundwa bhakwe
abhabhula, “Bhalaji hushijiji isha shi bhelana natyi. Pamu winjila umwo munzayaje idogovhi iya siinjilwe. Muyaule muilete hulini.
Nakhashele yayutyi uwabhula, 'Huje yenu mu bhomba ishi?', mubhajile ayanje ishi, 'U Bwana amwanza khashele abhuzwa ipa.'”
Bhabhalile nayaje idovhi ipinyile huzi hulyango uta ugwaguliwaza, bhayabhulila.
Bhamo abhantu bhalivhimile pala bhaha bhabhula, “Mubhomba yenu, ayaulile idogovhi ini?”
Bhabha bhulile nishi uYesu ishabhulele, na abhanya bhaleha bhashila.
Asundwa bhabhili bhahaleta idogovhi wa Yesu bhahalanga amenda gao pamwa yakwe ili uYesu awezyaje awinjile.
Abhantu ibhinji bhahalaga amenda mwibalabala, nabhamo bhalanga amasamba agabhatemile afume humagunda.
Bhala abhabha bhatile witanzi lwakwe na bhala abhadajile bhakhoma kelele, “Hosana! Asayiwe nuyahweza witawa ilwa Bwana.
Usaiwe hutawala bhuwinza wayise witu Daudi! Hosana bhunu uli humwanya”
Epo uYesu ahinjila hu Yelusalemu abhala hukanisa ahenya shila hantu. Ishi uwakati wali bhubhalile ahabhala hu Bethania bhala ilongo na bhabhili.
Isiku ilyalya fwata pali bha bhuya afume hu Bethania, ali ni nzala.
Alola ikwi ilya mtini amantyundu shahutali, abhala awenye huje agawezwa ahaje hahundti mwanya yakwe. Uwakati ula bhalaga wilyo, haga ahaga hahuthi ila amatundu, pipo hawali wakati mitini.
Alibhula, “Numo yayuthi uwa ilwa udundu afume huliwe nathele”. Asundwa bhahuvha.
Bhahinza hu Yelusalemu, wope ahinjila mushibhanza anda afumwe huzi abha kazwa nabhagula muhati iyikanisa. Agaluzanya imeza tana nwa nihela namatengo gabhala abhali bhakazwa injibha.
Haga aluhusu ya yunthi anyemule hahuthi mukanisa ahali hakaziwa.
Abhamanyizywa nayanje, “Lelo haga isimbilwe, 'nyumba yane ihaitwa ya labhe wabha panzi bhudti'? Lelo muvhishile ligwenyo lya bhafyula”.
Achungaji agosi hasimbi vhahuvha ishali ayanjile ilwa hugoje. Hata isho bhamwogopa pipo imbuga ihaswijiziwe namanyizye wakwe.
Shila wakati nishalyevhela pihafihaga, bhashilaga hujini.
Pali bhajenda nashaphi, bhalilola ikwi ili mutini lyumile paka pamakholo gakwe.
U Petulo ahinzuha nayanje, “Mwalimu! Enya, ikwiimitini ilyuhalilanile lyumile”.
U Yesu ajibule, “Mubhanje ni imani lelo mwa Ngulubhi.
Mwini imbabhula mubhanje ni imani ushili bhula igambaili, 'Epa, liwitaje lyilyo munsumbi khashele huli mashaka mmwoyo gwakwe lelo awamini ishayanjile shaibhoneha, isho shawanza Ungulubhi shawanza.
Lelo imbabhula: shila hatyu isha mushilavha nishamubhuzwa kwaajili yumwene, mwaminilaje huje poshala vhape vhwibhe vinyu.
Pala pamuwimilila na labhe, muwaziwa abhahumile hahundi amunaho ashizanye wabhene ashele hahuntyi ili uyise winyu uwali humwanya ambhahoshele amwe pia izwa mutulile.

Bhahafiha hu Yelusalemu nandele. Hata pali ajenda mushibhaza, bhaha bhalila agosi bhachungaji na asimbi na ashigosi.
Bhahabhula, “Mamulaka bhuli ubhomba amambo iga?” Wope yunanu uwa pelile ama mulaka huje ugabhombaje?”
U Yesu abhabhula, “Imbabhuzwa limo. Namwe mujibu khimba bhule huje nihumamulaka ashi ingabhomba iga.
Ulwozyo ulwa Yohana lwa hafuma humwanya au wabhanadamu? Ntabulili.”
Bhayangana bhene wa bhene bhahayanga, “Khashele khatuje, 'Wafumile humwanya', abhayanje, 'Mbona basi haga mwamwamini?'
Lelo khatuje wabhaha fuma wa bhanadamu,'....” Ibhahogopa abhantu, mana abhantu bhalolile uYohana huje kuwa kamili.
Bhahajibu uYesu bhayanga, “Hagatumenye. U Yesu abhula, “Wala ane simba bhula amwe humamulaka ashi ibhomba iga.
Ipo uYesu ahanda abhamanyizye huvhi fwani. Ayanga, “Umuntu atotile hugunda amizabibu, azyunguzwa ulubhaga, ahadiba ilina ilwa khandile ahamwele. Ahazenga ahantu atali bada yipo apanjizywa ugunda ugwimizabibu ashula isafali iya hutali.
Uwakati pawahafika hatu ma utumishi walimi imizabibu aposhele afume wabhene vimo ivimadudu gahugunda igimizabibu.
Lelo bhakata, bhakhoma nahanyizywa bila haiduhahutde.
Atuma utumishi uwinji bhavhahwalazywa mwitwe na hubhombele amambo agisoni.
Bado atuma uwinji, unuuwinji bha goga bhahabhombela abhinji amambo kama gigo, bhakoma bhamo bhabha goga.
Alisile umuntu umozaidi uwahutume, umwana uyangenwe. Wope aliwamwisho uwatumilwe wabhene. Ayanga, “Bhaza huheshimuu mwana wane”.
Lelo apangaji bhayanga na bhene kwa bhene, “Unu yuyo uwaliyhi. Izaji, natugoje, uhu ulithi uzabhewetu.”
Bhahavhamila, bhahagoga nahutaje huzi iyigunda gwa mizabibu.
Isho, Lelo ayibhomba bhuli utawala uwi gunda ili mizabibu? Ayinza na vhangamizywe abhalinza amizabibu na aipela abhanji ishamba ili mizabibu wa bhantu abhanji.
Hapete amanyile isimbo ili? “Iwe ilwa zenji bhalikhanile, lihabha liwe lwa nshinje.
Ili lihafuma wa Bwana, na liswizywa pamaso gityu.”
Bhahanza hukhate uYesu, Lelo bha hogopa umbungano. Pipo vhaminye huje bhayanjile ishifwano zaidi yao. Isho bhahaleha wabho.
Pipo bhahatuma bhamo na mahelodia wa mwene ili huteje hunongwa.
Pabhahafiha, bhahabhula, “Huje Mwalimo, tuminye huje haga usaga inzibho zhwazyunti haga ubhonesya apendelele pahati iya bhantu. Umanyizwa idala ilwa Ngulubhi pamwana lyoli. Lelo haki afumwe ikodi wakali sali au haa?
Lelo uYesu amenye aje bhalyeula na abhabhula, “Yenu munjela? Mbheli ihela injenye.”
Nabhayileta imo wa Yesu, Abhabhula, “Isura yana nu asimbo agagaliipa gananu? Bhayanga, “Ya Kaisari.”
U Yesu abhabhula, “Panji u Kaisari ivintu ivha Kaisari vavha Ngulubhi panji Ungulubhi.” Bhahaswiga.
Ipo Amasadukayo, abhayanga nahumo azywoshe, bhahabhalila. Bhabhuzya, bhahaga,
“Mwalimo, uMose atusimbile huje, 'Gashele uholo uwa muntu khafwile aleshile ushi khosi yakwe, lelo haga aleshile umwana, mutu ayimwenga ushi uwaholo, nawipatile abhana kwajili yaholo wakwe.'
Wali na holo saba, uwa wandilo ahamwega ula ushi afwa, haga ahaleha abhana.
Antele wope uwabhili amwega wope afwa, aleha abhana. Uwatatu wope shisho.
Nawa saba afwa bila aleshe abhana. Hu mwisho wakwe wope ushi ahafwa.
Uwakati uzyushe, pabhaizyuha nandtele, Ishi ayibhawananu? Maana bhala aholo bhunthi saba bhundthi bhali bhalume bhakwe.”
U Yesu abhabhula, Lelo! Ili sagalila huje mukhopilwe, pipo samuminye amasimbo wala ikhone ilwa Ngulubhi?”
Uwakati uwazyushe uwafume bhabhafile, haga bhayenga wala awinjile mundowa ila bhaibha na sha awandumi ahumwanya.
Lelo, ahusu abhafwe abhaizyuha, Lelo! Samwamanyila afume mushitabu isha Mose, ihabali ziha poli, shila Ungulubhi isha yanga abhula, 'Ani ni Ngulubhi uwa Ibulahimu, nani Ngulubhi Isaka, nani Ngulubhi uwa Yakobo?'
Umwene sa Ngulubhi uwa bhafwa, ila wali bhumi. Lili wazi atejile.”
uwa bhawasimbi ahenza ahuvha izyabhayangaga inongwa zyabho; alola huje uYesu abhajibule shinza. Ahabhuzya, “Lelo! amuli ishi ili mana ishilizywe zyunti?”
U Yesu ahajibula, “Ilimana yayini, “Uvha Israeli, U Bwana Ungulubhi uwetu, Bwana umo.
Ilazimiha hugane uBwana Ungulubhi uwaho, hunwoyo hwaho gwundti, huroho yaho yundti hunjele zyaho zyundti nawikhone lwaho lyundti.'
Iamuli iyabhili yayini, 'Iwanziwa ugane upalamani waho nishi amuli iyinje ingosi zaidi yizi.”
Usimbi ayanga, “Shinza Mwalimo! Uyanjile lyoli huje Ungulubhi aliumo na huje numo, uwinji zaidi yamwene.
Ugane umwene humwoyo gwundti, nahugane upalamani nishi puwiga ne wewe, nimuhimu mno kuliko uvifumwa nadhahibu izya lungulizye.”
Ulya Yesu pala pahalola ahafumwa ijibu ilinza, ayanga, “Awe haga ulihutali nu tawala uwa Ngulubhi.” Pipo numo hata umo uwa ajela hubhuzwe uYesu amaswali gagundti.
U Yesu ahajibu, lula uli amanyizya mushi vhanza ayanga, “Lelo! Asimbi bhayigabhuli huje uYesu Kilisiti ni mwana wa Daudi?
Daudi yuyo katika Roho Uuzelu, ayanjile, 'Bwana' ayanjile Bwana wane, khala kati yikho gwani hukhono ugwishulume pakaimbabhombe alugo pansi iyi magagagaho.'
U Daudi ahukuga Kilisiti, 'Bwana' Lelo! mwana wa Daudi nishi uli pugaishi gosi shimojile?”
Amanyizywe wakwe uYesu ayanga, “Muwiyenyeje nasimbi abhasugwa ajende ni kazu intali nalamuwe musokoni
na khale humatengo aga gosi umwaputile namu shikulukulu humaeneo agashigosi.
Natena bhalwa nyumba inzwainzwafwile bhala bha amaombi amatali sana abhantu khabha bhenyaje. Ibha abhantu bhaipaulozi uwa uli gosi.”
Pala uYesu akhala panzi apalamane ni phogoso isadaka muhati inyi shi bhaza. Ali abhenya abhenya abhandtu abhafumiga panyanga indalama muphogoso. Abhandtu abhinji atajili bhahabhehanyishe huwinji uwindalama.
Ushi ufwile umaskini ahenza naponye ivipande vibhili thamani yasenti.
Ipo abhakuga asundwa wakwe na bhabhule, “Amini imbabhula, ushi unu ufwile afumizwe agosi zaidi ya bhundti bhala amalizizizye apanye mpongoso iyisa ndaka.
Kwani bhundthi bhaponyizye elingananje huwinji uwivhi pato vhavho. Lelo ushiuda ufwile unu, afume humasikini wakwe, afumwa idalama yundti amabyo iziwanga.”
U Yesu pajendaga afume hushi bhaza, umo kati yabho asunda bhakwe ahabhuza, “Mwalimo, enya amawe gahunswisywa na mayumba!”
Abhula, Mugalola ayumba amagosi? Nalimo ilyalya isangala hatalimo pamwanya yilyenje ilyasa lya igwisiwa paka pansi”.
Nawope pali akhele pamwanya yi Gamba ilyi Mizaituni khosi ishibhanzu, Petulo, na Yakobo, Yohana nu Andeleya bhabhuzya husili,
“Tubhule, amambo igagaibhali? Na henu atenyeje amambo paga ifumila?”
U Yesu anda abhabhule, “Mubhanje maso umuntu yayundti asabhatezye.
Bhinji bhainza witawalwa ni bhaiyanga, 'Ane nene', na bhai bhatezya abhinji.
Pamwayuvha ivita na itetesi ili vita, mundawogope; amambo igalazima afumile, lelo umwisho gusili.
Insi iyifuma alye ninsi iyinje, utawala akhomane nutawala uwinji. Wayibha antezywa mwunti mwunti munsi, waibha ni zala. Uwo mwanzo wichungu.
Namwi munje maso. Munafisi nzyinyu maana bhai bhatwala amwe humabalaza nahusinagosi. Mwaikhomwa namwimwayegwa witanzi wa maliwali na watawala kwa ajili yalini, abheshuhuda wa bhene.
Lelo izyo lazima alumbililye wa pansi bhunti.
Paibhakata nabha vitwililye, munganje awogope huje munzayanje ayenu. Uwakati uwo, mungandasibhe izya munzayanje uwakati uwo pabhuzya saga mwimwe umzayanje ilyanza bhapele uwakati bhula; liyangaji maana sa mweme mwamuyanga yu Roho Uzelu.
Uholo aitaka uhola wakwe huje bhagoje nubaba nu mwana. Umwana ayepaasu ayise bhabho nabhagoje.
Mwayegwa nashila muntu hasababu iyitawa lyani. Lelo uwaijimba paka pamalishilo, umuntu uyo aipona.
Pailola ilyavitililye lyiwima pasaliwaziwa awime (imanyila amanyaje), epo abhali muhati iya Yuda bhanyilaje humagamba,
wope uyali wigulu anganda wishe aweje ivhapansi nyumba au aweje hahunti hali hunzi,
naulihugunda angandaa bhuye aweje umwenda gwakwe.
Lelo ole wabho abhashi abhikhanda nabhabha wonzya kati yisiku inzyo!
Mulabhaje huje ingandafumile uwakati uwisasa.
Maana waibha na malabha amagosi gala gasa gawahile afumile awande Ungulubhi paumbaga insi, pakaishi, na hamo wala haifumila andtele.
Bwana ugabhe haga azipunguzwaga insiku nanumo uwaponaga, lelo kwa ajili yate uliwa, azifupizye insiku izyo.
Umuda ugwo umuntu yayunti uwayibhabhula, Enyi, uKilisti ali ipa!' au 'Enyi, pala!' mungandawamini.

Imwanya ninsi zyainsinzanya, lelo amazyo gani haga insizanya na mwaha.

Lelo ula umalaika wabhola uganje, “Awogope Zakaria, eshi apute hwaohwo vwehwe. Na ushe waho Uzabeth aihupapila umwana. Olume na itawa lyakwe wayihumweta Yohana.

Na nyenye, ubhabhe bubu, sobhayanje, mpaka isiku lila nayayibhombeha. Ego kwasababu sewahovwezye enongwa zyane gape gayitimila huwakati wakwe.”

Eshi shambombeye UGOSI ensiku zila zyanenyizya esoni yane hwitagalilo elyabhantu.”
Umwezi uwa tanda umalaika uGabrieli asontezywe no NGOLOBHE abhalile mpaka mji wa hu Galilaya, itawa lyakwe Nazareti,
Hwa rendu ubikira ya pabhiliwa no muntu itawa lyakwe Yusufu. Wa hutali hwa Daudi, na itawa lyakwe ubikira uyo yu Mariamu.
Ahinjila munyumba yakwe wayanga, “Mwagona, upewewe eneema! no GOSI alipandwemo nawe.”
Wapa ashelile tee afwatana nenongwazyakwe. Asebha humwoyo endamuho ene yeshe.
Umalaika abhola, “Ugaje hogope, Mariamu, afwanaje upate eneema afume hwa NGOLOBHE.
Enya ubhahweje, uyanda na pape umewna ulume, na itawa lyakwe ubha hwumwete u 'Yesu.'
Oyo aibha GOSI abhahwetwe mwana yali humwanya uGOSI UNGOLOBHE alihupela itengo elye umwene u Daudi use wakwe.
Abhaitawale ekhaya eya Yakobo wilawila na umwene wakwe sewayibha no umalisholo.
UMariamu wabhola umalaika, zibhabhe wele enongwa ezi, afwanaje semenye ulume?
UMalaika wajibu wabhola, “Upepo Uselu abhahumwenzele pamwanya yaho, na engulu zyakwe yalipamwanya zibhahu vwenwsye. Neshe izyongozi afwatanaje oyo yayipapwa ayibha zelu mwana wa NGOLOBHE.
Antele, enye uholo waho Elizabeti wape apete ulyanda ulya mwana ulume.
Afwatanaje nalimo izu lyasagaliwezehala hwa NGOLOBHE.”
UMariamu wayanga, “Waga, enye ane endi wembombo wa GOSI. Ebhehuline neshe shoyajele.” Antele umalaika wasogola wabhala hwamwahale.
Basi u Mariamu wasogola ensiku ezyo wabhola hata ensi ya humagamba nanali mpaka ensi emo ya hwa Yudea.
Winjelo munyumba mwa Zekaria walamuha u Elizabeti.
Yabha, Elizabeti nahwovwa hula alamushe kwakwe uMariamu, ahana ahela handa ahwanje mvyanda vyakwe, Elizabeti wamema opepo Uzelu.
Wakhola hwizu elyemaha wanyaga usayilye, “Hwabhashe bhonti nawe empapwo yaho esaiwe.
Unfumiye izu eli, hata omaye uwu GOSI wane anenzelene?
Nenshe izu ilyalamusha gane ahana ahela hanga hasongwelwe mhati mvyanda vyane.
Wape nafu yayovyezye neshe naga itimila gabholelwe no GOSI.”
Omariamu wayanga, omwoyo gwane gwamwenye ONGOLOBHE,
Roho yane esongwezye ONGOLOBHE yanauye ane.
Afwanaje agwenyizye unyonge uwe mbombo wakwe. Eshe, enyaga ahwandileshi evikholo vyonti vyayikwizya osayilwe.
Afwatanaje owemaha ambombeye amagasi, lyape itawalyakwa lizelu.
ERehema zyakwe zidela evikholo ne vikholo hwebho bhahahuputa.
Abhombile amaha uhukhono gwakwe; abhanyampenye abhemashento afume masebho ezye moyo gabho.
Abhagwisizye agosi mmatengo gabho ageshimwene na nyonge abhabhosezye.
Abhenzala abhakutizizye aminza, bhape abhemali abhefwizye makhono wene.
Amwavwizye u Israeli uwembombo wakwa ili ahwizushe rehema zyakwe.
(Neshe shubhabhozezye ababa bhetu) Ibrahimu empapwo yakwe mpaka welawila.”
UMariamu wakhala nawo mpaka amezi gatatu nantele wawela abheale akhayayakwe.
Zyabha ensiku ezya pape hwakwe u Elizabeti nazya timila, wapapa umwana lume.
Bhahovwezye ajirani na mwabho bhakwe, aje GOSI amwonjezyezye erehema bhasongwa pandwemo nao.
Lyabha isiku elya nane wakati wa kutahiri omwana. Bhahanza hupele itawa elyayise, “Zakaria,”
Unyino wakwe wagalula wayanga, “Nkashele; seshasho basi ayibha yo Yohana.”
Bhabhola sepali amuntu afume hwamwenyu bhaho akwiziwe itawa elya Yohana.
Bhamwanya usewakwe sabhu hwmwete.
Wanza ahabampa wasimba aje, “itawa lyakwe yo Yohana.” Bhaswijitie bhonti.
Pepo na pepo ilomu lyakwe liguha numele lyakwe antele wanda ayaje. Nautelele ONGOLOBHE.
Bhinjilwa nowoga bhonti bhali bhakheye pandwemo, na. mambo ego gonti gatangazezwe ensi yonti yammagamba mgamba e Yudea.
Na bhonti bhabhagovwezye bhagabheha humoyo gabho, bhayanga, “Umwana uno ayibha wefwane hwele?” Afwaneje ukhono ogwa GOSI gwali pandwemo no mwane.
UZakaria uyise wamema opepo ozelu, wakuwawanyanga,
“Abhosewe OGSI, ONGOLOBHE wa Israeli, afwanaje abhenzeye abhantu bhakwe na bhaule.
Atemelesezye empeta eyataule afume mlyango ugwa Daudi, uwe mbombo wakwe.
Nenshe ayanjile afume huwandilo hwilumu elyakuwe akuwe bhakwe azelu.
Tisatulwe na bhibhi bhentu na mma khono gabho bhonti bhabhativitwa
Ili abhabhombele aminza ababa bhetu na hwizushe ipatano lyakwe izelu,
Ishilapo shalapiye Ibrahimu uyise wetu.
Afwanaje anzatavwilizya ate taushe nimakhono gabhibhi bhetu na humpute bila woga.
Nazelu nelyoli hwitagalilo lyakwe ensiku zyonti.
Nawe, womwana wahwetwa, ukuwe ukuwe wakwe yalimwanya, afwaneje awa wayitangulila hwita galila humaso ega GOSI ulenga nyizizye amadala gakwe,
Obhabhozye abhantu bhakwa usatule aje asajilwe embibhi zyabho.
Hwidala elye rehema lya NGOLOBHE wetu, afwatanaje hwezyo okhozyo lwalufumile amwanya lutifishiye,
Abhakhozye bhabhakhala hukisi hunzunda eyenfwa. nagalongozwa unamana getu hwidala ilinza.”
Ula, mwana wakula wonjelela amaha roho wakhala humapoli hata hwisiku elye fumila hwakwe u Israeli.
Enku zila endajizyo zyafumile hwa Kaisari Agusto ya je esimbwe eye matawa aga bhantu wonti mnsi.
Hii ilikuwa ene ebabhe ya hwande yehasimbwilwe epo Krenio nali liwali wa hushamu.
Abhantu wonti bhabhalile ahwinsimbisizye shila muntu amwao.
UYusufu wape asogoye hu galilaya afume hushijiji sha hu Nazareti azubhile abhale huu Yudea hadi humji ugwa Daudi, gukwiziwa Bethelehemu, afwatanaje umwahale wahutayari namwao abhahwa Daudi.
Ili asimbwe pandwemo no Mariamu, ushe wakwe bhapabhiliye wape ano lwanda.
Shabha katika akhale ohwo ensiku zyakwe ezya pape zya fishile.
Wapapa umwana wakwe uwahwande, wavwenesya amenda agubha na wagonia mwitori mwanzilela eng'ombe, afwanaje sebhapete enafsi munyumba ezya jenyi.
Na ensi yeyela, bhahali adimi bhakhalaga mwipoli na linde ikundi lwao bhatandilunaga nosiku.
Umalaika wa GOSI abhafumiye, nanali uzelu wa GOSI wabhakhozizye epande zyonti, bhinjilwa nowoga ogosi.
Umalaika abhabholele, “Mganje ahigope, afanaje ane embaletela enongwa enyinza eya she engosi yayayibho hwabantu wonti.
Eshe sanyono mnsi eya Daudi! apepwe kwa jili eyahulimwe uwataule wape yu Kristo GOSO!
Na ene ndiyo ndago hwilimwe, mbhahu mwaje umwa umwela bhavwenesyezye amenda ageshiwela agonile mwitori mwelela eng'ombe.
Nantele bhahali pandwemo nayo omalaika abhinji ajeshi abhamwanya bhahutelela ONGOLOBHE, na ya je,
“ Ayemehwaje ONGOLOBHE amwanya, na pansi ehwe amani hwabhantu bhabhagalile.”
Shabha, omalaika ebho na bhasogola abhule hwabho amwanya bhala udimi bhabholene, “Eshe sali mpaka Bethlehemu, tilirole elwo lwali bhombeshe lyati bhonezyezye ONGOLOBHE.”
Bhabhalile nanali, bhamwanjile oMariamu no Yusufu, nola umwana umwela agonile mwitori.
Na walipomwona bhafumizye enongwa yabhabholelwe afwatone nomwana oyo.
Wonti bhabhahovwezye bhaswijile hwago gabhobholelwe na dimi.
Lelo o Mariamu wazibhaha humwoyo gwakwe.
Bhala adimi bhawelile ohu bhahusomba ONGOLOBHE na hutelile humombo gonti gabhovwezye na galale eshe shabhabholelwe.
Hata nazyafishele ensiku nana ezya hutahiri ahetelwe tawa lwakwe Yesu, neshe nahetelwe no malaika sasele abhe lwanda.
Alafu nazyafishele ensiku hwabho, neshe sheri endogo ya anusa bhabhalile nao mpaka Yerusalemu bhabheshele OGOSI.
Neshe nshesibwilwe mdogo ya GOSI, “Shila mwana ulume wali lwanda ulwahwanda hwanyinawakwe akwiziwaje Golosu wa GOSI.”
Bhafumye sadaka neshe sheyajile katika endogo eya GOSI, “Enko nda bhabhele au makind abhenjebha bhabhele.”
Enya, pala payerusalemu palinomntu itawa lyakwe akwiziwaga Simoni. Umuntu ono alihwelyoli na humpute ONGOLOBHE. Umwahole agolaga ya zizya wa Israeli, na upepo uzelu ali pamwana yakwe.
Yali imalishe abhoneshewe hwakwe ahilile hupepo uzelu aje umwahale saga ehenzaga afwe bila hulole Kristi wa GOSI.
Isikulimo ahenzele mhatimwibhaiza alongozehwe no pepo uzelu. ambapo ayise bhakwe bhaletile umwana oYesu hubhombele gala gagahanziwuga mkawaida eye ndogo,
Eshi o Simioni aposheye mmakhono gakwe na hulimbe ONGOLOBHE na yanje,
“Eshi nduhusu nemtumwa waho embale mshinza alengane nizu lyaho.
Afwatanaje amaso gane gahalile uwaule waho,
Afwanaje uonesha humaso gabhantu bhonti.
Umwahale rukhozyo mataifa na bhe zelu wabhantu bhakwe Israeli.”
UYise nonyine wakwe bhali bhaswiga ego gagayangwilwe juu yakwe.
OSimoni wabhasaila abhabhola Mariamu unyina wakwe, “Eye ono abhehwelwe wagwe na bhoshe abhinji bhabali kati Israeli na bhe mbonesyo zyazya yiyangwa.
Nawe hwehwe imaje lwaijila humwoyo gwaho ilizibhoneshe esebho ezya moyo aga bhinji.”
Ahali ukuwa ushe itawa lyakwe Ana uledu wa Fanueli wa shikholo sha Asheri. Nu umri wakwe alina maha minji. Akheye nolume amaha saba baada eyelendu wakwe,
Wape fwele owemaha amarongo nane na mahaganne. Sasogolo mwibhanza ila aputa usiku no sanya na funje na labhe.
Oyo afumele sala yeyo asalifizye ONGOLOBHE. Na wonti bhali bhahwenyelezya eshahwaulwe katika Yerusalemu abhafumizyo enongwa zyakwe.
Basi nabhamala gonti gagalajiziwe aga mndongozi eya GOSi, bhahwelile hu Galilaya, mpaka iboma lwao, Nazareti.
Ola umwana wakula, na hwonjele amahaa amemile enshinshi, na neema ya NGOLOBHE yali juu yakwe.
Basi ayise bhakwe bhabhala hu Yerusalemu shila mwaha uwakati uweshikurukuru ya Pasaka.
Na fishiye umri wakwe amaha kumi na gabhle bhazubhile neshe sheli emila eye shikurukuru.
Nabhamalila ensiku wakati uwahwele hwabhoola umwana uYesu asageye hwisaro ohwo hu Yerusalemu na bhayise bhakwe sebhalolene.
Bhape bhamenyeje bhalipandwemo mshora, bhabhalile enjendo uwisiku lyonti bhanda humwanza mwa mwabho.
Nu sebhamwanga bhahwelile hu Yerusalemu ohu bhahumwanza.
Yabha na zyafiha ensiku zitatu, bhalola mwibhinza, akheye pahati ya manyizi, abhatejelezya nabhabhozye amaswali.
Wape wonti bhabhamwovwaga bhanswijile uwelewa wakwe na amajibu gakwe.
Na bhalolile, bhanswijile. Nonyina wakwe wabhola, “Mwana wane, mbone otibhombeye eshi? enye, uyise waho nane talili humwanza uzugumie”
Wabhabhola, “Yenu mnanza sagamwamenye aje ehwanziwa akhale munyumba eya yise wane?
Unape sebhalyelewe izu elyo lyabha bhozezye.
Hwiho pandwemo nabho mpaka hu Nazareti wape ali abeshimu, onyina agabheshele ego gonti humwoyo gwakwe.
Wape uYesu wazidi ahwonjelele katika hekima kimo, wapendezya ONGOLOBHE na bhantu.
Umwaha, ugwa kumi na tano owalongozye hwakwe Kaisari Tiberia, Pantio Pilato nali liwali owayahudi, na Herode omwene owa Galilaya, no Filipo oholo wakwe omwene uwa Iturea nensi eya Trakoniti, na Lisania no mwene owa Abilene,
Wakati owa kohani ogosi owa anasi no Kayafa, izu elya NGOLOBHE lya fishiye oYohana omwana owa Zakaria, mwipoli.
Afishele mnsi yonti yelikaribu ne Yordani, alombeleye owoziwa owa lete usajilwa olwa hwefwe embibhi.
Neshe shahwasimbilwe chuo eshe mazu aga kuwe Isaya, “Izu ya mntu wali mwipoli, “Lilenganyi idala elya GOSI, gagalosyaji omwashile hwakwe.
Entebha yonti yayimema nigamba nagamba hayisiwa, papatejile payibha pagoloshe papakwanyushe paile nganiha.
Bhonti abhebele bhayihulo owaule owa NGOLOBHE.”
Basi, abhabholele amabongano bhala bhabhaliye ili abhoziwe amwe mpapwo wenzoha wenu yabhasundile amwe ayinjile enkuni yehayenza?
Basi fumyaje amadondo gagahwanziwa ulusajilo, wala mgajeahwanza ayanje mmoyo genyu, “Tilinawo udada uIbrahimu eshi embabhola yaje amawe ega, ONGOLOBHE abhajiye ahwubhosrzye uIbrahimu abhana.
Neshi etwanga tayari ebhehwelwe pamashinshi age makwi. Basi, kila likwi lya sagalipapa amadondo aminza, lidumlwa nalitaje mmwoto.
Amabungano gabhozya, “Tikhozye wole eshi?”
Wabhajibu wabhabhozya, “Yali na magolola gabhele na apele yasaga aunigolola yali nevyalye wape abhombe eshoshesho.”
Bhabhasonjezya bhape bhenza ahwoziwe, bhabhozya,”Manyiziji, tubhombe yenu ate?
Wabhabhola, “Mgaje sonjezye ahantu zaidi ya hata hahapangwilwe.
Asikali bhape bhabhozya bhayanga, “ate nate tibhombe wele? Wabhabhole msafwele omntu wala msashitake ilenka antele myanje no mshahara gwenyu.”
Basi, abhantu nabhali bhabhagola gaganzafumile, wonti bhasega sebhaga mmoyo gabho enongwa ezya Yohana nkashe umwene Kristi.
UYohana wagalula wabhabhozya bhonti lyoli ane embozya namenze lelo ahwenza ohwemaha ashile ane sembwezizye ayengezye olwabho olye vilato vyakwe. omwahale ayibhoziwa hupepo ozelu no mwoto.
Afwanaje ubheto lwakwa lulimakho no wape ayozya tee mhati yakwe na bhonganye engano yakwe. Mshanga, antele amapetelo aigapemba mmwoto gwa sagaguzima.
Basi hurusundo hugamwabho aminji, abhalombeleye abhantu.
Lelo omwene oHerode akhalipiwe nomwe kwajili ya Herode, ushe wa holo wakwe, namabhibhi gonti gabhombile o Herode.
Ahonjezye eli neli afunjile oyohani mwijela.
Bhabhantu wonti bhabhamaushe ahinziwe no Yesu wape ahoziwe wape alabhile emwanya zya higushe.
Upepo uzelu ahishile pamwanya yakwe hufwano ongwebelebele, neshe enjebha izu lya fumile amwanya, “Awe wemwana wane wegene. Ensogwezewe nawe.”
No Yesu yoyo nahandile amanyizye, ali apate umri wakwe neshe amaha salathini. ategemelwa ajemwana wa Yusufu, wa Eli,
Wo Mathati, walawi, wa MeIki, wayana wa Yusufu,
Wa Matathia, wa Amosi, wa Nahumu, wa Esli, wa Nagai,
Wa Maati, wa Matathia, wa Semeini, wa Yusufu, wa Yuda,
Wa Yohana, wa Rese, wa Zerubabeli, wa SheaItieli, wa Neri,
MeIki, wa Adi, wa Kosamu, wa Elmadamu, wa Eri,
Wa Yoshua, wa Eliezeri, wa Yorimu, wa Matathi, wa Lawi,
Wa Simioni, wa Yuda, wa Yusufu, wa Yonamu, wa Eliyakimu,
Wa Melea, wa Mena, wa Matatha, wa nathani, wa Daudi,
Wa Yese, wa Obedi, wa Boazi wa Salmoni, wa Nashoni,
Wa Abinadabu, wa Aramu, wa Hesroni, wa Peresi, wa Yuda,
Wa Yakobo, wa Isaka, wa Ibrahimu, wa Tera, wa Nahori,
Wa Seruig, wa Ragau, wa Pelegi, wa Eberi, wa Sala,
Wa Kenani, wa Arfaksadi, wa Shemu, wa Nuhu, wa Lameki,
Wa Methusela, wa Henoko, wa Yaredi, wa Mahalalei, wa Kenani,
Wa Enoshi, wa Sethi, wa Adamu, wa NGOLOBHE.
UYesu amemile upepo uzelu, ahwelile afume hu Yordani, alongoziwe no pepo omuda ohwe nsiku arobaini mwipoli.
Apete amalabha no shetani. Nensiku ezyo sagalyanga ahantu mpaka nazyamalishe alolile enzala.
Oshetani wabholankoli, “Mwana wa NGOLOBHE, libhole ihwe eli wahe libumnga.”
UYesu agalula, “isimbwilwe: 'eyaje umntu sagaikhala hwibumunda tu.'”
Wizavwa pamwanya wabhonesya emilki zyonti ezyensi hudaka emo.
Oshetani wabhola, “Embahupele ahweenzi ene yonti, nefahari yakwe. Afanaje ehweli makhono gane, nane ehupele yayonti neshe shensongwele.
Basi ahwe nkoni namile hwitagalila lyane gonti ganzabhe gahuliwe.”
UYesu wagalula wabhola isimbwilwe, “omwinamile, “OGOSI ONGOLOBHE waho ompute omwahale mwene.”
Walongozya mpaka Yerusalemu wabheha pamwanya yemnala eshe shibhanza,” wabhola nkashile olimwana wa NGOLOBHE hwiponye pasi.
afwanaje esimbwilwe”, abhahwu lajizizye amalaika bhakwe bhalinde,
Na fwanaje, makhono gabho bhanzahumweje, osije ogabomula inama, lwaho mwiwe.”
OYesu wagalula, “Wabhashole, “eyagwilwe oganje hulenje GOSI ONGOLOBHE waho.”
Basi nawamala kila esha hulenje oshetani walehe wabhala humuda.
OYesu awelile humaha age opepo ozelu, wabhala hu Galilaya enongwa zyakwe zyazyambanile ensi zyonti ezya msheje msheje.
Wape asambelezyaga katika mmabhanza gabho ashimihwagwa nabhantu bhonti.
Wabhala hu Nazareti, epo pasongwelwe na isiku elye lutozyo hwinjila mwabhonza neshe sehali edeesturi yakwe wemelela ili abhazye.
Bhapela chuo esha akuwa Isaya, hwigula echuo, wanza papa simbwilwe,
Opepo owa GOSI au pamwanya yane afwatanaje amponyizye amafuta abhalombelele apena enongwa enyinza, antumile abhatangazizye bhabhapi nyilwe abhaule hwabho. Avipofu bhalolaje nantele abhaleshe bhashe huru bhabhabhonelwe.
Na tangazya omwaha ogwa GOSI gwagweteshehwe.
Washigalilo echuo, wahwezezya amtumishi wakhala, na bhantu bhonti bhabhahali mwisinagogi bhalangulila.
Wanda abhabhole sanyono ensimbo,”Ezi zitimiliye mmakutu genyu.”
Bhalola bhonti bhaswiga amazu age neema gagafumile mwilomu lyakwe, bhayanga ono semwana wa Yusufu?
Abhabhola, “bila shaka mbhambole eshilale eshi,” Ganga, hwiponye omwoyo gwaho, amambo gonti gatovwezye aje gabhombeshe hu Kapernaumu, gabhombeshe nepa na ntele katika ensi yaho wewe.”
Wayanga, “Amina embabhola aje nomo okuwa yabhahweteshewe mnsi ya kwa yoyo,”
Lelo lyoli embabhola bhahali afwele bhalibhinji katika ensi eya Israeli amaha aga Eliya, wakati amabhengo gafugwilwe amaha gatatu na miezi sita, enzala engosi yahinjiye ensi yonti.
Wala oEliya sagasontezyewe hwebho, ila hwafwele omo owa Sarepta katika ensi eya Sidoni.
Antele, bhahali abheukoma bhinji mwi Israeli omwaha wa kuwa Elisha, wala nomo yaponi ila oNaamani omntu wa Siria.
Bhamemile ilyoyo bhonti bhabhahali mwibhanza nabhovwa ego.
Bhasogola bhafumya hwonze eye boma bhantwala mpaka mshenje eyigamba, afanaje ekhaya yao enzegwilwe pamwanya yakwe, ili bhapate hutaje pansi.
Lelo omwahale ashilile pahati yao wabhola.
Hwiha mpaka hu Kaeernaumu, iboma elya Galilaya. Wabha asambelezwa isiku elya tunzye.
Bhanswiga nantele hunsambelezyo zyakwe, afwanaje izu lyakwe lili namaha.
Na mhati mwibhanza, mwoli omntu yali ne roho embibhi walila hwizu igosi,
“ Wayanga leha, endineye awe, u Yese wa Nazareti? uyenzele atitezye? Emenye aje hwewenu! wogolosu wa NGOLOBHE!”
QYesu wadamila, “Wayanga, biba ilomu mwepe ndipo lila!”Ipepo lya gwisya pahati, lyafuma asimbhombe nkahamo.
Bhakhatwa naswije bhont, bhayangana, bhayanga lizu hwele eli, afwatanaje, “abhatanga amapepo abhibhi huwezo na maha bhape bhafuma.”
Enongwa, zyakwe zyazyambona hwonti munsi ela.
Wafuma mwibhanza winjila munyumba ya Simoni. Wape, okhoi wakwe oSimoni onyina washe wakwe, akhetwe nensugusa ekhali bhalabha kwajili yakwe.
Hwemelela, papepe nao, waidamila ela ensugasa, yaleha mara eyo wapona wabhabhombela.
Na isanya nalya swanga, wonti bhali nabhinu abhe mpongo shahashaha bhabhaletile hwamwahale. Wabhabheha amakhon gakwe pamwanya ya shila mntu wabhaponia.
Ipepo bhape bhafumela mwabhantu abhinji bhakhoma ibwago nayanje, “Awe uli mwana wa NGOLOBHE!” Wabhadamila sagaleshile aje bhayangaje, kwasababu bhamanye aje yo Krisi.
Na hwasha, asogoye abhalile humo hwasehulina bhantu. Amabongano bhabha bhahumwanza bhafihahwamurahale bhazaga huzubhile agajesogola hwabhahale.
Wabhabhola, “Ehwanziwa alombelele enongwa enyinza ezya mwene uwa NGOLOBHE katika amaboma agamwabho nantele, afwanaje ensotelezewe.
“Basi ali alombelela katika amabhanza aga hu Uyahudi.
Yabha amabongono bhasonshezya alitejelezye izu elya NGOLOBHE, omwahule ali ayemeleye panshenje eye eyi dimi lya Genezareti.
Walola evyelelo vibhele vikheye panshenje eyi dimi. Lelo bhabhahwonza bhafumile bhahwozya enyavu zyabho.
Winjila mshelelo shimo, esho shakwe oSimoni, wamwanza ashibhesha hutali hashe neshe. Wakhala wabhamanyinzya mambongano ohu alimshelelo.
Hata nawamala ayanje, abholile oSimoni, “Isya mpaka pansi tee mwisye enyavuzyenyu mwonze esamaki.”
OSimoni wagalula wabhola, Gosi, tibhombile embombo eyalisye nosiku wonti setipete nkahamo, lelo hwizu lyaho ehwisya enyavu.
Basi nabhabhomba esho bhazyajile esamaki ziminji tee enyavu zyao zya hundile adumushe.
Bhabhapunjila okhono amwabho bhali mshombo esha bhele. bhenze abhavwe bhenzu bhavimemya vyonti vibhele hata nyahandile andwine.
OSimoni oPetro, na walola ego, agwiye pamafugamo ga Yesuwanyanga sogala hwiline, “Afwatanaj, ane endi mntu uwembibhi GOSI.”
Afwanaje akhetwe nenswigo, umwahale nabhonti bhabhali pa ndwemo nawo kwa sababu eyewinji uwesamaki wabhazyajili.
Antele Yakobo no Yohana bha Zebedao, bhali pandwemo no Simoni. O Yesu wabhola Simoni, “ogaje hwogope, afume eshi obhabha wahwonza abhantu.”
Hata nabhali bhavisagamishe pwani, evyelelo vyabho bhavileha vionti bhabhenjelela.
Yabha nahali humiongo ye maboma gala enya, palinomntu amemile ukoma, wape nawalola oYesu, agwiye dumbula walabha waga, GOSI,” nkohwanza owezizye anozye.”
Kisha Yesu alinyoosha mkono wake na kumugusa, akisema, “Nataka. Takasika.” Na saa ileile ukoma ukamwacha.
“Wakhana agaje hubhole omuntu, ila bhalaga ahwibhonesya hwa kohani, “ufumye, kwajili eya pone hwaho neshe oMusa shabhabholele ebhe ushuda, hwabhahale.”
Lelo enongwa zyakwa zyazida abwaje bhatangene amabongono aminji bhatejelezye na pone empungo zyabho.
Ilelo omwahale ali ahwiyefwa wabhala pasepali bhantu walabha.
Yabha isiku lila limo ali asambelezya na amafarisayo na amanyizi abhe ndongo bhali bhakheye epo, bhabhafumile kila shijiji eshe Galilaya na Yudea, na hu Yerusalemu. Na amaha aga GOSI wahali apate aponie.
Na enya, bhenza abhantu bhanyatiye mshitanda omntu yapoozile, bhahanzaga hutwale mhati na hubheshe hwitagalila lyakwe.
Hata nabhakosile enafsi eyahutwale mhati kwali eya mabungano ege bhantu bhazubhile hwigolo bhagefwa amatofali agapamwanya bhaswisya umwahale neshi tande shakwe pahati hwitagalila hwa Yesu.
Wape nalolile olweteho lwabho abhhdde, “Ee rafiki, usajilwe embibhi zyaho.”
Basi bhala asimbi na Mafarisayo bhada ayangane, “Aje wenu ono yayanga amazu agalije? Wenu yagasajila embibhi aliyo NGOLOBHE mwene?”
Na o Yesu, omenye onongwa zyabho wabhagalula wabhabhole, mhwibhozya yenu lumoyo genu?
Lyalili lyalolo lyalilihu, 'Aje usajilwe embibhi zyaho au aje sogola ubhale?'
Lelo mpate amanye aje omwana wa Adamu anazyo endajizo pansi epa ezya sajile embibhi, abholele, 'Ola ya poozile sogolahwitweshe eshitanda shaho bhalaga akhaya yaho.'
Shesho wemelela hwitagalila lyabho wahwitwehe shhila shagoneye wabhala akhaya yakwe ohwo wa mwembela ONGOLOBHE.
Wonti bhakhetwa na nswije bhateleye ONGOLOBHE. Bhamemele nowoga, bhayanga, “Sanyono tilolile amambo age ajabu.”
Baada yego wafuma walola yasonjezya esonga, itawa lyakwe yolawi akheye forodhani, wabhola nbejezye.”
Walehe vyonti wasogola wabheni ezya.
Na Lawi wabhombela eshikurunkuru eshigosi mnyumba yakwe hwali abungono ogosi, owa sonjezye esonga na bhuntu abhamwabho bhali bhakheye pashalye pandwemo nawo.
Yabha afarisayo na simbi bhabho bhabha bhabha una asambilizi wa bhakwe baje mbona mlyana mwele pandwemo nabhabhasonjezya esonga na bhubhali nembibhi?”
OYesu agalula wabhabhola, “Bhabhali bhinza sebhani nehaja eyaponywe, ila bhala bhabhinile.
Senahenzele abhakwinzye abhelyoli bali bhahali nembibhi bhapato alambe.”
Bhape bhabhola, “Asambelewa abha Yohana bhafunga maranyinji, na labhe eputo bhpe asambelewa abha Farisayo bhafunga. Lelo asambelewa bhaho bhalya nu mwele.”
LelooYesu abhubholele, “Mwagaga mgabhabhambo aje bhafunje bhabha anilye huhweji wakati ahweli ogosi owehweji pandwemo nao?
Lelo ennsiku zihwenza nayepe ogosi owehweje epo pabha ifunga ensiku ezyo.”
Wabhabhola eshilale. “Nomo yazembula shilakaeshi omwenda opya nabheshe mmwenda okolo na nkashile abheshele lila ipya. Na shila ishiraka sha omwenda opya, selilenganya na gula omwenda okolo.
Wala, nomo omntu yaponya edivai empya katika evyelelo evikolo. Na nkashile waponya ela, edivai empya ebha vibazule vila evyenlelo, edivai enyahale ebhahwitishe na vyelelo nibhanachishe.
Lelo edivai epya uwinza uwaponye katika evye lelo evipya.
Wala nomo yamwela edivai eyemwaha alafu ayisongwe epya, atafanaje ayanga ela eya mwaha, 'Yenyiza.”
Lyabha isiku elyatozye limo ali ashila katika mmagonda, asambelezyewabhakwe bhali bhadenya amasale na galye bhabhabhapalula mmakhono gabho.
Basi bhamo afarisayo bhabhabholo, “Mbona mbhomba lya selinza isiku elyatozye”?
OYesu, wabhagalula, wabhabhola, “Semwabhazizye hata lwelyo lyabhomile oDaudi nali nenzala, omwahale na bhala bhali nabho?
Jinsi shahinjiye katika enyumba eye NGOLOBHE, wega amabumunda gala agalanjizye wagalya, wabhapela nebho amwabho wakati seshinza agalye ila hwa Kuhani bene basi.”
Wabhabhola, “Amwana uwa Adamu yayoyo OGOSI owa tofye.”
Yabha isiku elyatozye elyamwabho ahinjiye mwisingogi wamanyizya na mwali omntu ambaye okho. Ogwakwe ogwendelo upozile.
Na simbi na bhafarisayo bhali bhauzijila ili balole aje abhaponie isiku elyatozye, li bhazyaje enongwa zyautake.
Lelo omwahale wagamanya gabhasebha wabhola ola yapoozile okhono, “Sogola, emelela pahati wasogola.”wemelela.
Eshi OYesu wabhabhola, “Embabozya amwe eshi, shinza isiku elyatozya abhombe aminza au abhombe amabhibhi, aponie omwoyo au atezye,
“Walangulila amaso wonti.”Epande zyonti wabhola ola omntu, golozya okhono gwaho wagolozya akhono gwakwe gwabha gwinza natele.
Lelo bhamemile nenkuni bhaynyana bhebho hwa bhebho bhabhombe we le Oyesu.
Yali ensiku zila asogoye abhalile mwigamba ili alabha. Ahendeleye osiku wonti hulabhe ONGOLOBHE.
Nayali sampwiti, abhakwizizye asambelezewe bhakwe, hwumwahale na abhasaluye kumi na bhabhele kati yabho bhebho nantele abhakwizizye “Bhamwa.”
Amatawa gabhala atumwa gali oSimioni (ambaye antele akwizizye yo Petro) no Andrea no holo wakwe, oYakobo, oYohana, oFilipo, oBartolomayo,
OMathayo, oTomaso, no Yakobo omwa wa Alfayo, oSimioni, ola okwiziwaga yo Zelote,
OYuda omwana wa Yakobo na oYuda oIskariote, ola yali goji.
Nantele oYesu ahishile pandwemo nabho afume hwigamba na hwemelele papali ntebha. Idadi engosi eyasambelezewa bhakwe (walikuwa huko, pamoja naidadi kubwa ya watu kutoka Uyahudi na Yerusalemu, na kutoka pwani ya Tiro na Sidoni.)
Na bhala bhabhalebhile ni mpepo embibhi. Bhaponizye.
Shila omo bhabhali pibhongano arenjele hu palamasye afwatanaje nguvu ezyaponye zyali zifuma mhati yakwe na aponizye bhonti.
Esho wabhenya amnyiziwa bhakwe, na yanje, “Msayilwe amwe mwemli bhapene, afwatanaje umwene owa NGOLOBHE wenyu.
Msayilwe amwe mwemli nenzala eshi, afwanaje mwakuta msayilwe mwemlila eshi. Afwanaje mwayiseha.
Msayilwe amwe ambao abhantu na yibhavitwa na bhahagule na bhalongonye amwe aje mlibhabhibhi kwajili ya omwana wa Adamu.
Shanji katika isiku elyo na rushe rushe nashe afwatanaje lyoli mwayibha ne thawabu egosi amwanya, afwanaje aise bhabho bhabhabhombeye shesho akuwa.
Lelo hele amwe mwemli bhatakili! Afwatanaje mmalishe ahweje ensombo zyenyu.
Aheli amwe mwemkute eshi! afwanaje mwayilola enzala hwitagalila. Aheli amwe mwemseha eshi! Afwanaje mwayizonda naline hwitagalila.
Aheli amwe, na mwasombwa nabhantu wonti! Afwanaje aYise bhabho bhabhabhombeye akuwa abhilenka shesha.
Lelo eyanga hwilimwe amwe mwemn tejelezya, bhagani abhibhi bhenyu na bhabhombele aminza bhabhavitwa.
Bhasayilaji bhala bhabhaswita amwena bhalabhilaji bhala bhabhabonela.
Hwamwahale ola yahukhoma imbuguzi limo, ugalusizyaje elyabhele. Neshe omntu ahufyola igolole lyaho opanje nelyabhele.
Opanje shila ya hulabha. Neshe omntu nkahufyola ahantu ambaho hahuliwe uganje alabha aje awezyezye.
Nenshe samsongwa abhantu aje sabhabhabhombele, namwe mubhombaje shesho.
Nkashe mubhaganaabhantu bhabhaibhaga na amwe tu, esho ihawobu shi hwilimwe? Afwanaje hata bhabhibhi bhabha gana bhala bhabhagana.
Nkashile mubhabhombela bhala bhabhabhombela amwe aminza esho abhabhe thawabu nshi hwilimwe? Afwanaje hata bhabhibhi bhabhombashesho.
Nkashile mkhopezya evintu hwabhantu ambabho mpambamala aje bhanza abhawezyezye, eyo thawabu ushi hwilimwe? Hata bhabhibhi bhabhakhopela abhibhi, na bhapambamala ahwejelele kiasi shesho nantele.
Lelo bhagani abhibhi bhenyu na bhabhombele aminza. Bhakhopelaji mgaje ahogepe ahusu awezyewe, na ethawabu yenyu yayibha ngosi. Mwaibha bhana abha yalimwanya afwanaje, umwahale yoyo mwinza hwabhantu bhasebhali nesombe.
Bhanji no lusajilo, neshe oYise hwenyu shali no lusajilo.
Mganje alonje, namwe semwayilongwa. Mgajerani, namwe semwayilaniwa. Sajilaji, namwe mwajisajilwa.
Bhapanji abhanje, namwe mwaipewa. Ekias eshe pyana - shashidinyiliwe, na tabhetabha na hwitishe hwitishe - mmafugamo genyu. Afwanaje eshi pimo sheshonti shamtumila, apimile shesho shayitumiha abhapimile amwe.”
Antele wabhabhola ofano. “Aje omntu yali shinsinzilu agalongozya ohwenje yali shinsinzilu? Nkashile bhabhombile esho, bas wonti bhaga dumbushila, mwilende?
Yasambelela sabha gosi ashile ya bhasambelezya, lelo shila mntu nkawasambelewa shinza abhaneshe osambelezi wakwe.
Yenu bas nkabhenye ahantu hahali mhati mwiliso elya holo waho, na ahantu hali mhati ya mwiliso lyaho sohwenya?
Obhahubhole hwele oholo waho, 'Holo, ehulabha enefwe ahantu hahali mhati yeliso lyaho,'nawe sohwenya aantu hahali mwiliso lyaho wewe? Olinafiki awe! Ahwande oyefwe ahantu mwiliso awe, ndipo nkobhalole shinza ahwefwe ahantu mwiliso elya holo waho.
Afwanaje nalimo ikwi ilinza lyalipa amadonda amabhibhi, antele nalimo ikwi ibhibhi lyalipapa amadondo aminza.
Afwanaje shila likwi limanyiha humadondo gakwe. Afwanaje abhantu sebhayabhila etini afume mumivwa, antele sebhayabhila ezabibu afume mmichongoma.
Omntu omwinza alishanga eshinza humwoyo gwakwe afumya gagaliminza, na omntu obhibhi alishanga eshibhibhi humwoyo gwakwe gafuma gagali mabhibhi. Afwanaje ilomu lyakwe liyanga gala gagamemile humwoyo gwakwe.
Yenu mnkwizya,'GOSI, GOSI', antele semgabhomba gala gegyanga?
Shilo mntu yahwenza hwiline na zyovwe enongwa zyane na bhombele embombo embabhalanje ejinsi shahweli.
Alengana no mntu yazenga enyumba yakwe, omwahale abana pansi, tee nazenje omsingi owenyumba pamwanya eyemwala imara. Amakoshi nagahenzele, na majenje agemenze gaikhomile enyumba, lelo segayizizye afwanaje yaze dwilwe shinza.
Lelo yayonti yahwovwa enongwa zyane sazitii; ofwano gwakwe yayola omntu yozenga enyumba pamwanya ma masanga pasepaliomsingi, amakoshi nagahishile humaha, enyumba ela yaseadilwe yonti.
Nawamala onongwa zyakwe zyonti mmakutu gabhantu ahinjiye, hupapernaumu.
Na obhambhambo wakwe oakida, omo ali bhinu tee alipapepe nefwa, wape alimntu yagene tee.
Nahovwezye enongwa ezye Yesu, asonte zyezye agosi abhayahudi, hwamwahale hulabhe aje aponie obhombambombo wakwe.
Bhope nabhafishile hwa Yesu, bhalabhile tee bhajile abhajiye, “Ono ombombele anongwa ezi,
Afanaje aligene itaifa lyetu, wape atizenjeye isinagogi.”
Basi oYesu abhalile pandwemo. Nabho nasagalihutali nenyumba, eyola oakida asontezyezye orafiki hwamwahale wabhola. 'GOSI, ogaje ahwiluvye afwanaje ane sefaa aje ewe oyinjile pansi pigalo lyane.
Eshi ehwilolile aje sefaa nene ahwinze hwaho, lelo panga izu tu obhombambo wane abhapone.
Afwanaje nane endi muntu nembehwelwe pansi eye ulongozi, endina sikari pansi yane, nkebholele ono bhala abhala na ono “enza” ahwenza, na obhomba mbombo, “Wane” bhomba eshi, abhomba.”
OYesu namwovwa ego aswijire, wagugalushila, obngano gwagwabhinjelelaga wanyaga.” Embabhola, hata bha Israeli, sendilolile olyweteho ogosi neshe olu.
Na bhala bhabhatumwilyu nabhahwela okhaya bhamwaga ola obhombambombo mwinza.
Napamande hashe, abhalile hwiboma limo lyakwiwaga Naini. Asambelezye wa bhakwe bhabhenjelezenye nalwo pandwemo no bongona ogosi.
Nawafiha apalamile nolwango ogwi boma eye, omntu yafyiye au anyetulwe, na mwana weka hwa nyina wakwe. Yali fwele, na mabungano wabhantu afume hwiboma bhali pandwemo nawo.
GOSI nawalola aloleye husajile wabhala, “Laha lile.”
Wasojela walipalamasya ijeneza bhala bhabanyetuye bhahemeleye, wayanga sahala ehubhala “imelela”
Ola ofwe wemelela. Wakhala wanda aje wapela onyina wakwe.
Owoga wabhakhata wonti. Bhasomba ONGOLOBHE bhayanga okuwa “OGOSI afumiye hwilite” na “ONGOLOBHE abhenyizye abhantu bhakwe”
Enogwa zyakwe ezi zyazyambanile huyudea hwonti na ensi zyonti zyazili mshe mshe.
Asambelezyewa abha Yohana bhaletela enogwa zyego gonti.
Esho oYohana wabhakwizya bhabhele asombeleziwa bhakwe wabhasondelezya hwa Yesu abhozye “Awe wewe ola yayenza, au timwenyelezyaje owenje?
Wape nabhafiha hwamwahale bhayanjile, “oYohana ya hwozya atisondezyezye hwiliwe aganjile aje awe, 'Wewe ola yahwenza au timwenyelezyaje owenje?”
Ne sala yeyo abhaponizye abhinji abhinu bhabho na efwa, eye mpepo embibhi, na avipofu abhinji bhalolile.
Eshi nkawagalula. Wabhabhola, bhalaji mubhale oYohana ega gamgalolilena govwe. avipofu bhalola alema bhajenda, abheukoma bhapona, adinda makutu bhahwovwa, bhabhafwiye bhazyoba, apena bhalombelelwa enongwa enyinza.
Wape heri omntu yeyonti yasavisiwa nane.”
Basi eshi asontelezewe bha Yohana na bhasogola, ahandile abhabhole amabongono enongwa ezya Yohana, “Mwafumile abhale mwipoli ahwenye yenu, isole wauyiziwa nehala?
Eshi mwafumile abhale ahwenye yenu, omntu yakwatiziwe amenda aminza? mmanye abhantu bhabhali namwenda ageu tukufu bhabhalya raha bhali mnyumba ezye shimwene.
Eshi mwafumile abhale ahwegegenu okuwa, Antele? Embabhole, na yali zaidi ya okuwa.
Oyo yayo asimbiliwa, “Ega, enya ehusontelezya ojumbe wane hwitagalila elye maso gaho, yabhalenganya idala lyaho hwitagalila lyaho,
Nane embabhola, neshi bhala bhapepwe na bhashe, nomo yaligosi neshe oYohana, lelo yalidodo humwene owa NGOLOBHE GOSI ashile omwene.”
Abhantu bhonti bhabhasonjezya esonga nabhahovwezye ego bhaheteshe, elyoli ya NGOLOBHE afwanaje bhoziwe. Huwoziwa uYohana.
Lelo abhafarisayo na bhana sheria bhali khene isunde elya NGOLOBHEhwabhene afwanaje sebhohoziwe nomwene.
OGOSI wayanga embalenganisye neye abhantu abheshikho eshi? bhape bhalengene neyenu?
Bhalengene nabhana bhakheye pasokoni, na kwizanye nabhayanga, 'tabhakhomeye efilimbi antele semwahanjile, tazondile antele semwalilile.'
Afwanaje oYohana owahozye ahenzele salya ibumnda wala samwela divai, namwa myanga myiga “Ano pepo obhibhi.
Omwana owa Adamu ayenzile alya na mwele, namwe myanga, enye, lyavi ono, na mwezi owe divai, rafiki wabho asonjezya!
Neshinshi ebhoneshe aje elinelyoli hwabhana bhakwe bhonti.”
Omntu omo owa mafarisayo amwanile alye eshalye hwamwene. Winjila mnyumba yakwe ofarisayo, wakhala pashalye.
Enya oshe omo owiboma lila wali wemabhibhi. Nazyoyile enongwa aje akheye pashalye panyumba eyola ofarisayo, aletile insupa marimari yeli nemaruhamu.
Wemelela hwisalo papepe na manama gakwe nawalila. Wanda hulagazizye mmagaga gakwe amansozi gakwe, na syomwole ni sisi elyamwitwe lyakwe, na humyante myante mmagaya gwakwe, na pashe gala amaruhamu.
Basi ola ofarisayo yamwanile nawolola shila wanyanga humwoyo gwakwe, omntu ono khashile alikuwe, “Handamenye oshe ono yahupalamasyasya, wenu wape aliwelewele yaje wemabhibhi.
OYesu wagamla wabhozya, “Simoni endine nongwa mbahubhole. “Wayanga” “sambilizi yanga!”
Wayanga “Omntu omo yakhopezya alinabhe madeni bhabhele, omo adagaya ehela miatano nowabhele amsini.
Bhape nabhali sebhalinahahuripe, abhasajiye wonti. bhabhele neshe bhabhele yo nanu yayihugana tee?
Simoni wagalula wayanga, “Amenyeje yayola yasajiye enyinji.” Wabhola oyamliye lyoli.”
Wagarushila ola oshe wabhola Simoni, “Walota oshe. Ono nahinjiye mnyumba yaho. Sohampiye amenze mmagagagane, eshi ono andayazyezye amansozi mmagagagane, na syomwole nisisi elya mwitwe lyakwe.
Awe sohanjayiye, lelo ono, awande pana hinjiye sagaleshile njayile tee mmagaga gane.
Sagapashile mwitwe lyane amafuta, eshi ono ampeshe amagaga gane amaruhamu.
Afwanaje nago, ehubhozya asajiye embibhi zyekwe zyazyalinjili, afwanaje asongwezye tee. Lelo yasajilya hasheoyo asongwelye hashe.”
Eshi abholele oshe, “Osajilye embibhi zyaho zyonti”
Esho bhala bhabhakheye pandwemo nawo bhahandile ayanje humoyo gabho wenu ono yasajilo embibhi?”
Wabhola ola oshe, “Olweteho lyaho lumwauye. Bhalaga hulweteho lwaho”
Yabha baada yego ali azyongola azyongola mmaboa namvijiji ali alombelela, na tungazye enongwa enyinza ezye umwene owa NGOLOBHE na bhala athenashara bhali pandwemo nawo,
Na abhashe bhamo bhamo bhali ne mpepo embibhi nepongo abhaponyizye bhape yo Mariamu yakwiziwa magdalena yazya fumile epepo saba.
Na Yohana oshe wa kuza owakili wakwe oHerode, Susana, na bhamwabho bhabhinji, bhabhatenganyaga huvintu vyao.
Ubungano ogosi na watangene, na bhala bhabha fumile shila liboma bhabhaliye ayanjile hufano.
“Ompanzi afumile abhale atote embeyu, yakwe wape nali atota, zimo zyalagashiye papepe nidara, zyakhanyilye enyonyi.
Zimo zyalageye pamwalo na zyahandile amele zyahomele afwanaje zyaha kosa orutubo.
Zimo zyalageye mmivwa na amivwa gahamela pandwemo zyazyo ya zisonga.
Zimo zyalageye pilongo elinza ayunga ego atatushe izu waganga yalinamakutu agahwovwa na ayovwaje.”
Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozya yenu ene omafano ogwo,
Wayanga, “Amwe apewewe azimanye esiri ezya mwene ONGOLOBHE, eshe bhamo humfwano, aje nkabhenye bhaganje alole nankabhovwe bhagale amanye.'
Na ogwo omfano. Emana yakwe ya yene embeyBhala lizu lya ngolobhe.
Bhala bhabhali papepe ni dala bhabhala bhahovwa, antele ahwenza oshetani alyefwa elyo izu mmoyo yaho, bhasibhe bhalyeteha na hwaulwe.
Na bhala abhapamwala bhabhala ambao nkabhovwa bhaliposhela lila izu sabhashiye, wape sebhana malandazi bhahweteha humda hashe, naufiha owa lengwe, bhahwibagula.
Zyazilagaliye pamivwa bhabhala bhabhovwenzwe, abhale hwabho bhosohwa ne shughuli no utabhazi na owalangani owemaisha ega, sebhatonia lyalyonti.
Na zila ezya pilongo elinza bhabala bhabhali no mwoyo ogwinza ogwa lyovwe izu, na likhate, esho lipapa amadondo esha jimbilizwe.
Nomo, omntu yahwasya, okhozyo na kwishile neshelelo. Au abheshe hwinzongo bali bhayibheha pamwanya pameza ili bhabhahwisya njila bhapataje alole okhizyo lwakwe.
Afwanaje nalimo izu lyalyobhele lyasagalya yibhoneha, antele lyalyobhele elyaje selyayi manyiha na fumile hwelele.
Hwiyenyi basi enamna shamhovwa afwanaje yalinahantu. Abhapewe na ola, yasanahantu abhafyolwe atahala, habhoneha aje anaho.”
Bhabhalila onyina wakwe na holo bhakwe bhashindwa abhapapepe afanaje amabungano.
Bhatwalile enongwa wabhola, “Onyina waho na holo bhaho bhemeleye hwonze bhahwanza alolane nawe.
Wagalula, wayanga “omaye wane naholo bhane bhabhebha bhabhahovwa izu elya NGOLOBHE na bhombe.”
Yabha ensiku zila wapanda mshelelo omwahale na sambelezyewa bhakwe, wabhabhola, “Nantele tilo woshe hadi hwisyela eyeidimi. “Bhasogola na matanga.
Bhape nabhali bhabhala, agonile otulo, yahishile etofani pamwanya eyidimi, eshelelo shahandile ameme ameze bhabha mhatari.
Bhabhalila bhadamuzya bhaga, “GOSI wa gosi! GOSI wa gosi! litega wabhoha!” Waidamila ehala na vwadangana ameze hwaleha hwabha hwinza.
Wabhabhola, “Olweteho lyenyu lulihwi?” Bhogope, bhaswiga, bhayango bhebho hwa bhebho,”Yenu ene paka, adamila ehalana menze gape gahumwogopa?”
Bhafiha mpwani mnsi ya bha wa Gerasini ye paramila hu Galilaya.
Wape na hishile hupwani, atangene nomntu omo owe boma, ola yaline mpepo, sagakwete amenda ensiku zinyinji, antele sagakheye pakhaya ila hamagwela.
Nalolile oYesu akholile eholo, agwiye hwitagalila lyakwe. Waganga hwizu igosi endi neyenu nawe, Yesu womwana wa NGOLOBHE yalimwanya? Ehulabha, ugajendavye”
Afanaje alidamiye lile ipepo ichafu limwepe omntu ola, afanaje apagewe wape mara nyinji, nantele bhalidaga mshifungo na apinyilye na manyolo ne mpengo, adumlaga gala amanyolo, ashembezyewaga mwipoli ne nguvu ezya lila ipepo.
OYesu wabhozya, “Itawa lyaho wewenu?” Wayanga, “Itawa lyane endijeshi” Afwanaje pepo bhinji bhamwinjiye.
Bhalabha asabhadamila aje bhafume abhale mwilende.
Eshi epo pali ikundi elye engorobhe enyinji bhadimazyaga mwigamba. Galabha agapele oruhusa ahwinjile zila, wagapele aruhusa.
Pepo bhafuma mwamntu ola bhinjila mgorobhe, lyape ikundi lyahishile mwigenge nanali, bhinjila mwidimi, bhafwa mmenze.
Adimi nabhalola lyalifumiye bhashembeye na zyambanye enongwa hwiboma, na mavueni.
Abhantu afumile abhale ahwenye gaga fumiye, bhabhalila oYesu bhalola omntu ola mwagafumile akwete amenda anenjele zyakwe, bhahogope.
Na bhala bhabhalolile bhabhabholele shasha hali shaponiziwe ola ya pageweni pepo.
Na mwabho abhantu abhensi ya bhagevasi yeli pasheje sheje bhalabhile aje asogole hwabhahale afwanaje bhali nowoga ogosi esho winjila mshelelo wawela.
No mntu ola yalya fumile ipepo alabhile oruhusa aje alondozyaje wape, lelo omwahale walaga wayanga,
“Wela amwenyu arombelele gagali mago ONGOLOBHE gabhombeye”Abhala, alombelele iboma lyonti, shangali magosi amambo ga bhombelwe no Yesu.
Eshi oYesu namwawela, obongano gwa karibizizye, esha seshelele afwanaje bhali bhahugolela wonti.
Enya omntu omo wenza itawa lya vwa yo yairo, wape mntu gosi owe shibhanza, wagwa pamagaga ga Yesu walabha iyinjile mnyumba yakwe,
Afwanaje elendu wakwe abhinile tee apalamila afwe, afwanaje mwana weka mwene, oumri wakwe alinamaha kumi na gabhele, wakati abhala obungano gwasonjile.
Noshe omo ambaye afumaga idanda omda ogwe maha kumi na gabhele, ali anankenye eshoma shakwe shonti abhapele aganga bila opone, nomntu yoyonti,
Abhalile hwisalo lyakwe wapalamazya opindo ohwemwenda gwakwe, mara elyo afume hwkwe idanda hwapoma.
OYesu wayanga, “Wenu ya mpalamasyezye?” Basi abhantu bhonti nabhakhana oPetro abholele, GOSI mgosi, amabonyano ega gahuzyongala na husonje.”
OYesu wayanga, “Omntu ampalamasyezye, afwanaje elola aje amaha gafumile.”
Ola oshe nawalola yaje sawezizye ahwobhe wenza ayinga, wagwa hwilagalila lyakwe, wabhola hwitagalila elya bhantu bhonti esababu eyahupalamasye nasha ponile nantele.
Wabhola, “Rendu, olyeteho lwaho luponizye. Bhalaga umwe no lweteho.”
Nali ayangaga ego ahenzele, omntu afume hukhaya eya ola ogosi, owe shibhanza, “Wabhola orendu waho afwiye. Ogajehuyanzyosambelezi.”
Lelo oYesu nawovwa, ego, wagalula ugajebhe, “Nowoga. Ateha awe wape, abhapone.”
Nawafiha mnyumba, sagaleshile omntu aje ayinjile hata omo, ila oPetro, no Yohana no Yakobo, no Yise wole, omwana no nyina.
Na bhantu bhonti bhali bhalilaga na zonde, wayanga, “Majelile safwiye, ono, eshi aganile tulo wene.”
Bhaseshile tee, afanaje bhamenye aje afwiye.
Wakhata, okhono, wakhola hwizu, wayanga, “sahala, bhoha”
URoho yakwe yawela, wape mara eyo wemelela. Wabhabhola wapele eshalye.
AYise bhakwe bhaswijile, tee lelo wabhakhana bhagaje hubhole omntu lyelifumiye.
Wabhakwizya bhala Thenashara, wabhapela owezo na mamlaka agahwefwe pepo bhonti na ponie empongo.
Wabhasontezya bhaulombelele oumwene owa NGOLOBHE na abhaponie empongo.
Wabhabhola, “Mganje hweje ahantu msafari yenyu endesa, wala echola, wala ibumnda, wala ehela wala omo wenye asahabhe na magolole gabhele.
Na enyumba yuyonti yamwayinjila, mkhalaje omwo anzaji omwo.
Na bhala bhasebhabhakalibizizye, na mfuma mwiboma omwo, kunyuntaji hata mankondi aga mmagaga egenyu abhe ushuda hwabhahale.”
Bhabhala bhasyongola shila shijiji, bhalombelela izu na abhunie abhantu shila mahali.
Nao Herode, omwene, wovwa enongwa zyonti zyazibhombeshe, wazugumila afwanaje abhantu bhamo bhayanjile eyejo oYohana azyoshele afume afwe,
Na bhamo bhagaga oEliya abhoneshe na bhamo, bhagaga bhabhala akuwa abhe mwaha azeyoshele.
Lelo oHerode wayanga, “OYohana, nadumuye itwe eshi wenu ono wehovwa amambo gakwe? Ahanzaga hulole.
Eshi bhala atumwa, nabhawelile bhabholele amambo gonti gabhabombile. wabhega wabhalanabho pa faragha paka piboma limo likwiziwa Bethsadia.
Namabongono nabhanya bhalondoleye wabhakari bizya, wabha ayanga nabho enongwa zya umwene owa NGOLOBHE, wabhaponia bhala bhabhali neshida eya pone.
Na isanyo lyahandile aswe, bhabhalila bhala Athenashara, bhabhola ulaje obongano ili bhabhale hushijiji na mmagondo aga mnshenje bhapaje apagone na evyalye afwanaje epa patihweli pigona wene.”
Wabhabhola, “Bhapeli amwe eshalye.”bhayaga” Seti na hantu zaidi eye mabumnda gasanu ne sanaki zibhele kasetibhala tibhakalile abhantu ebhabhonti evyalye.”

Bhabhamba esho bhabhakhazya bhonti.
Wega gala amabumnda gasanu na zila esamaki zibhele wenya amwanya humbunguni, wavi sayila, wavimensula wabhapela, asambelezewe bhakwe ili bhabhapele abungano.
Bhalya bhakuta bhonti, na eshi vila evimensushilo vyavyasageye bhabhongenye evitondo kumi na vibhele.
Yabha na putaga hufalagha, amanyiwa bhakwe bhahari pandwemo nawo, wabhabhozya, eshi amabongano ebhabha bhayiga ane neweni?
Bhagalula, bhayanga, “oYohana yahwozya, lelo bhamo bhayiga yo Eliya, nabhamwabho bhayiga mojawapo mwa kuwa abhemwaha azyoshele.”

Wabhasunda, wabhakhana bhagaje hubhole omntu enongwa ezyo,
Wayanga ahwanziwa omwana owa Adamu agaje amalabha aminji nakhanwe na zee na gosi abhe makohani na simbi na gakwe na isiku elya tatu lya zyoshe.
Wabhabhola wonti omntu yeyonti, “Yahwanza ambejezye na ahwikhane yoyo, ahwitweshe ikhobhehanyo lyakwe shila lisiku, andondolezyaje.
Afwanaje omntu yahwanza aponie enafsi yakwe ayiyitezya, na omntu yayitezye enafsi kwajili yane, esho ayiyiponya.
Afwanaje henu habhajiye omntu, azyagaezya mnsi omo zyonti, nkeshe wahwitezya yoyo na hwiyanganuzye?
Afwanaje shila yayindolela asoni ane na mazu gane, omwana owa Adamu wape ayihulole esoni omntu oyo nayenza no winza wakwe, no wayise no wa malaika abhinza.
Nane embabhola elyoli, bhahweli bhabhemeleye epa, ambao sebhayilenga efwa tee hata paka bhaulole oumwe owa NGOLOBHE.”
Afume amazu ego zyashilile ensiku nane abhejile oPetro, no Yohana, no Yakobo, wazubha mwigamba ili alabhe.
Yabha katika apute hwakwe esheni, esha hu maso gakwe shagaluhana, na amenda gakwe gabha mazelu gameta meta.
Na enya, abhantu bhabhele bhali bhayanga nawo! Bhape yo Musa no Eliya,
Bhabhoneshe huwinza. Bhayanga enongwa ezya fwe hwakwe, nayikamilisya hu Yerusalemu.
OPetro na bhala bhali pandwemo nabho bhali bhalemewe notulo. Lelo nabhadamla, bhalole owinza wakwe nabhala bhabhele bhabhemeleye pandwemo nabho.
Yabha ebho nabhahwibagula nawo, oPetro wabhila oYesu, GOSI, wabhagosi, shinza atee abhepa na tilenganye amahenje gatatu. Shimo shahwiliwa shimo shamusi esha mwabho sha Musa, no Eliya.” Esho ali samenye lyayanga.
Nali ayanga ego, lyafumiye ibhengo lyabhapola izunda bhogopa nabhinji mwibhengo elyo.
Izu lyafumile mwibhengo lyayanga, “Ono mwana wane teule. Wane mwovwaji omwahale.”
Na izu elyo nalyamaliha, Yesu abhoneshe ali mwene, bhape bhapona kati, sebhatangazya hwa mntu ensiku zila lyalyoli lilo gabhagalolile.
Yabha isiku, elya bhele yakwe nabhiha hwigamba, abugano ogosi watangene nawo.
Na enye, omntu omo katika obongano akholile hwiizu ayanjile, sambilizi, “Ehulabha mwenye omwana wane, afwanaje omwahale mwana wane mwene.
Na enye ipepo lihukhata wape akhoma ibwago, antele lihupela eshifapa, olu afuma itatafura wa sahuleha ila humalabha ohwikoyola koyola.
Embalabhile asambelezewe bhaho bhamwefe sebhawezizye.”
OYesu wagalula wayanga, “Amwe mshikholo mwase mlinolyeteho, mtejile embakhale nani we nahwejeshelane paka ndii? Rete omwana wa ho epe.”
Na ali ahubhalila, ipepo lyalagazya pansi. wapela eshifafa, oYesu wadamila ipepo ibhibhi, waponia omwana wawezyezya oYise.
Bhonti bhaswiga nabhaulola ogosi owa NGOLOBHE. Bhape nabhali bhaswiga amambo gonti gabhambile, abhabholele amanyiziwa bhakwe,
“ Gakhataji amazu ega mmakutu genyu, ufwanaje omwana owa Adamu abhala akhatwe mmakhono gabhantu.”
Lelo sebhalimenye izu lila, lyatisilwe hwabhale sebhalimenye, bhahogope hubhozye ofwano gwakwe gwenu izu elyo.
Bhahandile ayungane wenu yabhabhe gosi kati yabho.
Wape oYesu nawamanya esebho ezye moyo gabho, wamwega omwana ododo, wabhaha papepe no mwahale,

Apwanaje omwana owa Adamu sega henzele azitezye roho zya bhantu eshi azyaule, bhasogala bhabhala hushijiji esha mwabho.

Eshi baada eyego, GOSI abheshera na bhamwabho sabini wabhasontezya, bhabhele bhabhele bhatagalile bhale shila boma shila hwintu hwapambameye abhale yoyo.

Bhalaji. Enyaji, embasotezya nesheje bhana ngole mmahanyanga.
Mgaje ahweje ifuko wala echola, wala evilato, wala mgaje hulamushe omntu mwidala.
Ekhaya yoyonti yambahahwinjele, yanji na soti, 'Amani ebhanje mnyumba omu.
Nkashile ahweli omwana owe amani, eamani yenyu ebhawele hwilimwe.
Eshi khalaji pakhaya peepo, mlyonje na mwene evyabhahale, afanaje, obhombo mbombo ahwanziwa hupele omshahara gwakwe. Mgaje asame same afume ekhaya ene abhale ekhaya eyamwabho.
