Hula hu Yelusalemu hwali ni birika pandyango gwe ngole, lyalyalihwetwa hu lugha yeShiabrania hu Bethzatha, lyape lili na matao gasanu.
Abhantu bhinji abhinu bhahali, ampofu, avewete, bhabhahomele bhali bhagonile mumatao ego. {Khatililaga: Amazu ge sitali 3 segabhoneha mu nakala enyinza zi mwaha. “Bhagolezezye amenze avwalanganye.”') Hwa hali owakati umo ohalozelu muhati ya Gosi na vwalanganye menze.
Ola wa hali wa kwanza ahwinjile muhati amenze nagavwalanganywa oyo abhanga mwomi afumilane na hahonti hahali ha khetwe omuda ogwo.
No muntu wali abhinile humaha thelathini na nane wli mhati ye matao.
O Yesu nalolile agonile mhati ye matao nawamanya aje agonile pala omuda gwinji oYesu abhozya, “Ajile ohwanza abhe mwomi?”
Ola abhinu ajile, “Gosi sendi no muntu wambeshe mwi birika omuda amenze nagavwalanganywa. Lwelenga ahwinjile omuntu owenje antangulila.”
O Yesu wabhozya, “Bhoha ayeje igodolo lya ho obhalaje.”
Omuntu ola wapona, wega eshitala shakwe na wabhala. Isiku elyo lyali lisiku lye Sabato.
Ayahudi bhabhozya omuntu ola waponyiziwe, “Sanyono lisiku lya Sabato, solohusiwa abebe igodoro lyaho.”
Omwene ajile waponiziwe yayoyo wambozezye, “Ege igodoro lyaho bhalaga.”
Bhabhozezye, “Wenu wabhozyezye 'Ege igodoro lyaho bhalaga?'”
Haha nkashe ola waponile sagamenye, afwatanaje oYesu ali asogoye shi siri. Afuatanaje hwali awantu winji esehemu eyo.
Pamande yakwe oYesu amweje ola umuntu mshibhanza na hubhozye, “Enya, aponole! “Uganje abhombe mbibhi nantele ogakhomana ni jambo ibhibhi sana.”
Omuntu ola abhalile abhabhozye Ayahudi aje oYesu wamponezye.
Eshi, afuatanaje amambo ego Ayahudi bhayemvezye oYesu, afuatanaje abhombile amambo ega isiku lye Sabato.
O Yesu wabhabhozya, “Odaada wane abhomba embombo paka esalezi nane ebhomba embombo.”
Hunamuna eye Ayahudi bhahendeleye azidi bhahanzaga aje sababu yanankanye eSabato, ila hukwizye Ongolobhe oDaada wakwe, alihweshele sawa no Ngolobhe.
O Yesu ajile, “Etesheli, etesheli, Omwana sagabhomba ahantu hahonti ila hala halolile Oise wakwe abhomba, afuatanaje hahonti habhomba Oise haheho hanzabhombe Omwana.
Afuatanaje oDaada agene Omwana, na ahulanga kila hantu habhomba na ahaulanga amambo amagosi ashile ega ili nkamuswigage.”
Afuatanaje nanshi shila oDaada nafufula awafwe na abhapele owomi, sheshesho Omwana wope ahupele wowonti wagene.
Afuatane naje oDaada sahulonga wowonti, ila apiye Omwana alonje hwonti
ili bhonti bhamwogope Omwana sebhahu mwogopa oDaada. Umwene wasihumwogopa Omwana sahamwogope no Daada wantumile.
Eteshela, eteshela, omwene wahonvwa izu lyane na humweteshele wantumile ali no womi we wilawila na sagailongwa. Yaani ashilile afume hunfwa ahwinjile huwomi.
Eteshela, eteshela, embabhozya ensiku zihwenza na zihweli lula abhafwe nabhayovnwa izu lyakwe Omwana wa Ngolobhe, na bhonti bhabhayonvwa waikhala.
Nanshi shila oDaada shali nowomi mhati yakwe yoyo,
shesho apiye Omwana abhe no womi wope oDaada apiye Omwana amamlaka ili aje alongaje afuatanaje Mwana wa Adamu.
Munganje shangale hweli afuatanaje zihwenza ensiku abhafwe hbonti bhabhali mumakaburi bhayonvwa izu lyakwe
na bhope bhaifuma hunze: hwabhabhombaga enyinza ulyovyosyolwe womi, bhabhabhombaga embibhi oluvyosnsyo lwa longwe.
Sengabhomba ahantu hahonti afume huline nene. Nanshi shehovwa, shesho shelola alonje na alonje hwane hwe lyoli afuatanaje sehwanza she songwa ane, ila shasongwa omwane wantumile.
Nkashe ehwihakikisya nene, luhakikisyo lwane selwabhanga lwe lyoli.
Ahweli wamwabho wahakikisya ahusuane emanya aje lyoli uluhakikisho lwa hakikisizya ane we lyoli.
Mutumile hwa Yohana wope ahakikisizye lyoli.
Hata sheshi ulihakikisyo lwenduposhela selufuma hwa bhantu. Ninayasema haya ili kwamba mweze kuokolewa.
O Yohana ali lukhozyo lwalwa hahaga, na khozye mwahali tayari aisongwe huu muda ododo olukhozyo lwakwe.
Ulwetesho lwendi nalwo gosi ashile lula lwa Yohana, humbombo zila Odaada yza mpiye azikamilisye, anzyo embombo zyezibhomba zibhonesya aje Odaada antumile.
Odaada wantumile yoyo ahakikisizye ahusu ane. Semuwaile ahomvwe izu lyakwe au alole obele gwakwe omuda gwagwonti.
Semulinalyo izu lyakwe nkalikhale muhati afuatanaje semwamwetesheye omwene wantumile.
Mugenyelezya amazu msewa aje muhati yakwe muli owomi wewila wila, gego amazu gahakikisya ehabari zyane
semuhwanza ahwenez huline nkampate owomi wewilawila.
Siposhela huhwhiyonvwe afume hwa wantu,
ehwelewa aje nalumo olugano lwa Ngolobhe muhati yenyu.
Enenzele hwitawa lya Daada wane, semwamposheye. Nkashe owenje ayenze hwitawa lyakwe handamwaposheye.
Aje mwahenzaga ahweteshele amwe mwamposhela esifa afume hwa kila muntu wenyu ila semuhwanza esifa yefuma hwa Ngolobhe mwene?
Msagaje ane embabhatake hwitazi lya Daada. Wabhataka amwe yo Musa, ambayo mubheshele ategemele hwa mwa hale.
Mugali aje mhumweteshele oMusa, handamunetesheye nane afuatanaje ahaandishe ahusu ane.
Nkase muhwetehsele bhole amazu gane?
Baada ye enongwa ezi, oYesu abahlile hu Bahari ye Galilaya nantele huhweta isombe lye Tiberia.
Obhongano ogosi gwali guhufuata afuatanaje bhalolile ealama zyabhombile hwa bhala bhabhali bhawinu.
O Yesu azubhile pamwanya hadi sehemu ya pamwanya hwigamba na akhaye ohwo na bhanafunzi bhakwe
(Epasaka, ye shikulukulu sha Yahudi yali efishile).
O Yesu abhosezye amaso amwanya nalole owinji wa bhantu bhahwenza hwamwene, wabhozya oFilipo, “Tibhala hwii akale amabumunda aje ebhankabhapate alye”?
(Ila oYesu agayanjile ega hwa Filipo apimaga pima afuatanaje omwene yoyo amenye haibhomba).
O Filipo ajile, “Ata mabumunda hela hata dinari mia mbili seganzatosye shila muntu apate hashe hashe.”
O Andrea, omo webhanafunzi bhakwe ohoho wakwe oSimoni Petro abhozyezye
O Yesu, “Ahweli osahala epa ali na mabumunda gasanu ne samaki zi bhele, eshi ene ekhondeye yenu hwa bhantu abhinji enamuna ene?”
O Yesu abhozya, “Aje bhakhazyi abhantu pansi” (kulikuwa na nyasi nyingi mahali pale). Hivyo wanaume wapata elfu tano wakakaa chini.
Pamande oYesu wega amabumunda gasanu wasombwezye wabhagabhila bhala bhabhakheye. Shesho wabhagabhila esamaki alengane shabha hanzaga.
Abhantu nabhahakuta, abhabhozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Bhonganyi evigalizi vyavisageye aje nkaviganje ateje vyovyonti.”
Bhabhonganya na memwe evitondo kumi ne vibhele, evipande vye mabumunda visanu vyavyasageye na bhala bhabhalyanga.
Pamande abhantu na bhalola embombo zya bhombile bhajile, “Lyoli ono yayola okuwaa wahwenza munsi.”
O Yesu nagunduye aje bhahwanza ahukhate ili aje bhabheshe aje mwene wabho, ahwitenjile, nantele abhalile hwigamba omwene mwene.
Nahwali lyabhela, abhanafunzi bhakwe bhalushile abhale hwidimi idodo.
Bhapandile mwitoli bhali bhalobhoha abhale hu Kaperanaumu. (Enkisi yali eyenyiye no Yesu ali sele sayenzele hwabhene).
Eshipindi esho ehala engosi yali evugula, ne nsombe yali ehwendelela achafushe.
Nantele abhanafunzi bhakwe na bhali wakhomile emakasia kama shilini natano au thelathini wahalola oYesu ajenda pamwanya ye somba azuwilile itoli, wahogopa.
Ila wabhabhozya, “Nene mganjehwogope.”
Antele bhalitayali ahunyemle mwitoli, itoli nalyafihoa insi ya bhalaga.
Isiku lyalyafuatile, obhongano gwa hemeleye oupande wensombe bhalolaga aje nalimo itoli lya mwabho ila lila ambalyo oYesu na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhali sebhalipandile ila abhanafunzi bhakwe bhali bhahwibhaliyee bhebho.
(Japokuwa hwa hali amitoli gamo gafumaga hu Tiberia peepe ne sehemu hwabha lyanga amabumunda baada ya Gosi afumwe ulusalifyo).
Omuda embongano na bhamanya aje se yo Yesu wala sebhanafunzi bhakwe bhali hula, abhene bhebho wapende mwitoli bhabhala hu Kaperanaumu bhalondola oYesu.
Na bhahapata esehemu ya mwabho ye oimi dodo bhabhozya, “Mwalimwa ohenzele ndii ohu?”
O Yesu ayanga, abhabhozya, Etisheli, etisheli, munaanza ane, sio aje mwazilolile embombo ila afuatanaje mwaliye amabumunda nakute.
Leshi ashibhombela embombo eshalye shashi na nchiha, ila mshibhombele embombo eshalye shashikhala wilawila shila omwana wa Adamu shaibhapela, afuatanaje Ongolobhe Odaada abheshele omuhuri pamwanya yakwe.”
Pamande bhabhozya, “Hantu hahwanziwa abhombe aje abhombe embombo ya Ngolobhe?”
O Yesu ajibu, “Ene ye mbombo ya Ngolobhe: aje mwenteshe omwene wa ntumile.”
Bhabhozya, “Aje alama anshi zyobhabhombe, aje tibhazilole na humweteshele? Obhabhombe bhole?
Adaada bhetu bhaliye emanna mwipoli, nanshi sheyaandihwe, “Abhapiye amabumunda afume amwanya nkabhalye.”
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Etisheli, etisheli, sio yo Musa abhapiye amabumunda afume amwanya, bali Baba yangu ndiye awapaye mkate wa kweli kutoka mbinguni.
Afuatanaje ibumunda lya Ngolobhe lyalila lyalihwiha afume amwanya naipele ensi owomi.
Eshi bhabhozya, “Bhaga Gosi tipelaje amabumunda wilawila.”
O Yesu ahaga, “Ane endi libumunda lye womi, omwene wa hwenza huline sagailola enzala omwene wane teshela sagaichisila enzara omwene waneteshela sagaichisila na mwaha eshomelwa.”
Ijapokuwa embabhozezye aje, mundolile, lakini semuhweteshela.
Bhonti oDaada wampiye bhanzahwenze huline, na wawonti wahwenza huline senaihutaga honze kabisa.
Afwatanaje enishile afume amwanya, sehwahubhombe olusongwo lwane, ila ulusongwo lwa wantumile.
No olu lwo lusongwo lwakwe wantumile, aje nsatezye hata muntu omo bhala bhombiye, ila ehaibhazyosya isiku lya mwisho.
Afuatanaje ega gasongwa Odaada wane, aje wawonti wa humwenya Omwana na humweteshele apate owomi wewila wila; wenu wanaihuzyonsya isiku elya mwisho.
Pamande ayahudi walalamishila ahusu omwene afuatanaje ayanjile, “Ane endi libumunda lyalihwiha afume amwanya.”
Bhayanga, “Ono seyo Yesu omwana wa Yusufu, odaada wakwe no nyina wakwe timenye? Shili bhole esalezi aiga, 'Enishile afume humwanya`?”
O Yesu ahayanga, ajile, “Muganje alalamishalane mhati yenyu mwemwe.
Nomo omuntu wahwenza huline nkashe savutilwe no Daada wane wantumile, nane naihuvyonsya isiku elya mwisho.
Afuatanaje eyandihwe hwa kuwaa, 'Bhanzasambelezewe no Ngolobhe.' Shila wayomvwezya asambeleye afume hwa Daada, ahwenza huline.
Sio aje ahweli omuntu walolile Odaada, ila omwene wafuma hwa Ngolobhe- alolile Odaada.
Eteha, eteha omwene wanetesheye ali no womi wewilawila.
Ane endi libumunda lye womi.
adaada bhetu bhaliye emanna mwipoli, bhahafwa.
Eli ndiyo libumunda lyalihwiha afume amwanya, ili omuntu alye nkaganje afwe.
Ane endi libumunda lyalikhala lyalilishile afume amwanya. Nanshi omuntu wawonti nkalye ibumunda eli, aihwizya wilawila. Ibumunda lye mbefumye bele gwane alengane no womi ensi.”
Ayahudi bhavitwa bhebho hu bhebho bhanda abisanye bhaiga, “Omuntu ono awezizye bhole atipele obele gwakwe tiilye?”
Nantele oYesu wabhbhozya, “Etesheli, etesheli, nkashe semwailya obele gwa Mwana wa Adamu na mwele idanda lyakwe, semwaibha nowomi muhati yenyu.
Wawonti wailya obele gwane na mwele idanda lyane ali no womi wewilawila, nane naihuvyonsya isiku lya mwisho.
Afwatanaje obele gwane shalye she lyoli, ni danda lyane shimwelo she lyoli.
Omwe wagulya obele gwane na mwele idanda lyane akhala muhati yane, nane mhati yakwe.
Nanshi Odaada we womi shantumile, nanshi shakheye alengane no Daada, wakwe no mwene aikhala alengangane.
Eli libumunda lyali hwihaafume amwanya, sio nanshi shila Adaada wenyu bhaliye bhafwa. Omwene wanzalye ibumunda eli ayikhala wilawila.
O Yesu ayanjile enongwa ezi mshibhanza nahali afundizya hu Kaperanaumu.
Abhinji abhanafunzi bhakwe bhahomvweze ega, bhayanjile, “Eli lifundizyo likhone wenu wawezizye aliposhele?”
O Yesu afuatanaje amenye aje abhanafunzi bhakwe bhalalamiha iswali eli libhavisya, akawambia je jambo hili linawakwaza?
Eshi shaibha na waihulola omwana wa Adamu naihwiha afume hwahweli kabisa?
Yo Mpempo yayoyo wafumya owomi. Obele saguhwavwa nkahamo. Amazu ge njanjile hulimwe ga mpempo no womi.
Bhahweli abhantu hulimwe bhasebhahweteshela.” afuatanaje oYesu amenye fume hale ola wasaga hweteshela na ola omwene wanzahusyonshele.
Wabhabhozya, aje shasheshi nabhabhozezye aje nomo omuntu wayenza huline ila apewilwe no Daada.”
Baada yega abhanafunzi bhakwe wonti wawela akhosi na khatane nawo nantele.
O Yesu wabhabhozya bhala kumi na bhabhele, “Aje namwe muhwanza asogole?”
O Simoni oPetulo wayanga, “Gosi tibhale hwa nanu afatanaje awe oli ni izu lya womi wewilawila,
natetesheye na manye aje awe oligolosu wa Ngolobhe.”
O Yesu wayanga, “Aje ane senabhachaguye amwe, na omo wenyu yo setano?
Eshi aliayanga ahusu oYuda, omwana wa Simoni Iskariote, afwatanaje ali yoyoyo ali pamo na bhala kumi na bhabhele, ambaye wasyonsheye oYesu.
Pamande ye mambo ega oYesu asafiliye eshi hu Galilaya, afuatanaje sagaasongwelwe abhala huu Yahudi afwatanaje huuyahudi wapangaga ahubude.
Eshi eshikulukulu sha Yahudi, eshi kulukulu ye Vibanda, ya pepee.
Aholo wakwe nkabhozya, “Sogala apantu epa obhale hu Yahudi, abhanafunzi bhaho bhagalole amambo gobhomba.
Nomo wabhomba lyolyonti hu shi siri nkashe omwene yoyo ahwanza ajulihane pazelu. Nkashe obhomba ega, hwilanje wewe hwabha munsi.”
Hata bhaholo bhakwe sebhamwetesheye.
O Yesu nkabhabhozya, “Insiku zyane sezifishile bado, ila ensiku zyenyu kila muda zihweli.
Abhamunsi sebhawezizye abhavitwe amwe, ila bhamvitwa ane afuatane embahakikisya aje ambombo zyao mbibhi.
Zubhaji abhale hu shikulukulu; ane sembala hu shikulukulu afuatanaje omuda gwane guli seele afishe.”
Nayanga enongwa izyo hwa bhahala, asageye hu Galilaya.
Hata sheshi, aholo bhakwe na bhabhalile hushikulukulu wope nkahabhala, sio apazelu bali pasirisiri.
Ayahudi bhali bhahufuata hushikulukulu naje, “Ali hwii?”
Hwali no luyangano lwinji muhati mlubhongano ahusu omwene. Wamo bhajile, “Muntu mwinza.” Bhamwabho wajile, “Ndadi abhatezya olubhongano.”
Hata sheshi nomo wayanjile pazelu ahusu omwahale afuatanaje bhabhogope Ayahudi.
Ensiku zye shikulukulu nazyahali katikati, oYesu azubhile abhale mshibhanza na hwande asambelezye.
Ayahudi bhaswigaga na nayanje, “Huu namna wele omuntu amanye enongwa enyinji? Sasambeleye nkahashe.”
O Yesu ayanga naje, “Emanyizyo zyane se zyaline, ila zyoola wantumile.
Nkashe wawonti anzasongwe abhombe olusongwo lwakwe omwene, anzamanye emanyizyo ezi, aje zifuma hwa Ngolobhe, au aje eyanga afume huline nene.
Shila wayanga gagafuma hwa mwene yoyo ahwenza umwamu wakwe, na shila wahwanza oumwamu wakwe omwene wantumile, omuntu omuntu oyo we lyoli, na muhati yakwe nahumo abhombeshe zye malenka.
O Musa sagabhapiye amwe endajizyo? Ila nomo hata weka hulimwe wabhomba endajizyo. Yenyu muhwanza ambude?
Amabhongano gayanga, “Aje oli na mapepo. Wenu wahanza ahubude?”
O Yesu wayanga wagaa, “Ombombile embombo yeeka, namwe mwenti muswijile afuatanajenesho.
O Musa abhapiye etohara (sio aje efuma hwa Musa, ila efuma hwa daada), na hu Sabato mhutahiri omuntu.
Nkashe omuntu anzaposhele etohara hwi siku lye Sabato aje endajizyo zya Musa zinganje nankanywe, yeenu munvitwa ane afwatanaje ebheshele omuntu abhe mwinza kabisa hu Sabato?
Mganje alonje alengane sha mlola, ila alonje hulyoli.
Bhamo bhamo uYelusalemu bhaga, “Seyayono wabhahu mwanza ahude?
Enya, oyanga pazelu, na sebhayanga hahonti alengane no mwene. Sawezizye aje egabha aje alongozi bhamenye elyoli aje ono yo Kilisiti, ewezizye abhe?
Timenye aje omuntu ono afumila hwii. O Kilisti lwayenza, atasheshii, nomo wailola aje afuma hwii.”
O Yesu afumiaga izu lyakwe mwibhanza, asambele zyaga naje, “Amwe mwenti mumenye ane na mumeenye hwe fuma. Senamenye hubele gwane, ila omwene wantumile welyoli, semumenye omwene.
Emenye omwene afuatanaje enfumile hwa mwene na antumile.”
Bhalenga ahaate, ila nomo ata omo wabhosezye okhono gwakwe ahusu omwene afuatanaje esaa yakwe yaali seele afishe.
Hata sheshi bhinji mubhongano bhamwetesheye. Bhajile, “Kilisiti lwa yeenza, aibhomba embombo nyinji ashile zyabhombile omuntu ono?”
Amafarisayo bhabhonvwezye amawongano wakwepelena enongwa ezi eshi oYesu, na agosi bha dimi na Mafarisayo bhatumile amaafisa aje ahukhate.
O Yesu nkayanga, “Ali seele insiku ndodo embabhe pandwemo namwe, napamande naibhala hwa mwene wantumile.
Munanza ila semubhandole; hula hwembala, semubhawezye ahwenze.”
Abhayaudi bhayangama bhene hu bhene, “Omuntu ono anzabhale hwii aje tipotwe ahulole? Anzabhale hwa bhabhanyampene mhati ya yunanu bhamanyinzye Ayunani?
Nongwa bhole ene yayanjile, 'Mwainanza nantele semwainaga; hula hwembala semwaiwezya ahwenze'?”
Esalezi hunsiku zya mwisho, isiku igosi lye shikulukulu, pYesu ahemeleye azurizwe izu ajile, “Nkashe wa wonti ali ne sshomelwa, ayenze huline amwele.
Omwene waneteshe ane, nanshi amazu shagayanjile, afume mhati yakwe ganza hwiteshe amasoho gemenze gewomi.”
Ila ayanji ega alengane hushi Roho, afuatanaje bhala bhabhamwetesheye bhayihuposhela; Ompempo ali seele safumiziwe alengane naje oYesu ali samwamihwe.
Bhamo bhelubhongano, nabhahomvwezye enongwa eezi, bhajile, “Yoli ono kuwaa.”
Bhamo bhayanjile, “Ono Kilisiti.” Ila bhamo bhamo bhajile, “yenu, oKilisiti awezya afume hu Galilaya?
Amaazu segayanga aje oKilisiti aifuma hushikholo sha Daudi na afume hubenselehemu, hushi jiji shahali oDaudi?
Shesho, pala pabhoha olugabhano mhati yelubhongamo alengane no mwahale.
Bhamo mhati yabho handabhakhete, ila nomo wagolosezye okhono gwakwe hwa mwene.
Bhala ofisa bhawela hwa gosi adimi na Mafarisayo, bhope bhabhabhozya, “Yenu semletile?”
Amaofisa bhajile, “Nomo omunti wawayile ayanje nanshi ono haani.”
Amafarisayo nkabhahaga, “Namwe nantele mtejile?
Ahweli omuntu wawonti hwa gosi wahumweteha, au wawonti hwa Mafarisayo?
Ila ebha amabhongano bhasebhemenye endwajizyo - wapete amakhosi.”
O Nikodemo abhabhozya (omwene wabhaliye oYesu imwaha, ali pamo na Mafarisayo),
“Aje endajizyo zyetu ziholonga omuntu ila atejezewe na soti na amanye habhomba?”
Bhayanjile na hubhozye, “Ivi nawe ofumila hu Galilaya? Anza na oyenye aje nomo okuwaa wafumila hu Galilaya.”
Pamande shila munti ahabhala akhaya yakwe.
O Yesu abhalile hwigamba lye Mzeituni.
Khasha shampwiti ahenza nantele hushibhanza, na abhantu bhonti bhabhalila; ahakhala bhasambeleyezye.
Abhandishi na Mafarisayo bhaletela oshe wa khetwe humbombo yehuni. Bhabheha pahati.
Epo nkabhabhalila oYesu, “Mwalimu, oshe ono akhetwe mu huni, mumbombo lyoli.
Esalezi, endajizyo, zya Musa atilajizizye awapole na mawe abhantu nanshi ebho, oyigabhole hwego?
Bhanyanjile ega ahutejesezye aje nkabhabhe ne nongwa ya hutake, ila oYesu au ndeme mpansi ahaandiiha mwinkondi hwa dole hakwe.
Na bhahendeleye ahubhozye, ahemeleye na bhabhozye, “Omwene wasali nembibhi mhati yenyu, abhe wahwande ahupole amawe.”
Waundama nantele pansi, wadola mwinkondi hushidole shakwe.
Nabhahonvwa ego, bhasogoye omo baada ya wamwabho ahwande waliigogolo hata. Owamalishile wabho mwene, paamo no she waali pahati yabho.
O Yesu ahemeleye na nahubhozye wee shee wewe, bhabhatakile bhali hwii? Nomo ata weka walonjile?”
Wagaa, “Nomo ata weka Gosi.” O Yesu waaga, “Hata nene sihulonga. Bhalaga hwi dala lyaho; ahwande esalezi na hwendelele oganje abhombe embibhi nantele.”
Nantele oYesu ayanga na bhantu waga, “Ane endi lukhozyo lyensi; omwene wanzandondolele saganzajende munkisi ila anzabhe nolukhozyo lwe womi.”
Amafarisayo bhabhozye, “Ohwihakikisya wewe; oluhakikisyo lwaho see lwe yooli.”
O Yesu ayanga ahaga, “Hata nkashe ehwihakikisya neen oluhakikisyo lwane, lwe yooli. Emenye hwe nfumile na hwe mbala, ila amwe semumenye hwe nfumile wala hwembala.
Amwe mulonga shibele; ane sehulonga wawonti.
Ane hata nkashe elonje, endonga yane ye lyoli afuatanaje sendi nemwene, endi paamo no daada wantumile.
Ena, hundajizyo zyenyu iyandihwe aje oluhakikisyo lwa bhantu bhabhelilwe lyoli.
Ane ne hwihakikisye, no Daada wantumile ahakikisya.”
Bhabhozya, “Odaada waho ali hwii?” O Yesu ahaaga, “ane semumenye hata Odaada wane semumenye, mgali aje mumenye ane handa mmenye Odaada wane wope.”
Ayanjile enongwa ezi alipepe no lubhutilo nali asambelezya mshibhanza, na ali nomo ata weka wakhete afuatanaje esaa yakwe yaali seele afishe.
Eshi abhabhozya nantele, “Nahwisogolela mwainanza na mwaifwela mumbibhi zyenyu. Hula hwe mbala semuwezizye ahwenze.”
Abhayahudi bhajile, “Obhahwibude humwene, omwene wayanjile, 'hula hwe mbala semuwezezye ahwenze'?”
O Yesu abhabhozye, “Mufuma pansi; ane efuma amwanya. Amwe muli bha munsi omu; ane sendi wa munsi omu.
Eshi eshi, nabhabhozezye aje mwaifwa mumbibhi zyenyu. Labuda mweteshele aje ANE NENE, mwaifwa mu mbibhi zyenyu”.
Eshi bhabhozya, “Awe we nanu?” O Yesu wabhabhozya, Gala ganabhabhozezye ahwande huwandilo.
Endi ne nongwa nyinji ezya yanje nalonje ahusu amwe. Hata sheshi, omwene wantumile we lyoli ne nongwa zyamwonvwezye afume hwa mwene, enongwa ezi nayanga hwa bha Munsi.”
Sebhamwelewe aje ali ayanga nabho ahusu Odaada.
O Yesu ajile, Namu bhahubhosye amwanya Omwana wa Muntu, nkamwailola aje NENE, naje sebhomba lyalyonti nemwene. Nanshi Odaada shansambelezezye, ayanga enongwa ezi.
Omwane wantumile ali pamo nane, na omwene sandeshile nemwene, alenganaje shila muda ebhomba gala gasongwa.”
O Yesu lwayangaga enongwa ezyo bhinji bhamweteshe.
O Yesu ayange hwa Yahudi bhala bhabhamweteshe, “Nkashe mubhakhale mwizu lyane, epo mubhabhe bhanafunzi bhane lyoli,
namwe mubhaimanya elyoli, na elyoli ebhabhabheshe bhaushe.”
Bhajile, Ate tili shi kholo sha Ibulahimu na mwaha setiwayile abhebhaboyi bha muntu wawonti; obhayanje bhole aje, “Tibhabhe bhauusu?”
O Yesu wabhabhozya, “Etesheli, etesheli, embebhozya, wawonti wabhomba embibhi boyi we mbibhi.
Boyi sakhala pakhayo omuda gwonti; omwana akhala nsiku zyonti.
Eshi eshi, nkashele Omwana aibhabheha bhausu, mwaibha bhausu lyoli.”
Embamenye aje amwe mlishikholo sha Ibulahimu; muhwanza angoje alengane ni izu lyane selili no khalo mhati yenyu.
Eyanga enongwa zyenzilolile pamo na Daada wane, namwe pia mubhomba enongwa zya mwahonvwezye hwa daada wenyu.”
Bhayanjile na hubhozye, “Odaada wetu yo Abulahamu.” O Yesu abhabhozya nkashe mungali bhana bha Ibulahimu, handamubhomba embombo zyakwe o Ibulahimu.
Hata sheshi munanza hungoje, omuntu walenjele elyoli aje ehomvwezye afume hwa Ngolobhe. O Ibulahimu sagabhombile esho.
Mubhomba mbombo ya daada wenyu.” Bhabhozya, “Setapepwe muuhuni, tili Odaada omo, yo Ngolobhe.”
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Nkashe Ongolobhe yo Daada wenyu, handa mungene ane, afuatanaje handa mungene ane, afuatanaje enfumile hwa Ngolobhe; wala sehenzele hubeele gwane ila hwa mwene wantumile.
Yenu semgelewa amazu gane? Afuatanaje semuwezizye avumilile agatejezye amazu gane.
Amwe mli bha Daada wenyu, osetano na mhwanza abhombe oluziliho lya Daada wenyu. Aligoji ahwande huwando na sawezizye ahwemelele mlyoli afuatanaje elyoli nemo mhati yakwe. Nkayanga ilenka, ayanga afume mmwoyo gwakwe afuatanaje wilenka na Odaada wilenka.
Hata sheshi, afuatanaje eyanga zye lyoli, semueteshela.
Wenu hulimwe wahakikisye aje endine mbibhi? Nkashe eyanga zye lyoli, yenu semuneteshela?
Omwene wali wa Ngolobhe ateje zya amazu ga Ngolobhe; afwatanaje semulibha Ngolobhe.”
Ayahudi wayanjile na hubhozye, setiyanjile yoli aje awe oli Samaria na oli ni pepo?”
O Yesu ajile, sendi ni pepo; ila ehumwogopa Odaada wane, amwe semunogopa.
Sehwanza oumwamihwe; waline ali weka wahwanza na lonje.
Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, nkashe wawonti ayilikhata izu lyane, sagailola enfwa na mwaha.”
Ayahudi bhabhozya, “Esalaze tamanya aje oli ni pepo. O Abulahamu na kuwaa bhafwiye; oiga, “Nkashe omuntu akhate izu lyaho, saganzabhonje enfwa'.
Awe soli gosi ashile odaada wetu oAbulahamu bhafwiye shenje? Akuwaa bhope bhafwiye. Awe ohwibheha we nanu?”
O Yesu ajile, “Nkashe ehwizuvya nemwene, oumwihwe wane bure; yo Daada waline wanzuvya - ola wa muhuyanga aje Ngolobhe wenyu.
Amwe semumenye omwahale, ila ane emenye omwene. Nkashe embaje, 'semenye,' embabhe nanshi amwe, wilenka. Hata sheshi, engaemenyeamazu gakwe engakhete.
Odaada wenyu oAbulahamu asongwelwe na walilola isiku lyane na aalilolile na asongwelwe.”
Ayahudi bhabhozya,”Sofisizye omuri we maha amusini bado, nawe ololile o Ibulahimu?”
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, o Ibulahimu salibado apapwe, ANE EHWENDI.”
Nkabhatola amawe aje bhakhome, O Yesu ahobhele ahafuma honzehu shibhanza.
O Yesu nali ashile alolile omuntu okipofu ahwande apapwe hwamwehale.
Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozezye, “Mwalimu, “Wenu wabhombile embibhi, omuntu ono au yo yise no nyina paka apapwa mpofu?”
O Yesu ayanga, “Se yayono omuntu wala aise wakwe no nyina wakwe aje bhabhabhombila embibhi, yaani embombo zya Ngolobhe zikwinkushe ashilile hwa mwene.
Tihwanziwa abhombe embombo zyakwe shahuli pasanya. Osiku uhwenza pasetaiwezya abhombe embombo.
Omuda gwendi munsi, ane endi lukhozyo.”
O Yesu nayaanga amazu ega, aswiye mwinkondi, abhombele itotoo huu mate, na wapaha ola omuntu amaso na lila itope.
Wabhozya, bhalaga oyoje mwidimi lye Siloamu (Yebhoneha aje 'watumilwe').” Eshi omuntu abhalile anawe na wawela alola.
Ajilani bhakwe ola omuntu bhabhalolile hula ahwande aje labizi bhajile, Aje! ono wenje ola omuntu wakhalaga na labhizye?” bhamo bhajile, Na yoyo.”
Na bhamo bhamo bhajile, ndadi ono alengane nabho.” Ila ali ayaanga, NENE.”
Bhabhozya, “Esalezi amaso gaho gafunkushe bhole?”
Ajibuye, omuntu wahwetwa Yesuu abhombele itoto na pashe mmaso gane na mbozye, 'Bhalaga Siloamu unawe.' Esheshi nabhalile na nanawile nanapete alole.”
Bhabhozezye, “Ali hwii?” Ajile, “Maanyi.”
Bhatwalile ola omuntu wawaile abhe mpofula hwa Mafarisayo.
Lyope lyali lisiku lye Sabato oYesu lwa lengeye amatoto na hwigule amaso gakwe.
Amafarisayo bhabhozya ahandile bhole alole. Abhabhozya, “Abheshele itole mumaso gane, nanawile, neshi elola.”
Bhamo Amafarisayo bhajile, “Omuntu ono safumile hwa Ngolobhe afwatanaje saikhete eSabato.” Bhamo bhamo bhajile egawezehana wole omuntu we mbibhi abhombe embombo nanshi ezyo hwa wantuna gabhanyisha mhati yabho.
Nkabhabhozya ola ompofila nantele oyiga bhole ahusu omwahale afuatane naje ahiguye amaso gaho?” Ompofu wagaa, “Kuwaa.”
Hata isinku ezi Ayahudi sebhamweteshe aje ali mpofula wope apete alole paka pabhabhakwizizye oise no nyina wapete alole.
Bhabhobhozezye aise no nyina, Aje, ono mwana wenyu wamuyiga apepwe mpofu? awezizye bhole alole esalezi?”
Aise no nyina bhajile, “Timenye aje ono mwana wetu na aje apepwe mpofula.
Shili bhole esalezi alola, setimenye no ola wamwiguye amaso setimenye. Bhozezi yoyo. Muntu gosi. Anzahwiyelezye yoyo.”
Aise no nyina bhayanjile enongwa ezi afuatanaje bhahogope Ayahudi. Shila Ayahudi bhahetehene aje nkashe wawonti ayeteha aje oYesu oKilisti, aitengwa Wibhanza.
Hunamuna ene, oise no nyina wakwe bhajile, “Omuntu gosi, bhozyaji yoyo.”
Hu mara ya bhele, bhakwizizye ola omuntu wawaile abhe mpofula na hubhozye, “Pele Ongolobhe oumwamihwe. Timenye aje omuntu ono muntu we mbibhi.”
Ola omuntu ahayanga, “Abhe we mbibhi, ane sehwelewa. Ahantu hamo hemenye nali mpofula: esalezi ehwenya.”
Eshi nkabhabhozya, “Abhombeye yenu? Ahiguye amaso gaho?”
Ajile, “Embabhozezye ila amwe semuhwonvwa! Yenu mhwanza ahonvwe nantele? Amwe semuhwanza abhe bhanafunzi bhakwe nantele?
Bhalijile naje, “Awe oli mwanafunzi wakwe, ikla ate tili bhanafunzi bha Musa.
Timenye aje Ongolobhe ayanjile no Musa, ila hwomo omuntu, seti menye hwafuma.”
Ola omuntu ayanga na bhahozye, “Yenu, enongwa ezi zyaswije, aje semumenye hwafuma, na ayiguye amaso gane.
Timenye aje Ongolobhe sabhonvwa abhembibhi, nkashe omuntu wawonti ahuputa Ongolobhe na abhombe olusongwo lwakwe, Ongolobhe mwonvwa.
Ahwande peyandile Insi ene sewaile abhoneshe omuntu aiguye amaso gamuntu wapepwe mpofula.
Egalije omuntu ono safumile hwa Ngolobhe, handasabhombile hahonti.”
Bhayanjile na hubhozye, “Uhapepwe mumbibhi mhaani, awe atisambelezya ate?” Nkabhabhenga mshibhanza shabho.
O Yesu ahonvwezye aje bhamwefizye mshibhanza. Amweje na hubhozye, “Aje ohumweteha Omwana wa Muntu?”
Ayanjile naje, “Wenu, Gosi, aje nkemweteshe?”
O Yesu abhozya, “Uloolile, woyanga nawo yayoyo.”
Ola omuntu ayanga, “Gosi ehweteshela epo nkafugamiye.
O Yesu ayanga, “Alonje enenzele Munsi omu aje bhala bhasebhahwenya bhapete ahwenye nabhala bhabhahwenya bhabhe mpofula.”
Bhamo Amafarisayo bhalipamo nawo bhahonvwa amazu ege nahubhozye, “Nate eshi tili mpofula?”
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Nkashe mgali bha mpofu, handasemli ne mbibhi. Hata sheshi muyiga, 'Tilola,' embibhi zyenyu zikheye.”
Etesheli, Etesheli embabhozya, ola wasahwinjila ashilile mundyango gwi goma lye ngole, ila azubha hwidala lya mwabho, omuntu oyo mwibha na fyozi.
Omwane wa hwinjila mundyango yodimi we ngole.
Hwa mweme olinzi we dyango ahwigulilwa. Engolezolyonvwa izu lyakwe na azikwi zya engole zyakwe hu matawa gabho na zifumye honze.
Naizifumya honze ezye zyazili zyakwe azitangulila ne Ngolobhe zihulondolela, afuatanaje bhalimenye izu lyakwe.
Sezinzahumwanze ojenyu ila zinza hupemushile, afuatane sezigamenye amazu ga jenyu.”
O Yesu ayanga ofwana ogu hwabhene, ila sebhazyelewe enongo ezi zyali ayanag hwa bhene.
O Yesu ayanga nabho nantele, “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, Ane endi ndiango gwe ngole.
Bhonti bhabhatanguliye bhibha na bhafyozi, ila engole zibhonvwa.
Ane endi ndiango. Wawonti wahwinjila ashilile huline, aifyoliwa ainjila muhati na fume, wope aipata edyo.
Omwibha sahwenza ila ahwibhe, agoje, natezye, enenzele nkawepate owomi bhabhe nawo winji.
Ane endi dimi mwinza. Odimi omwinza afumya owomi wakwe huu ngole.
Oboyi wabhehwelwe, nasio aje dimi, ola engole se vyoma vyakwe, azilola embwa zihwenza na azileha na zishembele.
Ne mbwa zikhata na nyampanye. Zishembela afuatanaji oboyi wabhe hwelwe sazisajila engole.
Ane endi dimi mwinza embamenye bhabhali bhahuline, wope wamenye ane.
Odaada amenye, nane emenye Odaada, nane eufumwa owomi wane hungole.
Endi nazyo engole zimo zyasaga zya mwigoma eli ezyo zyope ehwanziwa azilete, zyope zinzahonvwe izu lyane zibheligoma limo no dimi omo.
Ene ndiyo maana Odaada angene: Eeufumye owomi wane alafu nantele aweje.
Nomo wawega afume huline, ila eufumya nene. Endi waamuzi gwa ufumye na endi waamuzi ogwagwefwe nantele. Endiposheye elajizyo eli afume hwa Daada.”
Olwaganyishe lwafuma afume hwa yahudi afuatana na maazu ega.
Abhinji bhabho wahaga, “Ali ni pepo ndii na pelusu yenu muhumwonvwa?”
Bhamo bhayanga, “Ege semazu gamuntu wali ni pepo. Ipepo ligamwigula amaso ompofu?”
Nkashahenza Eshikulukulu Shabhehwe Wakifu hu Yelusalemu.
Hwali shipindi shi sasa, oYesu ali ajenda mushibhanza muukumbi wa Sulemani.
Ayahudi nkabhazyongola na hubhozye, “Paka ndii waibheha nsebho? nkashe awe we Kilisiti, tibhozye peupe.
O Yesu ajile, “Embabhozezye ila semuhweteshela. Embombo zyenzibhomba witawa lya Daada wane, ezyo zihakikisha pamwanya yane.
Ata sheshi ahweteshela alenganaje amwe semuli ngole zyane.
Engole zyane zihonvwa izu lyane; Enzimenye, zyope zinanza ane.
Embapiye owomi wewilawila sebhatega na mwaha, nomo hata weka waibhafyola afume mukhono gwane.
Odaada wane, wampiye ebho, yo Gosi ashile bhamwabho bhonti, na nomo hata weka wali no uwezo wa fyole mukhono gwa Daada.
Ane no Daada tili hantu hamo.”
Bhanyemla amawe aje nkabhapole nantele.
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Embalanjile embombo enyinji enyinza afume hwa Daada. Hu mbombo zyalihu kati yezyo zyamuhwanza ampole na mawe?”
Ayahudi bhahaga, “Setihupola na mawe hu mbombo yayonti yeli nyinza, ila okufuru awe wo muntu ohwibheha aje oli Ngolobhe.”
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Seya handihwe mundajizyo zyenyu, 'Nayanjile, “'Amwe muli mangolobhe'”?”
Nkashe abhakwizizye mangolobhe, hwa bhala Izu lya Ngolobhe lya bhenzeye (na Maazu segawezi abudwe),
muyanga ahusu ola Odaada afumizye na husontezye munsi, 'Osalanya,' alengane naje nayanjile, 'ane endi Mwana wa Ngolobhe'?
“Nkashe sebhomba embombo zya Daada wane, mungaje aneteshele.
Ata sheshi, nkashe ezibhomba, ata nkasemuneteshela, zyetesheli embombo aje muwezye amanye na hwelewe aje Odaada ali muhati yane nane muhati ya Daada.”
Bhalenga na hu khate oYesu, ahwisogoleye afume mumakhono gabho.
O Yesu ahwibhalila hwi syelelye Yordani esehemu hula oYohana hwahozyaga ahwande, ahakhala ohwo.
Abhantu abhinji bhahenza hwa Yesu. Bhahendeleye ayanje, “O Yohana lyoli sagabhombile eishara yoyonti, ila enongwa zyonti zyayanjile Yohana ahusu omuntu ono zye yoli.”
Abhantu abhinji bhamweteshela oYesu epo.
Omuntu omo itawa lyakwe ali yo Lazalo ali bhinu. Afumiye hu Bethania, eshijiji sha Mariamu na odaada wakwe oMasa.
Ali yo Mariamu yayola wapeshe Ogosi Amarhamu na hufute amagaga gakwe hwii sisi lyakwe, ola oholo wakwe oLazalo wali bhinu.
Ailombo ebha bhatumile oujumbe hwa Yesu na yanje, “Gosi, enya ola wogene abhawa.”
O Yesu na honvwa ajile, “Empongo ene se yafwe, ila, baada yeshoye umwamihwe wa Ngolobhe aje Omwana wa Ngolobhe apate amwamihwe ashilile hwenyo empongo.”
O Yesu agene oMasa no dada wakwe no Lazalo.
Lwa honvwezye aje oLozalo bhinu, oYesu akheye insiku izbhele ashizanye pala pahali.
Eshi baada yelyo abhabhozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Saali huu Yahudi nantele.”
Abhanafunzi bhabhozya, “Mwalimu, Ayahudi bhali bhalenga ahupole na mawe, na aweohonza awele hwohwo nantele?”
O Yesu ayanga, “Esala zya pasanya sezili kumi ne zibhele? Omuntu ajenda pasanya sawezizye abomele, afuatanaje alola hulukhozyo lwa pasanya.
Ata sheshi nkashe anzajende no siku, anzabomele afuatanaje olukhozyo nalumo muhati yakwe.”
O Yesu ayanga enongwa ezi, baada ye nongwa ezi, abhabhozya, “Owamwetu oLazalo agonile, ila embala aje empate ahubhosye afume mutulo.”
Abhanafunzi bhabhozya, “Gosi, nkashe agonile, anzabhoshe.
Ensiku izyo oYesu ali ayanga ahusu enfwa ya Lazalo, ila abhene bhamenye aje ayanga ahusu agone otulo.
O Yesu nkayanga na bhene pazelu pazelu, “O Lazalo afwiye.
Lusongwo lwendiinalwo hulimwe aje senahali hula aje mubhe no lweteshelo. Saali hwa mwene.”
O Tomaso wa hetwaga Pacha, abhozya abhanafunzi amwabho, “Nate saalitifwe pamo no Yesu.”
O Yesu lwa henzaga amweje oLazalo akheye mwilende insiku zine.
Yope e Bethania yaali pepe ne Yelusalemu nanshi ekilometa arubaini ne zisanu eshi.
Abhinji kati ya Yahudi bhahenzele hwa Masa no Mariamu abhazinde alengane no holo wabho.
O Masa ahonvwa aje oYesu ahwenza, abhalile akhomane nawo, ila oMariamu ahendeleye akhale pakhaya.
O Masa abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, nkashe ogabhiye epa, okolo wane handa safwiye.
Ata sheshehwelewa aje lyalyonti lyobhalabhe afume hwa Ngolobhe, anzahupele.”
O Yesu abhozya, okolo waho anzavyoshe nantele.”
O Masa abhozya, emenye aje anzavyonshe huu vyoho wi siku lya mwisho.”
O Yesu abhozya, “Ane endi luvionsyono womi; omwane waneteshela, ata nkashe aifwa, hata sheshi aibha ahwizya;
no mwene wahwizya na netehsele ane saga ifwa. Uhweteshela eli?”
Wabhozya aje, “'Sawa, Gosi ehweteshela aje awe oli Kilisiti, Mwana wa Ngolobhe, omwene wa hwenza munsi.”
Nahamala ayanje eli, abhalile ahukwizye odada wakwe oMariamu hufaraga. Ajile, “Omwalimu ali epa nantele ahukwizya.”
O Mariamu na hovwezye ega, abhoshele nanali na bhale hwa Yesu.
Wope oYesu ali sayenzele aliseele muhati ye shijiji, aliseele lwa khomanaga no Masa.
Ayahudi bhabhali no Maliamu munyumba na bhala bhabhli wahuzinda, bhabhoshele nanali na afume honze, bhalondoleye; bhamenye aje abhala hwi kaburi aje alile ohwo.
O Mariamu, ahafiha pala oYesu palolaga na agwiye pansi pamagaga gakwe na hobhozye, “Gosi, nkashe ogahali epa, oholo wane hande sagaafwiye.”
O Yesu nalola alila, na Ayahudi bhahenzele pamo nawo bhali bhalila huu moyo gabho na sebhelele;
ajile, “Mugonizye hwii? Bhabhozye, Gosi, enza oyenye.”
O Yesu alilile.
Ayahudi nkabhayanga, “Oyenye sha gene oLazalo!”
Bhamo muhati yabho bhajile, “Sio yayono, omuntu wabhombile amaso gola wali mpofu, sagabhombile ono muntu aje agaje afwe?”
O Yesu alilaga humwoyo gwakwe nantele, abhalile hwi lende. Hwali ligwenya, niiwe libhehwele pamwanya lyakwe.
O Yesu ajile, “Lyefwi iwe.” O Masa, oilombo wakwe oLazalo, omwene wafwiye, abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, hu muda ogu, obele gubhabhe gu bholile, alenganaje ali fwee ensiku zine.”
O Yesu abhozya, “Ane senabhozezye aje, nkashe ohweteshela, obhaulole oumwamu wa Ngolobhe?”
Nnkabhalyefwa iwe. O Yesu abhosya amaso gakwe amwanya naje, “Daada, ehusombezya afuatanaje onomvwa.
Namenye aje ononvwa omuda gwonti, ila alengane no lubhongano lwalwe meleye anzongole aje enjanjile ega, aje bhapate ahweteshele aje awe ontumile.”
Naayanga ega, alilile hwizu igosi, “Lazalo, fuma honze!”
Ofwe afumile honze apinyilwe amakhono na magaga husanda zyakhatile, na amaso gakwe apinyilwe ne shitambala.” O Yesu abhabhozya, “Mwigulili muleshele abhalaje.”
Oyahudi abhinji bhabhahenzele hwa Mariamu nalole oYesu habhombaga, bhamweteshela;
bhamo bhabhalile hwa Mafarisayo na bhabhozye enongwa zyazibhombile oYesu.
Agosi bha dimi na Mafarisayo bhabhongene pandwemo mwi baraza na yaanje, “Tibhabhombe yenu? Omuntu ono abhoembombo enyinji.
Nkashe tibhahuleshe eshi mwene, bhonti bhanza humweteshe; Alumi bhayenza na hweje vyonti evyetu ni taifa lyetu.”
Hata omuntu omuntu muhati yabho, oKayafa, waali dimi Ogosi omwaha ogwo, abhabhozya, “Semumenye hahonti.
Sahusebhelela aje ehwanziwa aje omuntu omo afwe esababu ya bhanje ashile itaifa lyonti na litega.”
Eege sohagayanjile afuatanaje no mwene, mhati yakwe, ali dimi ogosi omwaha gula, ayanjile aje oYesu aifwa sababu ya bha munsi;
na se huje hwabha munsi bhene ila oYesu apate abhabhonganye abhana bha Ngolobhe bhabha nyanpene hutali hutali.
Eshi ahwandile isiku elyo na hwendelela bhapanjile ahugoje oYesu.
O Yesu sagajendile apazelu pazelu hwa Yahudi, ila asogeye epa na bhale ensi yelipeepe ni poli hunsi yehwetwa Efraimu. Epo akheye nabhanafunzi.
Epasaka ya Yahudi yali pepe, na bhinji bhazubhile abhale hu Yelusalemu honze yensi sheli sele ePasaka nkabhahwiyozye bhebho.
Bhali bha humwanza oYesu, na ayanje kila muntu na bhali bhemeleye mshibhanza, “Musebha yenu? Aje saga ayenza mushi kulukulu?”
Owakati ou ogosi wa dimi na Mafarisayo bhali bhafumizye endajizyo aje nkashe omo aimanya oYesu hwali, ahwanziwa afumye etaarifa aje nkabhapate ahukhate.
Isiku ilya sita selisele ePasaka, oYesu abhalile hu Bethania, hwa hali oLazalo, omwene wali avyonshele afume hwa bhafwe.
Bhalenganyizya eshalye shana ndabhela owho, no Martha abhombelaga owakati owo oLazaro ahali pamo na bhale bhabhakheye pashalye pandwemo no Yesu.
Pamande oMariamu ahege eratli ye manukato gagalenganyiziwe hu nardo enyinza, gagali ne maana engosi, wapaha oYesu mumagaga, na husyomole hwi sisi lyakwe; enyumba yonti yamemile nunsi gwe manukato.
O Yuda Iskariote, omo we bhanafunzi bhakwe, ambaye wanzahugalushe oYesu, ajile,
“Yenu amanukato ega segagalu ziwanyaga huu mpeya mia zitatu na bhapele apena?”
Wope ayanjile ego, sio aje hubhasajile apena, afuatanaje ali mwibha: omwene ali wa bheshe ehela na ali ahwega zimo zyazibhelwe omwo zya mwene yoyo.
O Yesu ajile, “Leshi abheshe hali naho alengane ni siku lya syelwe hwane.
Apena mwaibha nabho ensiku zyonti ila ane semwaibha nane ensiku zyontii.”
Owinji ogosi wa Yahudi bhapete amanye aje oYesu ali ohwo bhopebhenza, sio aje yo Yesu tu ila bhalole no Lazaro ola oYesu wavyonsezye afume hwa bhafwe.
Bhope agosi bhayangene aje wagoje oLazaro;
alengane no mwale abhinji katika Wayahudi walienda zao bha bhalile ahumweteshela oYesu.
Na isiku ila bhele uwinji gosi wali hushikulukulu bhahonvwezye aje oYesu ahwenza hu Yelusalemu,
bhahejile amasamba ge mikwige mitende na afume hoze na abhale ahumwejelele na bhakhomile ekelele, “Hosana! Asailwe wahwenza hwitawa lya Gosi, Omwene we Israeli.”
O Yesu ayeje enyana-ye punda ayipandale; nanshi shila shehandihwe,
“Oganje ahwogope, lendu Sayuni; enya, Omwene waho ahwenza, apende enyana-ye punda.”
Abhanafunzi bhakwe sebhagelee amambo ega epo ahwande; ila oYesu na mwamihwe, nkabhakomboha aje amambo ega gahandihwe na huje abhombile amambo ega hwa mwene.
Lila ikundi lyalya pandwemo no Yesu lula lwa kwizyaga oLazaro afume mwilende, bhahakikisya hwabhanje.
Yali alengane neshi aje uwinji wa bhantu bhabhalile ahuposhele alenganaje bhahomvwezye aje abhombole embo eyo.
Amafarisayo bhakwepelana bhene hwa bhene, “Enya, esalezi semuwezizey abhombe lya lyonti; enya, ensi ebhalile hwa mwene.”
Bhamo Ayunani bhali pandwemo na bhala bhabhalile apute hushikulukulu.
Ebhabhaliye oFilipo, wafumile Betsaida ye Galilaya, bhalabha bhaga, “Gosi, ate tiziliha ahulole oYesu.”
O Filipo ahabhala abhozya o Andrea; Andrea no Filipo bhabha ahubhozye oYesu.
O Yesu ayanga ahaga, “Esala efishile hwa Mwana wa Adamu amwamihwe.
Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, abhenyu he ngano nkase hagwiye pansi hafwa, hakhala shesho hene; ila nkahafwa, hana pape endondo zinyinji.
Omwane wasongwa owomi wakwe anzautezye; ila ola wauvitwa owomi wakwe munsi omu anzaugolosye hata womi wewila wila.
Omuntu wawonti wanza ambombele ane, andondolelaje; nane pehwendi omuntu wane paibha. Omuntu wawonti wabhombela ane anzanogope.
Esalezi omwoyo gwane guhwalangana: nane enje bhole? 'Odaada, anfyozye esala ene'? Ndio maana enjifishiye esala ene.
Odaada, alimwamishe itawa lyaho.” Izu ilinza afume humwanya na huje, “Endimwamisha nantele embali mwamishe nantele.”
Olubhongano lwalwahemeleye peepe nawo bhahonvwa, bhayanga aje huli omungurumo. Bhamo bhajile, “Ohalo ozelu ayanjile nawo.”
O Yesu abhabhoyza naje, “Izu ili selya henzele huline, ila hwalimwe.
Esalezi oulonje wensi ene ehweli: Esalezi ogosi wensi aitagwa honze.
Nane nkemwamihwe munsi, embarute bhonti huline.”
Wayanjile ego abhonesyaga aje enfwa bhole ya mwaifwa.
Olubhongano lwaga, “Ate tonvwezye hundajizyo aje oKillisiti aibha wilawila. Awe oiga bhole, 'Omwana wa Adamu amwamihwe pamwanya'? Ono Omwana wa Muntu wenu?”
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Olukhozyo luhweli pandwemo namwe omuda ododo. Bhalaji afuatane naje mlinalyo olukhozyo, aje enkisi nkepotwe aitole. Omwene wabhala munkisi samenye hwabhala.
Muli nalwo olukhozyo, lweteshelaji olukhozyo olwo nkamubhe bhana bhelukhozyo.” O Yesu ayanjile ega ahwisogolela ahobha bha salole.
Japo oYesu abhombile eishara nyinji witazi lyabho, ila sebha mwetesheye
lifishe izu lya kuwaa oIsaya, lyayanjile: “Gosi, wenu waizyeteshela enongwa zyetu? Okhono gwa Gosi gwiguliwe wenu?”
Ndio maana abhene sebhahetesheye, alengane naje oIsaya ayanjile nantele,
“Abhadiye amaso, na agabheshele makhome amoyo gabho, bhageteha engabhaponia.”
O Isaya ayanjile enongwa ezi afuatanaje alolile oumwamu wa Yesu na ayanjile enongwa zyakwe.
Ila, hata bhagosi abhinji bhamweteshe oYesu; ila alengane na Mafarisayo, sebhaheteha bhahogope atengwe msibhanza.
Bhasongwelwe ahwilole hwa bhantu ahwilole ahwilole hwa Ngolobhe.
O Yesu afumizye izu lyakwe naje, “Omwene waneteshela ane, saneteshela nene wene ila nola wantumile ane,
omwane wambonela ane ahubho ane ahubhonela yayola wantumile.
Ane nahenzele nanshi olukhozyo munsi aje shila muntu waneteshela aganje akhale munkisi.
Nkashe omuntu wawonti anzahonvwe amazu gane sagakhata, ane sehulonga; afuatanaje sagahenzele ailonje insi ila injifyole insi.
Omwene wananza ane nkasage teha amazu gane, ali nawo wahulonga: izu ilyo lyenjenjile lyalyaihulonga isiku lya mwisho.
Afwanaje ane senayanjile hunafsi yane. Ila yo Daada wantumile, omwene yoyo andajizizye lye mbalombelele na yanje.
Ane emenye aje endajizyo zyakwe zye womi wewilawila; ila ego gelombelela ane - nanshi Odaada shambozezye, shashesho shelombelela hwa bhene.”
Isalezi seliseele eshikulukulu ye pasaka, afuatanaje oYesu amenye aje esala ya efishile eyaje aifuma munsi omo abhale hwa daada, endwemo abhagene abhantu bhakwe bhabhali munsi, abhagene oupeo.
Osetano abhehwelwe haani humwoyo gwa Yuda Iskariote, omwana wa simoni, ahushitushile oYesu.
O Yesu amenye aje odaada abheshele evintu humakhono gakwe naje afumile hwa Ngolobhe nantele ali abhala hwa Ngolobhe.
Abhoshele pashalye na ahalile pansi omwenda gwa honze. Ahejile itaulo ahwifunjile yoyo.
Nkahaponya amenze mumbakuri na wanda abhozye amagaga abhanafunzi bhakwe na bhapugute ni taulo lya hwifunjile yoyo.
Ahenza hwa Petro, na oPetro ahabhozya, “Gosi, uhwanza anazye amagaga gane?”
O Yesu ayanga na hubhozye, “Lyebhomba solimenye esalezi ila eshi obhahwelewe pamande.”
O Petro abhozya, “Sobhanozye amagaga gane na mwaha.” O Yesu ajile, “Nkashe sembahumwezye sobhabhe ne sehemu pandwemo nane.”
O Simoni Petro abhozya, “Gosi, onganjenozye amagaga gane wene, ila namakhono ni twe lyane.”
O Yesu abhozya, “Wawonti wayojile sahwanziwa ahwoje ila amagaga gakwe, nahuje mwinza obele gwakwe gwonti; amwe muli bhinza, ila se mwenti.”
O Yesu amenye ola wanzahugalushile; ndio maana ajile, semwenti mli bhinza.”
O Yesu lwali abhozizye amagaga gabho na wega omwenda gwakwe na khale nantele, abhabhozya, “Aje Muhwelewa hale hembabhombela?
Mukwizya ane “Mwalimu” nantele myiga Gosi ene yoli, afuatanaje endi shesho.
Nkashe ane ne Gosi ne mwalimu, embozizye amagaga genyu, amwe namwe ehwanziwa abhozye amwenyu amagaga.
Embapiye ofwana aje amwe mubhombe nanshi ane zyanabhombile hulimwe.
Etesheli, Etesheli, embabhozya, oboyio segosi ashile ogosi wakwe; wala yule ambaye ametumwa ni mkuu kuliko yule aliye mtuma.
Nkashe ozimenye enongwa ezi osaiwaje nkobhazibhombe.
Seyanga aje amwe mwenti, afuatanaje embamenye bhala bhembachaguye - eyanga ezi ili aje amazu gawezye akamilishe: 'Omwene walya ibumunda lyane ambasesezye ikhaata lyakwe.'
Embabhozya izii esalezi shalilisele afume aje nkalyaifumila, mwawezye ahweteshele aje ane NENE.
“Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, wamposhela ane ahuposhela yayola wantumile mimi.”
O Yesu lwa yangaga ega, ayanzihwe hu mwoyo, ahakikisizye na yanje, “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya aje omo wenyu aingaluha.”
Abhanafunzi bhakwe bha henyanya, bhahuswiga aje wenu wahuyanga.
Hwali ne meza, omo we bhanafunzi bhakwe ahagamiye musifubha mwa Yesu ola oYesu wagene.
O Simoni oPetro abhozezye omwanafunzi ono na huje, “Tibho wenu wahuyanga.”
Omwanafunzi ola wahagamiye mshifubha mwa Yesu na hubhozye, “Gosi, yonanu?”
O Yesu ajile, “Wemba tobhezye ishipande shi bumunda na hhupele.” Shesho nali atobhezezye ibumunda, apiye oYuda omwana wa Simoni Iskariote.
Baada yi bumunda, Osetano amwinyiye. O Yesu ahabhozya, “Haala howanza abhombe habhombe nanali.”
Nomo omuntu pameza wamenye emaana ya Yesu ayanje enongwa ezi hwa mwahale.
Bhamo bhasebhele aje afuatanaje oYuda ekhete ifuko lye mpeya, oYesu abhozya, “Kala evintu vyatihwanza vye shikulukulu,” au aje ahwanziwa afumye evintu hwa peena.
O Yuda na hejelela ibumunda, ahafuma honze nanali; hwali sikuu.
O Yuda lwali asogoye, oYesu ayanjile, “Eshi omwana wa Adamu amwamihwe, no Ngolobhe amwamihwe hwa mwehale.
Ongolobhe anzahumwamishe hwa mwene yoyo, na anza humwamishe nanali.
Bhana mwadodo, ehwendi pamo namwe omuda dodo. Mubhananze, nkashe shanabhabhozizye Ayahudi, 'Hwembala, semuwezizye ahwenze.' esalaze embabhozya amwe, nantele.
Embapiye endizyo empya, aje mganane nanshi ane shehabhagene amwe, shesho shesho namwe ehwanziwa aganane mwemwe hu mwemwe.
Afuatanaje neli awantu bhanzamanye aje amwe muli bhanafunzi bhane, nkashe muli no lugano shila omo no wamwabho.”
O Simoni Petro abhozezye, “Gosi, ubhala hwii?” O Yesu ayanga, “Apantu pe haibhala esalezi sobhawezye anfuate, ila obhananze pamande.
O Petro abhozya, “Gosi, yenu ensafuate hata salezi? Ane embafumwe olwizyo lyane huliwe.”
O Yesu ajile, “Aje obhafumwe olwizyo shauli ya huline? Etesheli etesheli ehubhozya, ehanda sebhakuje bila haana mara hatatu.”
Oganje aguleshe omwoyo gwaho abhe ahwalangane. Ohumweteshela Ongolobhe neteshele nane.
Mu nyumba ya Daada wane muli mabhombo minji agakhale; nkashe semugali esho hande ebhozezye, afuatanaje embala abhalenganyizye apakhale awe.
Nkashe embale nabhalenganyizye nayenza nantele abhakaribizye hwa line, aje pendi ane namwe mubhanje.
Mumenye idala hwembala.”
O Tomaso abhozezye oYesu, “Gosi, setimenye hwobhala; Aje! Tibhalimanye bhole idala?
O Yesu abhozezye, “Ane endili dala, lyoli, no womi; nomo wagenza hwa Daada ila ashilile huline.
Nkashe mugamenye ane, handamumenye no Daada wane nantele; ahwande esalezi na hwendelele muhamanya na mulolile omwane.”
O Philipo abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, tilanje Odaada, esho shibhabhe shitiyiye.”
O Yesu abhozya, “Sendi pandwemo namwe hu muda otali, no oliseele somenye ane, Philipo? Wawonti wandolile ane alolile Odaada; shili bhole oyanga, 'Tilanje Odaada'?
Semuhweteshela aje ane endi muhati ya Daada, oDaada ali muhati yane? Amazu geyanga hulimwe seyanga kulengana nane nene; baadala yakwe, Odaada wa hwizya mhati yane abhomba embombo yakwe.
Neteshele ane, aje ehwendi muhati ya Daada, no Daada ahweli mhati yane; shesho neteshe ane afutane nembombo zyane eshi.
Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, omwane waneteshela, ane embombo zila zyebhomba, aibhomba embombo ezyo wope nantele na aibhomba hata embombo engosi afuatanaje embala hwa Daada.
Hahonti hamulabha hwitawa lyane, embabhombe aje Odaada nkamwamihwe hwa Mwana.
Nkashe mulabhe ahantu hahonti hwi tawa lyane, eho embabhombe.
Nkashe mubhangane, mubhazighate endajizyo zyane.
Nane embahulabhe Odaada, Wope anzabhapele omwavwi wamwabho aje abhe pandwemo namwe wilawila,
Ompempo we lyoli. Ensi sewezizye ahuposhele omwane afuatana naje seuhulola, au humemwe omwene, ata sheshi amwe mumenyo omene, afuatane na aibha muhati yenyu.
Senaibhaleha mubhene; Naiwela hulimwe.
Hu nsiku endodo, ensi seyayindola nantele, ila amwe mundola. Afuatane naje ahwizya namwe mwaizya nantele.
Hwi siku elyo mwaimanya aje ane ehwendi muhati ya Daada, naje amwe muli muhati yane, naje ane endi muhati yenyu.
Wawonti wakhata endajizyo na zibhombe, yayola omo wangene ene na wangene ane; na wangene ane aiganwa no Daada wane, naihugana na naihwibhonesya ane nene hwa mwene.”
O Yuda (siyo Iskariote) abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, Aje! Yenu yebha fumile aje obhahwibhonesye wewe?
O Yesu ayanjile ajile, “Nkashe wawonti wangene, abhakhate izu lyane. Odaada wane anza hugane, na tibhahwenze hwa mwene na tibhabheshe okhalo gwetu pandwemo no mwahale.
Wawonti wasangene ane, sakhata amuzu gane. Izu lya mhonvwa se lya line ila Daada wantumile.
Enjanjile enongwa ezi hwalimwe, omuda gwe hwizya pandwemo namwe.
Ata sheshi, Mfariji, Ompepo Ofinjile, lyane Odaada aihutuma hwitawa lyane, aibhasambelezya enongwa zyonti na aibhabheha aje mkoboshe gonti gehayanjile hulimwe.
Olusongwo embapele olusongwo lwane amwe. Sembapele na ensi sepela. Muganje abheshe amoyo genyu abhe no walangano, no bhonga.
Mwahonvwezye shila shehabhabhozezye, esogola nantele naiwela hulimwe.' Nkashe mugangene ane, mwenzabhe no losongwo afuatanaje embala hwa Daada, afuatanaje Odaada gosi ashile ane.
Esalezi yanje namwe amazu gaminji, afuatanaje ogosi wensi ene ahwenza omwene saali ne nguvu pamwanya yane.
Sembayanje namwe amazu gaminji, afuatanaje ogosi wensi ene ahwenza omwene saali ne nguvu pamwanya yane,
aje ensi epate amanye aje egene Odaada, ehomba hala Odaada handajizya ane, nanshi shila shampiye endajizyo. Bhoshi, tifume apantu epa.
Ane endi mzabibu ogu gwe lyoli, odaada wane omwene mkulima we mzabibu.
Isamba lya salipapa endondo, elyefwa ila isamba lya lipapa endondo alyefwa ili aje nkali papaje tee.
Amwe muli bhinza alengane ne nongwa yembabhozezye.
Mukhale muhati yane na muhati yenyu. Nanshi isamba seligapapa lyene nkaselili mumuzabibu, shesho namwe, nkase mukhala muhati yane.
Ane endi mzabibu; amwe muli nsamba. Wakhala muhati yane nane muhati yakwe, omuntu ono apapa endondo zinyinji, afuatanaje bila ane amwe simuwezizye abhombe embombo yayonti.
Nkashe omuntu wawonti wasaga abhakhale muhati yane, abhatagwe nanshi osamba na hwome; abhantu bhabhonganya amasamba na agataje humwoto, na galongolela.
Nkashe mubhakhale muhati yane, na nkashe amazu gane ganzakhale muhati yenyu, labhaji lyalyonti lya mubhahwanze, namwe mubhabhombelwe.
Hweli odaada amwamihwe, naje mupapa endondo zinyinji naje bhanafunzi bhane.
Nkashe odaada wane shangene ane, ane nane embagene amwe, khalaji mulugano lwane.
Nkashe mubhakhate endajizyo zyane, mubhakhale mulugano lwane nashi shehete endajizyo yza daada wane na khale mulugano lwakwe.
Enjanjile enongwa ezi hulimwe aje olusongwo lwane lubhe muhati yenyu na aje olusongwo lwenyu lubhombeshe abhe golusu.
Olu lulajizyo lwane aje mganane amwe hu mwemwe nanshi sembagene amwe.
Nomo omuntu waali nolugano ogosi ashile ou aje afumwe olwizo lwakwe eshauli ya bhanje.
Amwe muli bha mwetu nkamubhabhombe gala gembalajizya.
Sembakwizyabhaboyi, afuatanaje oboyi samanya kila habhomba ogosi wakwe. Embakwizya amwe bhamwetu, alenganaje embabhozezye enongwa zyonti zyenonvwezye afume hwa Daada.
Semwansaluye ane ila ane nabhasaluye amwe na bhabheshe aje mubhalaje apape endondo, na endondo zyenyu zipate akhale. Eli lili eshi aje hahonti hamulabha hwa Daada hwi tawa lyane, anzabhapele.
Enongwa ezi embalajizya aje mganane shila muntu nowamwabho.
Nkashe ensi enzabhavitwe, mumanye aje ebhanvitwe nene sheli seele abhavitwe amwe.
Nkashe mugali bha munsi, ensi handa ebhagene nanshi bha mwabho; Afuatanaje amwe semuli bha munsi na afwatanaje senabhachaguye afume munsi, afuatane neshi insi ebhavitwa.
Komboshi izu lyana bhabhozezye, 'Oboyi se gosi ashile ogosi wakwe.' Nkashe bhanjenvezye ane, bhaibhaye nvya lyane, handabhakhete iklyalimwe lyape.
Bhaibhabhombela amambo ega gonti alengane ni tawa lyane alengane sebhamenye ola wantumile.
Nkashe engalisenenzele na bhabhozye handasabhabhombile embibhi, ila esalezi sebhali noudhuru hu mbibhi zyabho.
Wanvwitwa ane ahuvitwa yo Daada nantele.
Nkashe sembombile embombo muhati yabho enganomo omo wabho waibhombile, handasebhali ne mbibhi; ila esalezi wabhombile gonti gabhele bhalolile na bhvitilwe ane no Daada wane.
Ene efumila aje izu likamilishe lyalyandihwe mundajizyo: 'Zyabhowanvitwa ane bila li kosa.'
Wazinda ayenzele, wembahufume hulimwe afume hwa Daada, ono yayono, Ompepo we lyoli, wafuma hwa Daada, aihakikisizya.
Amwe mhakikisizya afuatanaje muuli pandwemo nane afume ahwande.
Embabhozya enongwa ezi aje mganje avisye.
Bhaibhafumya mwonze mumabhanza; lyoli esala ehwenza shila waibhabuda aisebha aje abhomba mbombo enyinza hwa Ngolobhe.
Bhaibhabhomba enongwa ezi alengane sebhamanye Odaada wala sebhamenye ane.
Embabhozezye enongwa ezi aje ensiku nkazyafiha zyafumile mwaiwezya agakomboshe na shila shanabhabhozezye muwezye bhene. Sembhabhozezye alengane ne nongwa ezi ahwande huwandilo alenganaje nali pandwemo namwe.
Japo esalezi, embala hwola wantumile; ia nomo omo wenyu wambozezya, “Obhala hwii?”
Alengane enjanjile enongwa ezi hulimwe, ozungumizu umemile muoyo genyu.
Ata shesho, embabhozya elyoli: shinza hulemwe nkanasogola; afuatanaje wabhazinzya sagayenza hulimwe; ila nkanabhala naihutuma hulimwe.
Nkawenza oyo wabhazinzya aiyomezya ensi ahusiane ne mbibhi, ahusiane ne lyoli na ahusiane nolonzi.
Ahusiane ne mbibhi, alenganaje sebhaneteshe ane,
ahusiane ne lyoli, afuatanaje embala hwa Daada na semwaindola nantele;
ahusiane no lonzi alenganaje ogosi we nsi ene alongwilwe.
Endinago minji gabhabhozye, ila semubhagelewe esalezi.
Ila, omwene, Ompepo welyoli, nkawenza aibhalongozya mulyoli yonti; afuatanaje sagaiyanga hu sababu yakwe yoyo; ila wawonti ganzagonvwe anzagayanje amambo ego; na aigabhonesya hulimwe amambo gagayenza.
Omwene aimwamiha ane, alenganaje aigayanga mambo gane na agatangazye hulimwe.
Evintu vyonti vyalinavyo oDaada vyaline; eshi eshi, enjanjile aje Ompepo ayaga amambo gane na gabhonesye hulimwe.
Bado ensiku ndodo, semwaindola nantele; baada ye muda ododo nantele, mwaindola.”
Bhamo awanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozanya, “Ye yenu yatibhozya, “omuda ododo, na semwaindola nantele,' no omuda ododo nantele,' mwaindola,' alengane embale hwa Daada?”
Eshi eshi bhayanga, “Hantu nshi hayanga, 'Bado omuda odod'? Setimenye zyayanga.”
O Yesu alolile aje wazilishe ahubhozezye, wope ayanga, “Muhubhozezya mubhene ahusu eli, shenjanjile, 'Bado omuda ododo, semwaindola nantele; baada ye muda ododo mwaindola'?
Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, mwalila na hwilombozye, ila ensi yayisongwa, mwazugumile, ila ensi enzugumila yenyu yaigaluha lusongwo.
Oshe abhazugumizu lula lwa bhano uchungu alengane naje omuda gwa pape gufishile; ila nkawa papa omwana, sakomboha nantele ambabha, afuatanaje no lusongwo lwakwe aje omwana apepwe munsi.
Amwe nantele muzugumiye esalezi, ila naibhalola nantele; na moyo genyu gaisongwa na nomo waiwezye abhefwezye olusongwo lwenyu.
Isiku elyo semwaimbozya enongwa. Etesheli, etesheli, Embabhozya nkamulabhe lyalyonti hwa Daada, aibhapela hwi tawa lyane.
Paka semulabhile lyalyonti witawa lyane; labhaji mubhaposhele aje olusongwo lwenyu lukamilishe.
Enyanjile namwe hunjango yasemanyiha, ila esala ehwenza senaiyanga hujango yasemanyiha baada yesho naibhabhoyza papa zelu ahusu Odaada.
Isiku elyo mwailabha hwitawa lyane, sembabhozya aje nailabha hwa Daada husababu yenyu;
Afuatanaje Odaada yoyo abhagene alenga mungene ane na afuatanaje muneteshe aje enfumile hwa Daada.
Nafumile hwa Daada na enenzele munsii; nantele, esogola munsi na embala hwa Daada”.
Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozya, “Oloola, esalezi oyanga papazelu na sotumila amalibho.
Esalezi, timenye aje amenye amambo gonti, na sohwanza omuntu wawonti abhozezye enongwa. Afutanaje tihweteshela aje ofuma hwa Ngolobhe.
O Yesu ajile, “Esalezi eneteshe?”
Enya, esala ehwenza, yoli nalyoli ifishile, mwainuha kila muntu amwabho mwaindeha nene. Ila sendi nemwene afuatanaje oDaada ahweli nane.
Embabhozya amambo ega aje muhati yane mubhe na songwe. Munsi muli amashida, ila hwipeli omwoyo, enjitolile ensi.
O Yesu ayanjile amambo ega; nantele abhozya amaso gakwe ahwenyelezye amwanya na yanje, “Daada, esala efishile; mwamishe omwana waho ili omwana wope nkamwamishe awe -
nashi shila shopiye enguvu huu vyonti vyavili nobele aje abhapele owomi wewilawila bhonti wopiye.
Ou wowomi wewilawila: aje bhamanye awe, Ongolobhe we lyoli na woli humwene, nolo wotumile, oYesu Kilisti.
Namwamishe epa pansi, naimalezye embombo yohampiye aje enjibhombe.
Esalaezi, Daada, omwamishe ane pamoja nawe wewe huumihwe uula wendi nowo pandwemo nawe sheti seele abhombwe ensi.
Nalikwinkuye itawa lyaho hwa bhantu bhompiye epa pansi. Bhali bhantu bhaho; ila wampiye ane. na bhope bhalikhete izu lyaho.
Esalezi ohwelewa aje shila hantu hompiye ane hafumile huliwe,
hu mazu gala gompiye ane— Embapelile abhahale amazu ego. Wagejeleye nantele na wamanya aje ane enfumile huliwe, na bheteshela aje awe wontumile.
Embaputila abhahale. Senjiputila ensi ila bhala bhompiye afuatanaje abhahale wahuliwe.
Evintu vyonti evyahuline vyahuliwe na vila vyolinavyo vyahuline nane emwamihwa hwevyo.
Ane sehwendi nantele munsi, ila bhahale bhahweli munsi, nane esalezi ehwenza huliwe. Daada Wozelu, omwoyo obhasonje hwi tawa lyaho lila bhabhe nolwonvano nanshi shila ane nawe shatili no lwonvwano.
Nanali nabho, nabhasonjele hwitawa lyompiye; Nawasonjele, na nomo mhati yabho watejile ila omwana otezu, amazu nkagatimile.
Esalezi ehwenza huliwe; ila eyanga ega munsi aje olusongwo lwane lugoloshe muhati yabho bhebho.
Embapiye izu lyaho; embavitilwe aje abhene sebha munsi, nanshishi ane shasendi wa munsi.
Sembaputila aje obhefwe munsi ila obhasonje nola obhibhi.
Abhene sebhamunsi nanshi shila ane shasenali wa munsi.
Ubhabheshe bhagolosu huliwe wewe mu lyoli; izu lyahaho ye lyoli.
Wantunile munsi, naane embafumile munsi.
Alengane nabhene ane neene ehwifumya huliwe aje wope nkabhahwifumyaje huliwe hwela elyoli.
Sio aje ebha bhene bhembaputila na bhala bhabha yeteshela ishilile izu lyaho
aje bhope ebho bhabhe no lwonvwano nanshi shila awe Daada, sholi muhati yane nane muhati yaho. Embaputila aje abhene bhawezye abhe muhati yetu ili ensi nkeyeteshele aje awe wontumile.
Omwamihwe ula wompiye ane - nane embapiye abhehali, aje bhawezye abhe no lwonvwano nanshile ate shatili no lwonvwano -
Ane muhati yabho wope muhati yane, aje nkabhawezye akamilisiwe huu, aje ensi nkemanye aje yooli awe wontumile, na abhagane, nanshi shila awe shongene, ane.
Daada hala hompiye ane - Eziliha aje abhene wope bhawezye abhe pandwemo nane apantu pehwendi wawezye alole oummwamihwe wane, ula wompiye: afuatanaje awe ohangane ane shagelisele misingi gensi.
Daada welyoli, ensi seyamenye awe, ila ane namenye awe; na bhamenye aje ohantumile.
Nabhashele aje itawa lyaho limanyishe hwa bhene, embalibheshe limanyishe aje olwonvwano olwo lwo hangene ane luwezye abhe muhati yabho, nane embezye abhe muhati yabho.”
O Yesu nayanga enongwa ezi, asogoye na bhanafunzi bhakwe ahwenyezye entebha ye Kidron, hwa hwali ne bustani, huula omwene na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhahinjila muhati yakwe.
Esheshi ola oYuda, wahanzaga ahugalushe, wope aimenye eshemu eyo, afuatanaje oYesu abhalaga husehemu ela mara hahinji abhalaga na bhanafunzi bhakwe.
Wope oYuda, nawapata ikundi lya sikari na maofisa afume hwa gosi adimi bhahenza ne tala, ikurunzi ne silaha.
Wope oYesu, ohu amenye shila hantu hahali habhombeha zaidi yakwe ahwifumizye hwitazi na abhabhozya, “Wenu wamuhumwanza?”
Wope wajile, oYesu Mnazareti.” O Yesu abhabhozya, “Ane nene” Wope oYuda wagalushe oYesu ahali ayemeleye na asikari bhala.
Eshi eshi embabhozya, “Ane nene” bhawela shingunga bhagwa pansi.
Wabhabhozya nantele, “Wenu wa muhumwanza? Bhope waga nantele “oYesu Munazareti.”
O Yesu wabhobhozya, “Embabhozezye aje ana nene; eshi nkashe munaanza ane, bhaleshi ebha abhnje bhabhalaje.”
Ega gali esho aje lila izu likamilishe; pala nayangaga; hwa bhala bhohampiye, senatezizye hata weka.”
O Simoni Petro, waali ni panga, wega nahudumule ikutu lya hundeelo oboyi wa Dimi ogosi. Ni tawa lyakwe oboyi ola ali yo Malko.
O Yesu abhozya oPetro, “Wezya ipanga lyaho hu ala yakwe. Yenu ensamwelee eshikombe shila shampiye oDaada?”
Eshi lila ikundi lya skari na jemedari, na boyi bha Yahudi, bhakhata oYesu na hupinye.
Wope walongola nasoti pa hwa Anasi, amwane ali khoi wa Kayaafa, ola wali wa Dimi ogosi omwaha ogwo.
O Kayafa wabhapiye oushauri Ayahudi yahanziwaga aje omuntu omo afwe husababu ya bhantu.
O Simoni oPetro alondoleye oYesu, na shesho omwanafunzi wamwabho. Nola omwanafunzi ali afamahamiha hwa dimi ogosi, wope ahinjila pandwemo no Yesu mwibehewa ilya Chungaji ogosi;
o Petro ali ayemeleye honze hu ndiango. Ola omwanafunzi wa manyishe hwa dimi ogosi, afumile honze abhala ayanje nola oshe oboyi waalindaga ondiango na humwinjizye oPetro.
Ola oboyi walindaga ondiango, abhozezye oPetro, “Aje awe solo pandwemo na bhantu bha muntu ono?” Wope ajile, “Ane wenje.”
Na bhala aboyi bha gosi bhahemeleye apantu pala; bhapembile omwoto afuatanaje hwali isasa, na shesho bhali bhahwota omwoto aje apate ilyoto. Wope oPetro ali nabho, ahwote omwoto ali ayemeleye.
Odimi ogosi abhozezye oYesu ahusu abhanafunzi bhakwe ne nsambelezyo zyakwe.
O Yesu ajile, “Enjebho zyezye pazelu ensi; Ane na sambelezezye wilawila mshibhanza na pantu pala Ayahudi pabhabhonganaga. Nane senayanjile lyalyonti.
Yenu mwabhozezyaga? Bhabhozyaji ahusu hala hanayanjile. Ebha abhantu bhamenye amambo gananjile.
O Yesu nahayanga ezyo, omo wa gosi ali ayemeleye wa khoma oYesu hu khono ogwakwe na pamande waga, “Esho, shashi hwanziwa ahugamule odimi ogosi?”
Wope oYesu ajile, “Nkashe enjanjile enongwa zyazyonti embibhi obhe keti hwego amabhibhi, na nkashe egomoye shinza yenu ekhomwa?
O Anasi atwala oYesu hwa Kayafa hwa chungaji ogosi ali afungulwe.
O Simoni oPetro ali ayemeleye wahwikosya ilyoto yoyo. Bhala abhantu bhabhozya. “Aje, awe nawe soli pandwemo na bhanafunzi bhakwe?” Wakhana waga, “Ane weenje.”
Omo omo waboyi bhachungaji ogosi, waali holo wa lume waadulwe ikutu, ajile, “Se wewe elolile hula hu bustani?”
O Petro akhana nantele, na Ehanda ahekuga.
Bhahamwega oYesu afume hwa Kayafa paka hu Praitorio. Hwali shapwiti na mazansha. Abhene bhebho sebhahinjiye ePraitorio bhasiye ahwiyonvwe ailye epasaka.
O Pilato abhabhalilia ahayanga. “Ahaga listako bhole lyalihuhusu omuntu ono?”
Bhayanga na hubhozye, “Nkashe ono muntu agalisebhomba mbibhi, handa setiletile huliwe.”
O Pilato abhabhozya, “Mweji amwe mwemwe, mulonje alengane nendijizyo zyenyu bhope.” Ayahudi bhabhozya, “Endajizyo sezitibhozya abude omuntu wawonti.”
Bhayanjile ezi aje izu lya Yesu likamilishe izu lya ayanjile ahusu enfwa yakwe.
O Pilato ahinjila nantele hu Praitorio akwizya oYesu; ahabhozya, “Aje, awe oli mwene wa Ayahudi?”
O Yesu ajile, “Aje, awe ombozya ni swali eli ohwanza amanye au afuatanaje bhatumile aje ombozye ane?”
Wope oPilato ajile, “Ane sendi Yahudi, aje seshashesho?” Ikabela lyenyu no chungaji ogosi ebho bhabhaletile huline; awe obhombile yenu?
O Yesu ajile; oumwene wane sewamu omu, nkashe oumwene wane ugaali wa munsi omu aboyi bhane handa bhahomaniye waganje anfume hwa Yahudi. Lyoli oumwene wane seufuma epa” Pansi
O Pilato abhozya, “Aje awe eshi oli mwene?” O Yesu ajile, “awe shili shoyanga aje ane endi mwene, afuatana neshi napepwe alenganeshi ane enenzele munsi aje embe keti weela elyoli. Wawonti waali neyo elyoli elitejezya izu lyane.
O Pilato abhozya, “Elyoli yenu?” Wope nayanga ego ahabhala hwa Yahudi na bhabhozye “Selola nkahamo hwa muntu ono.
Amwe mulinoutamaduni wamubhomba emwegulile ofungwa omo owakati we Pasaka. Aje muhwanza aje embigulile omwene wa Yahudi.”
Bhahomile ekelele bhaile, sio ono, tigulile oBaraba.” Wope oBaraba alifyozi.
O Pilato amwejile oYesu na hushete.
Bhala asikari bhapotile aminvwa nalenganye taji. Bhaibheha pitwe lya Yesu na hukwatizye amenda ge rangi ye nshamwamu nshamwamu.
Bhamwenzela na aje, “Awe mwene wa Yahudi! na hukhome hu makhono gabho.
O Pilato afumile honze na bhabhozye abhantu, “Enyaji embaletela ono omuntu hulimwe aje mumanye ane senalilolile ibhibhi lyalyonti muhati yabho.”
Eshi oYesu afumile honze; ali akwete etaji ye minvwa na menda amashamwamu. O Pilato ayanga, “Enyaji abhozya mwenyi omuntu ono epa!”
Omuda ochungaji ogosi wa gosi nabhahalola oYesu, bhakhoma ekelele bhaga, “Yenvyaji, yenvyaji.” O Pilato abhabhozya, “Mwenji amwe mwemwe muyenvyaje, afuatanaje ane sendilola akosa muhati yakwe.”
Ayahudi bhabhozya oPilato, “Ate tili ne ndajizyo, na hundajizyo yeeyo ehwanziwa afwe afuatanaje omwene ahwilola aje mwana wa Ngolobhe.”
O Pilato nahonvwa enongwa ezyo azidile ahwogope,
ahinjila Mpraitorio nantele na hubhozye oYesu, “Awe ofuma hwii? Ata sheshi, oYesu sagayanjile.
Nantele iPilato abhozya, “Aje, awe soyanga nane? Aje, awe somenye aje ane endi nouwezo wa humwigugulile no uwezo wa huyemvye?”
O Yesu ajile, “Ogali ne nguvu ashile ane ogalisopewilwe afume amwanya. Eshi, omuntu wanefwizye huliwe ali ne mbibhi engosi.”
Afumilane ni jibu eli, oPilato ahanzaga ahuleshe weene, ila Aayahudi wahakhoma ekelele bhaga, “Nkashe obhahuleshe wene awe soli wamwabho oKaisari: Shila wahwibheha aje mwene ayanga shingunga sha Kaisari.”
O Pilato na honvwa enongwa aleta oYesu honze nantele ahakhala pitengo lye lonzi pala papamanyi she aje sakafu, ila hushiEbrania, Gabhatha.
Isiku lye maandalizi ge pasaka nalyafishile, omuda gwe saa tanda. O Pilato abhozya Ayahudi, “Enyaaji omwene wenyu ono epa!”
Bhakhoma ekelele, “Sogozi, sogozi, muyenvye!” O Pilato abhabhozya, “Aje eyenvye omwene wenyu?” Wope Ochungaji ogosi ajile, “Ate setili no mwene ila o Kaisari.”
O Pilato nkafumya oYesu hwabhene aje ayenvewe.
Wope bhamwega oYesu, wope wafuma, ohu anyemuye eshikhobhe hanyo shakwe yoyo paka hula hufuvu litwe, hu Shiebrania bhaiga hu Golgota.
Nkabhayenvya oYesu na bhala alume bhabhele, omo oupande ou owamwabho oupande ou, no Yesu pahati yabho.
O Pilato ahandiha eshimanyilo na bheshe pamwanya pashi khobhehanyo. Epo pahandihwe: YESU WENAZALETI, OMWENE WA YAHUDI.
Abhinji bha Yahudi bhabhazya eshimanyilo esho pantu pala pabhayenvezye oYesu pali pepe ne khaaya. Eshi manyilo esho shahandihwe hushi Ebrania, hushi Rumi na hushi Yunani.
Ogosi bha dimi bha Yahudi bhabhozya oPilato, “Sio hwandishe, 'Omwene wa Yahudi; ila omwene ajile ane endi mwene Wayahudi.”
Wope oPilato ajile, “Genandishe enandishe.”
Askari nabhayenvya oYesu, bhahega amenda gakwe na gagabhanye vilondo viine, shila sikari ilondo limo, Shesho inkanzu, lila selyalilisonilwe ila lyali litabhilwe lyonti afumile pamwanya.
Bhakwepelana bhebho hu bhebho, “Tinganje alipasule ila tikhome yekola aje libhe lyananu.” Eli lyafumiye aje lila izu likamilishe, lila lyalyajile bhagabhenye amenda gane, no ninkanza lyane bhakhomeye ekola.”
Asikari bhabhombile embombo ezi. Onyina wakwe oYesu, no dada wa nyina wakwe, oMariamu oshe wa Kleopa no Mariamu Magedelena - abhashe ebha bhali bhemeleye pepe neshi khobhehanyo sha Yesu.
O Yesu nalolile onyina wakwe pamonola omwanafunzi wagene bhemeleye peepe, abhozye onyina wakwe, “Wee shee, enya, lola omwana waho ono epa!”
Abhozya omwanafunzi, “Enya, ono epa onyina waho. “Afume esala eyo ola omwanafunzi amwega abhale akhaya yakwe.
Baada yelyo, o Yesu amenye aje gonti gamalishe gamalishiye aje akamilisye amaazu, ajile, “Elola eshomelwa.”
Eshelelo shashilimemile shali shibhehwelwe pala, bhabheha esifongo yememile Isiki pamwanya ye ufito we hisopo, bhabheshela mwilomu lyakwe.
Wope oYesu naibhonga ezyo, ajile, “Emalishe.” Pamande aundamiha itwe lyakwe, aibheha eroho yakwe.
Afwatanaje waali wakati wahwiyandaale, afuatanaje amabele segahanziwaga asagale pashikhobhehanyo owakati we Sabato (afuatanaje eSabato yaali ye muhimu), ayahudi bhalabhile oPilato aje amagaga gabho bhala bhabhali bhayenvezewa gabudulwe, naje na mabeele gabho bhagisye.
Osikari ahenza abudule amagaga gamuntu owa kwanza no wa bhele ali ayonvewa pandwemo no Yesu.
Nabhafishila oYesu, bhamweje afwiye eshieshi sebhabudula amagaga gakwe.
Ata sheshi omo wa sikari alese oYesu hu mbazu ne mpalala, gahafuma amenze gidanda.
Wope walolile eli afumwizye olweteho no lweteho lwakwe lwe lyoli. Omwene amenye hayanjile he lyoli aje namwe mweteshele.
Enongwa ezi zyahali aje lila izu lyalya ya ngwilwe nkalifishile, “Nomo hata omo wamwene waibudulwa.”
Nantele izu lyamwabho liyiga, “Bhahumwenya omwene wabhalese”
Baadaye nongo ezi oYusufu we Arimathaya, afuatanaje ali mwanafunzi wa Yesu, ila shi siri abhogope Ayahudi, alabhile oPilato aje agweje obele gwa Yesu. Wope oPilato apiye oluhusa. O Yusufu ahenza agwefwe obele gwa Yesu.
Wope o Nikodemo ola olwahwande wafwatile oYesu no siku wope ahenzele. Omwene aletile osangano manemane no udi, oumwamuwe latili mia e yeeka.
Bhahega obele gwa Yesu bhagupinya mumpongoso ye shitani pandwemo na gala amafuta, nanshi shahali ekawaida ya Yahudi omuda gwa syele.
Apantu oYesu pabhayenvezye pali nee bustani; muhati yela ebustani mwali ni kaburi ipya sayahali omuntu wawaile asyelwe omwo.
Afuatanaje lyali lisiku lye maandalizi hwa Yahudi, na afuatanaje lila ikaburi lyali peepe, bhahagoni oYesu muhati yakwe.
Khasha isiku lya hwande lya mulwa sanu, shahuli nkisi, oMariamu Magederena ahenzele hwi kaburi; ahalola lila lila iwe lyepile pikaburi.
Ahashembela abhale hwa Simoni oPetro na hwola omwanafunzi wamwabho ola oYesu wagene, nkabhabhozya, “bhamwejile Ogosi mwikaburi, na setihwelewa hula hwabhagonizye.”
O Petro no mwanafunzi ola wamwabho bhahafuma abhale hwi kaburi.
Bhonti bhanyilile pandwemo; ola omwanafunzi wamwabho anyililiye tee ashile oPetro nagishe hwi kaburi abhe wa hwande.
Ahemelela na hwenye ikaburi; alola ela empogoso egonile, ila sagaahinjiye muhati.
Wope oSimoni oPetro wope ahafiha ahinjila muhati yi kaburi. Wailola ela empogoso egonile pala
nela eleso yayali hwitwe lyakwe seyali ogonile pandwemo ne mpogoso yayagonile panshenje yakwe.
Ola omwanafunzi wamwabho wope ahunjiye muhati yi kaburi; walola na hweteshele.
Afuatanaje paka owakati owo bhaali seele sebhagamenye amaazu aje yalazimishe oYesu afufushe nantele hwa bhafwe.
Abhanafunzi wahala nantele mukhaya zyabho.
O Mariamu ali ayemeleye pi kaburi alila, aali ahwendelela alile ahemeleye ahenya mwikaburi.
Ahabhalola ahalo ozelu bhabhele bhabhali no waje ozelu bhakheye omo hwitwe owa mwabho hu magaga apantu oYesu paali agonile.
Bhope bhabhozya, “Oshe, yeenu olila?” Wope afuatanaje bhamwejile Ogosi wane, naane seehwelewa hwa bhabheshele.”
Nahayanga ego, agalushe na hulole oYesu ali ayemeleye. Ila sagamenye aje ali yo Yesu.
Wope oYesu abhozya, “Maye yenu olila? Ohumwanza wenu?” Wope ohumwenyu yayola walenganya ebustani abhozya, “Gosi, nkashe wewe womwejile, mboozye, hwoobheshele nane embahumweje.”
O Yesu abhozya, “O Mariamu.” Wope agaluha yoyo na hubhozye hu Shiaramu, “Raboni,” esho hwahuje, “Mwalimu.”
O Yesu abhozya, “Oganje nguse, afuatane naje senzubhile abhale hwa Daada; ila obhale hwa holo bhane obhabhozye aje embazubhe abhale hwa Daada wane ola waali Daadi wenyu, Ongolobhe wane no Ngolobhe wenyu.”
O Mariamu oMagedelena ahenza abhabhozya abhanafunzi, “Elolile Ogosi,” naje abhozezye amambo ega.
Na hwahali ndyabheela, isiku elyo, isiku lya hwande lya mulwasanu, na mandiango gaali gafungwilwe pala abhanafunzi pabhahali hubhogope Ayahudi, oYesu ahenzele na hwemelele pahati yabho n abhabhozye, “Olusongwo lubhe hulimwe.”
Na hayanga ego abhalanga amakhono gakwe no bhazu lwakwe. Wope abhanafunzi nabhalolile Ogosi bhasongwelwe.
O Yesu abhabhozya nantele, “Olusongwo lubhe namwe. Nanshi Odaada shantumile ane, shesho shesho nane nabhafumile amwe.”
O Yesu nayanga ego, abhavuvia abhabhozya, Posheli Ompempo Ofinjile.
Wawonti wamuhusajila embibhi, bhasajilwe; na bhala bhamwaibhafunjila bhaifunjilwa.”
O Tomaso, omo wa bhala kumi na bhabhele, wahetwaga Didimasi, sagali na bhanafunzi amwabho oYesu lwa henzaga.
Bhala abhanafunzi amwabho bhabhozya pamande, “Tilolile Ogosi.” Wope abhozya, “Nkashe sembalole eshimanyilo she nsumari mumakhono gakwe, nabheshe evidole vyane hwesho eshimanyilo, nantele abheshe amakhono gane hubhazu lwakwe sembahweteshele.”
Na zyashila ensiku nane abhanafunzi bhali ampande nantele, wope oTomaso ali pandwemo nabho. A andiango nagafungwa oYesu ahemeleye pahati yabho. Na ayanjile, “Olusongwa lubhe namwe.”
Ahabhozya oTomaso, leeta eshidole shaho na alole amakhono gane; leeta eepa amakhono gaho obheshe pabhazu lwane; oganjebhe wasaahweteshela obhee wa hweteshela.”
Wope oTomaso ayanga ahaaga, “Gosi wane nantele Ngolobhe wane.”
O Yesu abhozya, Afuatanaje waandola, oyetesheye. Bhasailwe bhala bhabhahweteshela, bilaalole.”
O Yesu abhombile ezyaswije nyinji hwitazi lya bhanafunzi, zyasagaziwaile ahwandihwe mushitabu eshi;
ezi zyandihwe aje nkamweteshe laje aje oYesu yo Kilisiti, mwana wa Ngolobhe, aje namu hweteshela mubhe no womi hwitawa lyakwe.
Baada ye nongwa ezyo oYesu ahwibhonesya nantele hwa bhanafunzi hunsombe ye Tiberia; eshi sha sheshi shahwibhonesezye yooyo:
O Simoni o Petro alipandwemo no Tomaso wa kwiziwa Didimas, o Nathanaeli wa hu kana ye Galilaya, abhana bha Zebedayo na bhanafunzi bhamwabho bhabhele bha Yesu.
O Simoni Patro abhozya, “Ane embala ahwonze ensamaki.” Bhope bhabhozya, “Ate nate tibhala nawe.” Wahabhala bhahinjila mwi toli, ila nusiku owo bhonti sebhapete hahonti.
Shapwinti na hwahasha, oYesu ahemeleye hufukweni, wope abhanafunzi sebhamanyaga aje aali yo Yesu.
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Bhavijana, muli hahonti ahalyee?” Bhope bhayanga bhaga, “Hamuna.”
Wabhabhozya, “Isyii owavu oupande wendeelo witoli, namwe munzapate hashee, “Bhahisya owavu bhope sebhawezizye aakuunye nantele afuatanaje esamaki zyali nyinji.
Ola omwanafunzi oYesu wagene wabhozya Petro, “Yo Gosi.” Wope oSimoni Petro lwa honvwa aje yo Gosi, wahwipinya omwenda gwakwe (afuatanaje sagaakwete shinza), pamande wahwiponya mwinsombe.
Bhala abhanafunzi bhamwabho wahenza mwotori (sebhali hutali ne pwani, yali mita mia yeva afume ufukweni), bhope bhali bhakunya zila enyavu zyali zimemile ensamaki.
Na bhafiha hufwekweni, wagulola omwoto gwe kaala pala pamwanya yakwe pali ne nsamaki pandwemo na mabumunda.
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Leeti zimo ensamaki zyamwonzile esalezi eshi.”
O Simoni Petro waazubha aguvute gula owavu gwagwali gumemile ensamaki engosi, esamaki zyali 153; hata nkashe zyali nyinji, ula owavu sewazembushe.
O Yesu abhabhozya, “Enzaji mupate vigulilo ilomu.” Nomo ata weka hwa bhanafunzi walenjele ahubhozye, “Awe we weenu?” Bhamenye aje ali yo Gosi.
O Yesu ahenza, ahega lila ibumunda, pamande abhapela, abhomba shesho huunsamaki zila.
Ene yaali mara tatu oYesu hwa bhanafunzi bhakwe baada ya ovyionshe afume hwabhafwe.
Baada ya hwigule ilomu, oYesu abhozya oSimoni Petro, “Simoni mwana wa Yohana aje, ongene ane ashile ebha?” O Petro ahaga, “Ena, Gosi; “Awe omenye aje ane agene.” O Yesu abhozya, “Lisya awanangole bhane.”
Abhabhozya emara ya bheele, “Simoni mwana wa Yona, aje, ongeene?” O Petro ahaga, “Ena, Gosi; awe omenye aje ane egene. “O Yesu ahaga, “Dima engole zyane.”
Abhozya nantele emara ya tatu, “Simoni, mwana wa Yohana, Aje ongene?” Wope oPetro azugumila huu shila shabhozezye mara hatatu, “Aje awe ongene?” Wope ahaga, “Gosi, omenye gonti; omenye aje egene.” O Yesu ahaga, Lisya engole zyane.
Eteshela, eteshela, ehubhozya, nawahali kijana wamanyene akwate amenda weewe na abhale hwa hwonti hwo hwanza; ila nawaibhagoogolo waigolosya amakhono gaho, no weenje aihukwatizya amenda na hutwale hwa sohwanza abhale.”
O Yesu ayanjile ega aje abhonesye aje nfwa bhole o Petro yagamwamishe Ongolobhe. Nayanga ega, abhozya oPetro, “Onfwate.”
O Yesu agalushe na hulole ola omwanafunzi ola oYesu wagene wabhalondola- Ono yayola wahagamiye pashifubha sha Yesu omuda gwe shalyee sha na ndabhela na hubhozye, “Gosi, wenu wanzahugalushe?”
O Petro alolile nantele wabhozya oYesu, “Gosi, Ono omuntu anzabhombe eyenu?”
O Yesu ahaga, “Nkashe ehwanza aje asagale paka lwanayenza, elyo lihusu yenu?” Nfwaate.”
Enongwa ene yaahendelela mhati mwa bhala aholo, aje omwanafunzi ono sagaifwa. Ila oYesu sagabhozezye oPetro aje omwanafunzi oyo faafwa, “Nkashe ehwanza aje omwene asagale paka lwanayenza gahuhusu yenu?”
Ono yo mwanafunzi wafumya oluhakikisyo lwe enongwa ezi na timenye aje oluhakikisyo lwakwe lwe lyoli.
Gahweli amambo gamwabho gaminji oYesu gabhombile. Zigadolilwe zyonti elola aje ensi ene seyahenzaga aye avibheshe evitabu vyavigadolilwe.
Eshitabu shila eshikulu nasimbile, Theofilo, nahayanjile zyonti zyahandile uYesu abhombe na manyizye,
mpaka isiku uYesu lyahejelewe humwanya. Eli lyabhombeshe uYesu nawafumya eamri ashilile hwa Umpepo Ufinjile hwa atumwe bhakwe bhabhasaluye.
Baada ye mayemba agateswe, abhoneshe ali mwomi ne mbonesyo nyingi zyazyabhoneshe. Hunsiku amalongo gane ahwibhonesezye hwa bhantu bhakwe nayanje ezyeumwe zya Ngulubhi.
Na patangene nabho abhalajizizye aje bhasahasogole mu Yelusalemu, lelo bhagule edagano zyayanjile, “Zyamwahumvwaga neyanga afume huline
aje uYohana abhozya naminzi lelo ane embabhozye nu Mpepo Ufinjile nkazyashila ensiku zishe.”
Nabhakhomene pandwimo bhahabhuzya, “Aje eshi jibha lwubhabhagomoshezye oumwene a Izraeli?”
Umwene ahaga se shinza hulimwe amanye ezyahwibhesheye umwene Ungulubhi.”
Lelo mubhaposhe ikhone nawinza hulimwe Umpepo Ufinjile, namwe mwaibha bhaketi bhane, mu Yelusalemu, mu Uyahudi mu Samaria, na humalishilo uwensi.”
Nawayanga ezyo uYesu wabhuha wanyamulwa humwanya nabhamwenya, ibhengo lyakwinshila watega sebhalola na maso gabho.
Nulwabhahwenya humwanya kwa makini akienda, ghafula, abhantu bhabhili bhemelela pahati yabho bhakwite amenda amazelu.
Bhaga, “Mwe bhantu bha hu Galilaya, yenu mwimeleye epa?” Muhwenya abhala humwanya? Unu uYesu yamuhulola abhala humwanya ahwenza shesho sha muhulola abhala.
Nabhanvwa isho bhaela afume hwigamba lye mizeituni, abhale hu Yerusalemu humwendo wa Sabato.
Nabhafiha bhahabhala hwigulu amatawa gabho bhabhebha. Petro, Yohana, Yakobo, Andrea, Filipo, Thomaso, Batholomayo, Mathayo, Yakobo Omwana wa Alfayo, Simoni Zelote nu Yuda Umwana wa Yakobo.
Bonti ebho bhabhungene neshi umuntu umo, bhahendelela ne mputo. Bhali na abhashe, uMariamu unyina wa Yesu, nailumbu bhakwe.
Ensiku zila uPetro ahimilie pahati pa holo bhala bhahali abhantu 120, ahaga,
Mwe bhantu ehali huje enongwa zya Ngulubhi zitimile, zyayanjile Umpepo Ufinjile hwilomu lya Daudi zyazyayanjile uYuda, yabhalongole bhaala bhabhakete uYesu.
Umwene ali pamo nate aposhile ifungu lyakwe elye faida humbombo ene.”
(Neshi umuntu unu akalile ugunda huhela ila eye mbibhi zyakwe nepo ahagwiye abazuhu ivyanda na maula gahafuma na hwitishe.
Bhonti bhabhakhalaga hu Yerusalemu bhuhumvwizye na ieneo elyo hahalyeta itawa hunjango yabho “Akeldama” ugwo “gunda gwi danda.”)
“Mushitabu eshe Zaburi shijile, 'Ambe ugunda gwakwe gubhe lisami asahakhale umuntu nkumo;' tikunde, 'Umuntu uwinje ayeje enafasi yakwe eyelongozi.'
Elyo lye muhimu aje ulume umoyajendaga pandwimo nate lula uYesu nalihulite nahinjilaga nafume,
ahwande lila uYohana na hozyaga abhantu mpaka isiku lila uYesu nahabhushile abhale humwanya, lazima abhe keti we luzyuho pandwimo nate.
“Bhabhala hwitagalila alume bhabhili, uYusufu yahetelwe Barnaba, itawa elya mwabho ali yu Yusto, nu Mathiya.
Abene bhalabha bhaga, “Awe, Ngolobhe umenye amoyo gabhantu bhonti tilaaba abhantu yusaluye
ahweje enafasi ya Yuda yabhombile embibhi nasogole hulite.”
Bhakhoma ekula ekula yagwila uMathiya yabhehwelwe pandwemo na bhaala atumwe ilongo nu weka.
Nalyahafiha isiku elye Pentekoste, bhonti bhabhongene pandwemo.
Gwahabhafumila ungulumo afume humwanya neshi ugwihala ehali. Gwamema munyumba yonti mwabhakheye.
Zyahabhafumila emele neshi, zigabhanyishe nabhe pamwanya ya shila muntu (pitwe).
Bhonti bhapata Umpepo Ufinjile bhahanda ayanje enjango ezyenje neshi Umpepo shasungwilwe umwene.
Bhahali ayahudi bhabhakhalaga mu Yelusalemu bhabhaputaga bhabhafuma shila nsi pansi.
